### [1] [Approaching human parity in the quality of automated organoid image segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03053)
*Chase Cartwright,Gongbo Guo,Sai Teja Pusuluri,Christopher N. Mayhew,Mark Hester,Horacio E. Castillo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合通用基础模型 SAM 与领域特定工具的复合方法，用于自动分割并测量诱导多能干细胞（iPSC）来源的类器官（organoid）球体的尺寸与形态。该方法在所有测试条件下均能产生一致且准确的分割结果，其性能在部分指标上达到甚至接近人工标注者间的变异性（inter-observer variability）水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 类器官（organoid）的发展过程中伴随着快速的形态与细胞组织变化，需要先进的成像与分析工具来准确监测其生长轨迹并研究疾病进程。现有工具无法在所有测试条件下均实现足够精确的图像分割。

Method: 引入了一种复合方法，将通用基础模型 Segment Anything Model (SAM) 与一个现有的领域特定工具相结合，用于自动分割源自诱导多能干细胞（iPSC）的发育中球体的图像，并测量其大小和形状。

Result: 没有单一现有工具能在所有测试条件下实现足够精确的分割；新提出的复合方法在除极少数最具挑战性图像外的所有图像上均产生了一致且准确的结果。该方法的准确性在一种指标上达到了人工标注者间变异性（inter-observer variability）的水平，在其余指标上也与之非常接近。

Conclusion: 所提出的复合方法能够可靠地自动分割类器官图像，其表现接近人工标注的一致性水平，为类器官发育的高通量自动化分析提供了一种有效方案。

Abstract: Organoids are complex, three dimensional, self-organizing cell cultures which manifest organ-like features and represent a powerful platform for studying human disease and developing treatment options. Organoid development is characterized by dynamic morphological and cellular organization, which mimic some aspects of organ development. To study these rapid changes over the course of organoid development, advanced imaging and analytical tools are critical to accurately monitor the trajectory of organoid growth and investigate disease processes.
  In this work, we focus on computer vision and machine learning techniques to automatically measure the size and shape of developing spheroids derived from pluripotent stem cells (iPSCs), which are typically the starting material for generating organoid cultures. To facilitate this task, we introduce a composite method that combines the Segment Anything Model (SAM), a general-purpose foundation model, with an existing domain-specific tool. This composite method is evaluated together with several existing tools by testing them on organoid image data and comparing with the results of manual image segmentation. We find that no single existing tool is able to segment the test images with sufficient accuracy across all test conditions, but the newly introduced composite method produces consistent and accurate results for all but a very small fraction of the most challenging images. Finally, we compare the accuracy of this method to the variability between manual segmentations by independent annotators (inter-observer variability) and find that by one measure it performs at the level of inter-observer variability and by others it performs very close to it.

</details>

### [2] [Taxonomy of Instanton Corrections in Infinite Distance Limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03005)
*Manuel Artime,Ralph Blumenhagen,Panagiotis Leivadaros*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过BPS保护的高阶导数$R^4$项作为可精确求解的示例，分析了在模空间无穷远极限下，对光塔态（light towers of states）进行单圈Schwinger积分所生成的瞬子修正，并发现该积分精确捕捉了作用量位于特定窗口内的瞬子。该结论在八维和七维环面紧致化（toroidal compactifications）的模空间中得到了验证，并进一步通过分类学（taxonomy classification）框架重构了该提议，以确定与任意无穷远极限相关的涌现瞬子谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在模空间（moduli space）无穷远极限下，通过Schwinger积分对光塔态进行单圈积分能够生成哪些瞬子修正，并明确这些瞬子作用量（instanton action）与引力截断（gravity cutoff）和光塔质量尺度之间的关系。

Method: 以BPS保护的高阶导数$R^4$项作为可精确求解的示例，在八维和七维环面紧致化（toroidal compactifications）的模空间中，对光塔态进行单圈Schwinger积分，并与瞬子修正进行比对；同时采用分类学（taxonomy classification）框架重新表述该结果。

Result: Schwinger积分精确捕捉了作用量位于窗口$(\Lambda_{\rm sp}/M_{\rm light})^{-1}\le S_{\rm inst}\le \Lambda_{\rm sp}/M_{\rm light}$内的瞬子，即作用量受引力截断$\Lambda_{\rm sp}$与最轻塔质量尺度$M_{\rm light}$比值上下限约束的瞬子。在八维和七维各极限下，该积分完整重现了窗口内的瞬子贡献。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种通过Schwinger积分从光塔态生成瞬子修正的普适框架，并借助分类学（taxonomy classification）确定了与任意无穷远极限对应的涌现瞬子谱（emergent instantonic spectrum）。

Abstract: Using the BPS-protected higher derivative $R^4$-term as an exactly solvable example, we analyze which instanton corrections are generated by a one-loop Schwinger integral over the light towers of states that arise in infinite distance limits in moduli space. We find that the Schwinger integral fully captures precisely those instantons whose action lies parametrically in the window $(Λ_{\rm sp}/M_{\rm light})^{-1}\le {\rm S}_{\rm inst}\le Λ_{\rm sp}/M_{\rm light}$, that is, instantons whose action is bounded by the ratio of the gravity cutoff and the mass scale of the lightest tower. This proposal is supported by considering the entire moduli space of toroidal compactifications in eight dimensions, together with a number of limits in seven dimensions. In each case, integrating out the light towers via the Schwinger integral reproduces the complete contribution of the instantons within the above window. We further recast the proposal in terms of the taxonomy classification, allowing us to determine the emergent instantonic spectrum associated with any infinite distance limit.

</details>


### [3] [The Fate of Nucleated Black Holes in de Sitter Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03015)
*Xiaoyi Shi,Gustavo J. Turiaci,Chih-Hung Wu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过包含观察者的引力路径积分，为欧几里得Nariai几何作为de Sitter空间中最大质量黑洞成核（nucleation）的瞬子（instanton）解释提供了更坚实的理论基础，并证明成核后的黑洞经历标准的霍金蒸发而非此前声称的“反蒸发”过程，最终回到最大熵的真空态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，欧几里得Nariai几何被提议作为描述de Sitter空间中最大质量黑洞成核的瞬子，但该解释缺乏更严格的理论基础。本文旨在通过引入观察者，利用引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）为该瞬子解释提供更可靠的依据。

Method: 首先重新审视霍金-莫斯瞬子（Hawking-Moss instanton），并以此为基础研究标量场对黑洞成核的增强效应；随后通过引力路径积分分析成核后黑洞的半经典演化（semiclassical evolution），并检验量子态的光滑性。

Result: 包含观察者的引力路径积分生成了跃迁速率所需的虚相位（imaginary phase）；标量场可以增强黑洞成核，暗示了存在de Sitter解的标量势存在一个量子引力边界；此前声称的“反蒸发”（anti-evaporation）通道是不物理的，源于一个具有奇异视界（singular horizons）的量子态；在光滑态中，黑洞经历标准的热霍金蒸发（thermal Hawking evaporation）；该蒸发过程不受大的量子引力修正影响。

Conclusion: 成核的黑洞会完全蒸发，回到最大熵的de Sitter真空，使得整个过程构成一个玻尔兹曼涨落（Boltzmann fluctuation）。该结果与无边界态（no-boundary state）显式一致，且蒸发过程不受大的量子引力修正影响。

Abstract: The Euclidean Nariai geometry has long been proposed as the instanton describing the nucleation of maximal-mass black holes in de Sitter space. We place this interpretation on firmer footing by showing that, once an observer is included, the gravitational path integral produces the imaginary phase required for a transition rate. As a warmup, we revisit the Hawking-Moss instanton and, as a byproduct, find that scalar fields can enhance black-hole nucleation, suggesting a quantum-gravity bound on scalar potentials with de Sitter solutions. We then study the subsequent semiclassical evolution of the nucleated black hole. We show that the previously claimed "anti-evaporation" channel is unphysical, arising from a quantum state with singular horizons. In a smooth state, the black hole instead undergoes standard thermal Hawking evaporation. We verify explicit agreement with the no-boundary state and argue that this evaporation is not subject to large quantum-gravity corrections. The nucleated black hole thus evaporates completely back to the maximally-entropic empty de Sitter vacuum, making the full process a Boltzmann fluctuation.

</details>


### [4] [Generalized Free Fields in de Sitter from 1D CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03037)
*Kanato Goto,Alexey Milekhin,Herman Verlinde,Jiuci Xu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，一对相同的1D大N CFT（如SYK模型低能极限或高维CFT中的线缺陷）包含一个天然的子代数，该子代数构成一个广义自由场代数（generalized free field algebra），定义在d+1维德西特时空（de Sitter spacetime）的一条类时测地线（time-like geodesic）上。该构造利用大N因子化（large N factorization）、1D共形对称性（1D conformal symmetry）以及德西特格林函数的分裂表示（split representation）。对于3D德西特时空，全息映射扩展到体时空内部，并退化为标准的HKLL方案（HKLL prescription）在德西特时空下的调整版本。此外，该构造可自动实现在协变形式的Schwarzian量子力学中，并且与德西特/DSSYK对应关系（de Sitter/DSSYK correspondence）相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一对相同的大N一维共形场论（1D CFT）中是否存在天然的子代数结构，该结构能够关联到德西特时空中的广义自由场代数，从而为德西特空间中的全息原理（holographic principle）提供新的理论支持。

Method: 利用大N因子化、1D共形对称性以及德西特格林函数的分裂表示，构造从1D CFT算子子代数到德西特时空类时测地线上广义自由场代数的全息映射；对于3D德西特情况，将映射推广到体时空内部并适配HKLL重建方案；在协变形式的Schwarzian量子力学中自动实现该构造。

Result: 发现一对相同的大N 1D CFT中存在一个自然算子子代数，对应d+1维德西特时空类时测地线上的广义自由场代数；对于3D德西特，该全息映射扩展到体时空内部并退化为调整后的HKLL方案；该构造在协变Schwarzian量子力学中得到自动实现。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一维大N CFT与德西特时空全息对应的一种具体实现机制，并为德西特/DSSYK对应关系提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We show that a pair of identical large $N$ 1D CFTs, like the low-energy limit of the SYK model or a line-defect inside a higher dimensional CFT, contains a natural sub-algebra of operators that comprise a generalized free field algebra living on a time-like geodesic in d+1-dimensional de Sitter spacetime. The construction uses large $N$ factorization, 1D conformal symmetry, and the split representation of de Sitter Green functions. We show that for 3D de Sitter spacetime, the holographic map extends into the bulk and reduces to the standard HKLL prescription adjusted to de Sitter spacetime. We describe how our construction is automatically implemented in a covariant version of Schwarzian quantum mechanics and comment on the relevance of our results to the de Sitter/DSSYK correspondence.

</details>


### [5] [Squeezed-state radiation in shockwave scattering: QCD-Gravity double copy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03038)
*Anna M. Staśto,Himanshu Raj,Raju Venugopalan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，强场冲击波散射中的多胶子辐射谱可描述为广义Susskind-Glogower（gSG）压缩相干态；基于双拷贝结构，多引力子辐射可类似描述。该gSG态在近最小不确定构型下可实现极大压缩参数(~ln(¯n))，导致引力波谱的量子噪声增强至超越当前及未来探测器的灵敏度，凸显了研究强场Lipatov区域引力辐射的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究描述了胶子和引力子在强场冲击波散射中的有效Lipatov顶点，但多粒子辐射的量子态结构尚未被充分刻画；本文旨在从压缩相干态角度统一理解多胶子与多引力子辐射的量子特性，并探索其可观测物理后果。

Method: 采用广义Susskind-Glogower（gSG）压缩相干态形式来刻画n粒子胶子辐射谱；利用双拷贝结构（double copy structure）将胶子框架推广至引力子情形；通过分析物理参数空间评估压缩参数的大小及近最小不确定构型条件。

Result: 多胶子辐射谱可被描述为gSG压缩相干态；多引力子辐射可类似描述；gSG态在近最小不确定构型下压缩参数可达~ln(¯n)（¯n为平均引力子占据数）；对应引力波谱中的量子噪声增强至超出当前及未来探测器灵敏度。

Conclusion: 研究强调了在强场Lipatov区域系统研究引力辐射的重要性；该框架揭示了强场QCD与引力辐射之间的深层结构对应，并为引力波量子噪声的观测提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Gluon and graviton radiation in strong field shockwave scattering are described by effective Lipatov vertices, with the graviton Lipatov vertex proportional to the bilinear of its QCD counterpart. We show here that the n-particle gluon radiation spectrum can be described as a generalized Susskind-Glogower (gSG) squeezed coherent state and discuss the properties of such squeezed states. The double copy structure of the radiative frameworks suggests that multi-graviton radiation can be similarly described as a gSG state. We examine the physical parameter space and show that very large squeezing parameters $\sim \ln({\bar n})$ (where ${\bar n}$ is the mean graviton occupancy) are feasible for nearly minimal uncertainty configurations of the gSG state. Quantum noise in the corresponding gravitational wave spectrum is enhanced above the sensitivity of current and future gravitational wave detectors. Our results point to the importance of a comprehensive study of the strong field Lipatov regime of gravitational radiation.

</details>


### [6] [Pseudo-Evanescent Feynman Integrals from Local Subtraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03051)
*Alessandro Georgoudis,Ben Page*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种计算“伪消失”（pseudo-evanescent）费曼积分的新方法，利用局域减除技术将这类积分表示为红外与紫外区域贡献的组合；通过两圈例子验证，并成功重算了双圈全加五点振幅。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在四维时空下严格为零的“伪消失”费曼积分（pseudo-evanescent integrals）在维数正规化（dimensional regularization）框架中具有非平凡的贡献，但缺乏系统性的计算方法。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 利用局域减除技术（local subtraction techniques），将伪消失积分分解为圈动量空间（loop-momentum space）中红外区域（infrared region）和紫外区域（ultraviolet region）的贡献之和，并借助$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon)$修正实现表达式。

Result: 两圈实例表明，许多伪消失费曼积分可简化为单圈积分的乘积或其单重积分。在双圈全加五点振幅的重算中，软区域和共线区域的贡献与已知红外结构精确抵消，有限余项完全来自紫外区域贡献。

Conclusion: 本文方法为处理伪消失积分提供了有效途径，并揭示了该类积分中红外与紫外贡献的层级关系；除方案依赖的对数项外，红外结构完全由已知形式描述。

Abstract: We introduce a new approach for the computation of the class of Feynman integrals whose integrands vanish in strictly four-dimensions, so-called ''pseudo-evanescent'' integrals. We argue that, up to $\mathcal{O}(ε)$ corrections, local subtraction techniques can be used to express pseudo-evanescent integrals in terms of contributions from infrared and ultraviolet regions of loop-momentum space. We study two-loop examples and find that many pseudo-evanescent Feynman integrals are reduced to either products of one-loop integrals or one-fold integrals thereof. As a demonstration of the power of our approach, we use it to recompute the two-loop all-plus five-point amplitude. We find that, up to scheme-dependent logarithms, all contributions from soft and collinear regions cancel exactly against known infrared structure and that the finite remainder is entirely given by contributions from ultraviolet regions.

</details>


### [7] [From Quivers to Geometry: 5d Conformal Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03119)
*Antoine Bourget,Mario De Marco,Michele Del Zotto,Julius F. Grimminger,Andrea Sangiovanni*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明所有5维无陈-西蒙斯能级的平衡（ADE型）特殊酉箭图都能由一个5维共形物质超共形场论（SCFT）作为紫外完备化，并在M理论中给出了相应的局部卡拉比-丘（Calabi-Yau）三维流形实现，从而系统探索了希格斯分支（Higgs Branch）、与class-S构造及仿射格拉斯曼流形（affine Grassmannian）的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决5维平衡特殊酉箭图（balanced ADE-shaped special unitary quivers）在无陈-西蒙斯能级（Chern-Simons level）时的紫外完备化问题，并建立其与共形物质超共形场论（conformal matter SCFT）之间的对应关系。

Method: 通过显式构造局部卡拉比-丘三维流形（local Calabi-Yau threefolds），在M理论（M-theory）框架下实现每一类平衡ADE型特殊酉箭图模型。

Result: 所有5维无陈-西蒙斯能级的平衡ADE型特殊酉箭图均存在紫外完备化，该完备化是5维共形物质超共形场论；给出了对应的局部卡拉比-丘三维流形的显式构造。

Conclusion: 该统一描述为系统探索这些模型的物理性质（如希格斯分支）以及与class-S构造、仿射格拉斯曼流形之间的联系提供了框架。

Abstract: We show that all 5d balanced (ADE-shaped) special unitary quivers with no Chern-Simons level admit a UV completion which is a 5d conformal matter SCFT. We give explicit local Calabi-Yau threefolds realizing each of these models in M-theory. This unified description enables a systematic exploration of their physical properties, such as their Higgs Branch, as well as connections to class-S constructions and the affine Grassmannian.

</details>


### [8] [Flat Space Physics from AdS Actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03155)
*Walker Melton*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将平直时空（flat spacetimes）用双曲切片（hyperbolic slices）层叠，逐片应用AdS/CFT体-边界对应词典，构造了平直时空的全息对偶性（holographic dualities）。研究将闵可夫斯基空间（Minkowski space）和克莱因空间（Klein space）中的无质量标量场以及闵可夫斯基空间中的有质量标量场的四维作用量约化到三维dS和AdS切片上，揭示了约化理论的连续谱结构、边界项联系以及不同渐近极限的几何解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平直时空的全息对偶性尚未完全建立，现有AdS/CFT对偶性主要适用于反德西特时空。本文试图通过双曲切片方法将AdS/CFT体-边界对应词典逐片推广到平直时空，从而为构造平直时空的全息对偶性提供理论基础。

Method: 将四维闵可夫斯基空间和克莱因空间中的无质量标量场以及闵可夫斯基空间中的有质量标量场的作用量，通过双曲切片（hyperbolic slices）约化（reduce）到三维dS和AdS切片上的作用量。约化过程中考虑了非紧致$x^2$方向上的积分，并分析了边界项在光锥（lightcone）处不连续场构型下的作用。

Result: 在闵可夫斯基空间和克莱因空间中，约化后的理论均具有来自非紧致$x^2$方向约化的连续谱（continuous spectrum）。约化后作用量之间通过光锥处不连续场构型产生的边界项（boundary terms）相联系。无质量情形下，约化场在单位双曲切片边界附近的不同渐近极限分别对应光锥（light cone）或零无穷远（null infinity）极限；有质量情形下，仅有一种边界模式具有简单的几何解释。

Conclusion: 双曲切片方法为平直时空的全息对偶性提供了可行的构造方案，揭示了无质量和有质量标量场在约化过程中的不同渐近行为，以及边界项在连接不同约化理论中的关键作用。

Abstract: Flat spacetimes are foliated by hyperbolic slices that are geometrically three-dimensional de Sitter or anti-de Sitter spaces. As such, it is possible to construct flat space holographic dualities by applying the AdS/CFT bulk-to-boundary dictionary slice by slice. In this work, we reduce 4D actions for massless scalars in both Minkowski space and Klein space and massive scalars in Minkowski space to actions on these 3D dS and AdS slices. In both Minkowski and Klein space, the reduced theories have a continuous spectrum of fields originating from the reduction over the noncompact $x^2$ direction. These actions are linked by boundary terms arising from field configurations discontinuous across the lightcone. In the massless case, different asymptotic limits of the reduced field near the boundary of the unit hyperbolic slice replicate either light cone or null infinity limits of the field; in the massive case, only one boundary mode of the reduced field has a simple geometric interpretation.

</details>

### [10] [Quasinormal modes and continuum response of de Sitter black holes via complex scaling method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03277)
*Shoya Ogawa,Okuto Morikawa,Takuya Hirose*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将复标度方法（complex scaling method）应用于四维 Schwarzschild--de Sitter (dS) 时空的黑洞微扰，将出射波边值问题转化为非厄米谱问题，从而在同一框架下处理准正则模极点与旋转连续谱。研究重点关注连续谱能级密度，并分析了非零宇宙常数对标量、电磁和引力扰动中极点与连续谱的影响，同时讨论了向弦启发耦合通道系统和高维 dS 黑洞的推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法在处理黑洞准正则模（quasinormal modes）时，通常只关注离散极点，而连续谱响应（continuum response）的贡献未被充分纳入统一框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，将复标度方法引入 Schwarzschild--dS 时空的微扰，以系统分析连续谱能级密度，并考察非零宇宙常数对谱结构的影响。

Method: 采用复标度方法将出射波边值问题转化为非厄米谱问题，从而统一处理准正则模极点和旋转连续谱。针对标量、电磁和引力场，使用 Regge--Wheeler 型微扰方程进行分析。此外，讨论向弦启发耦合通道系统（string-inspired coupled-channel systems）的扩展，并证明该方法同样适用于高维 dS 黑洞的张量型和矢量型扇区。

Result: 发现非零宇宙常数对极点和连续谱结构均有显著修正。复标度方法能够有效提取连续谱能级密度（continuum level density），该量表征超越孤立准正则模频率之外的连续谱响应。方法在标量、电磁和引力扰动中均适用，并可推广至耦合通道及高维情形。

Conclusion: 复标度方法为黑洞物理学中准正则模与连续谱响应提供了统一且有效的谱分析框架，尤其适用于包含宇宙常数的时空背景，并具备向耦合通道和高维系统推广的潜力。

Abstract: We apply the complex scaling method to black-hole perturbations in four-dimensional Schwarzschild--de~Sitter (dS) spacetimes. The method converts the outgoing-wave boundary-value problem into a non-Hermitian spectral problem and enables quasinormal-mode poles and the rotated continuum to be treated in a common framework. We focus in particular on the continuum level density, which characterizes the continuum response beyond isolated quasinormal-mode frequencies. Using Regge--Wheeler-type perturbation equations for scalar, electromagnetic, and gravitational fields, we investigate how a nonzero cosmological constant modifies the pole and continuum sectors. We also discuss a possible extension to string-inspired coupled-channel systems, and illustrate that higher-dimensional dS black holes can be treated within the same framework, at least in tensor- and vector-type sectors. Our results indicate that complex scaling offers a useful spectral framework for analyzing both quasinormal modes and continuum response in black-hole physics.

### [11] [Stable Magnetic Lorentz-Violating Vacua in Gauge-Invariant Nonlinear Electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03341)
*E. Plácido-Flores,Román Linares,V. López,C. A. Escobar*

Result: 在三个双参数模型中，物理上容许的洛伦兹破缺真空仅在磁分支中得到实现；哈密顿有界性本身并不足以导致自发洛伦兹对称性破缺，还需满足额外的稳定性条件。对称性破缺条件与强场因果性判据之间存在可关联的对应关系。

Conclusion: 在Plebański形式中，以单不变量势描述的非线性电动力学可以支持稳定的洛伦兹破缺磁真空，但需满足哈密顿下界与正Hessian条件；电分支及部分单参数模型则无法同时满足这些条件。该研究为理解规范不变非线性理论中对称性破缺的物理可行性提供了系统框架。

Abstract: We investigate gauge-invariant nonlinear electrodynamics in the Plebański first-order Hamiltonian formulation, taking the single-invariant potential $\hat V(P)$ as the primary object. Our focus is on the existence of stable Lorentz-violating magnetic vacua. For three explicit two-parameter models -- rational asymmetric, logarithmic, and exponential -- we determine the regions of parameter space in which nontrivial constant electromagnetic vacua are compatible with an effective Hamiltonian bounded from below and a positive-semidefinite Hessian. In all three cases, physically admissible Lorentz-violating vacua are realized in the magnetic branch. We further discuss the electric branch and several additional one-parameter models, illustrating that Hamiltonian boundedness by itself does not ensure spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking. We also comment on how the symmetry-breaking conditions are related to known strong-field causality criteria.

### [13] [On the Algebraic Origin of Four-Dimensional Space-time in the IIB Matrix Model: Dimensional Selection via Rigid Supersymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03611)
*Tetsuyuki Muramatsu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在IIB矩阵模型（IIB matrix model）框架下，通过分析全环有效作用量中的量子径向修正与刚性超对称代数几何约束之间的一致性，提出了一种四维时空的解析推导。研究发现，原始十维表述中刚性超代数（rigid superalgebra）所施加的120个独立代数自由度的张量障碍（tensor obstruction）仅在四维中因Clifford代数（Clifford algebra）退化与霍奇对偶（Hodge duality）而消失，这一机制被称为“代数锁定（algebraic locking）”。结论表明，四维时空是超对称量子真空数学一致性的必然结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该工作旨在回答一个长期未解的基本问题：为什么我们的宇宙呈现(3+1)维时空结构。作者试图从非微扰（non-perturbative）视角，在IIB矩阵模型框架内为四维时空的涌现提供解析证明，而非依赖数值模拟或唯象假设。

Method: 方法基于一致性条件分析：一方面考察全环有效作用量（all-loop effective action）中由量子诱导的径向修正（radial corrections）；另一方面考察刚性超对称代数对几何结构施加的约束。通过引入“一致性过滤器（consistency filter）”，研究了原始十维理论中刚性超代数产生的120个独立代数自由度所构成的张量障碍，并检验该障碍在哪些维度下能够被解除。

Result: 研究结果表明，120自由度的张量障碍仅在四维时空条件下消失，其原因在于四维Clifford代数的代数退化性质与霍奇对偶的共同作用。作者将这一解除机制定义为“代数锁定”，并由此论证四维时空是唯一能够同时满足量子修正与超对称代数一致性的维度。

Conclusion: 论文得出核心结论：四维时空并非动力学偶然（dynamical accident），而是超对称量子真空（supersymmetric quantum vacuum）存在数学一致性的必要条件。该发现为IIB矩阵模型中的时空涌现机制提供了新的理论支撑。

Abstract: This paper presents a novel analytical derivation of four-dimensional (4D) space-time within the framework of the IIB matrix model (IKKT model). We address the long-standing question of why our universe exhibits a (3+1)-dimensional structure from a non-perturbative perspective. By investigating the consistency between quantum-induced radial corrections in the all-loop effective action and the geometric requirement of a rigid supersymmetric algebra, we identify a fundamental consistency filter. In the original ten-dimensional formulation, the rigid superalgebra imposes a massive tensor obstruction consisting of 120 independent algebraic degrees of freedom, which forbids any scale-dependent quantum evolution. We demonstrate that this obstruction vanishes uniquely in four dimensions due to the algebraic degeneracy of the Clifford algebra and Hodge duality, a mechanism we define as ``algebraic locking.'' Our results suggest that 4D space-time is not a dynamical accident but a mathematical necessity for a consistent supersymmetric quantum vacuum.

</details>

Abstract: We give new results on the structure and representations of the three lattices $\mathbf{Λ}_{\mathrm{k}},\mathbf{Λ}_{\mathrm{k}\mathcal{C}},\mathbf{Λ}_{\mathrm{k}}^{\ast }$ relevant to code CFTs realizing Narain conformal field theories. In this construction, $\mathbf{Λ}_{\mathrm{k}}^{\ast }$ denotes the dual of the even lattice $\mathbf{Λ}_{\mathrm{k}}$ and $\mathbf{Λ}_{\mathrm{k}\mathcal{C}}$ is an even self-dual intermediate lattice with a (d,d) signature. We study the inclusion relations $\mathbf{Λ}_{\mathrm{k}}\subset \mathbf{Λ} _{\mathrm{k}\mathcal{C}}\subset \mathbf{Λ}_{\mathrm{k}}^{\ast }$ characterized by the discriminant group $\mathbf{Λ} _{\mathrm{k}}^{\ast }/\mathbf{Λ}_{\mathrm{k}}$ isomorphic to $\mathbb{Z}_{\mathrm{k}}$ and provide explicit constructions of these $\mathbb{R}^{(\mathrm{r}d,\mathrm{r}d)}$ lattices first for rank $\mathrm{r}=d=1$ and then for higher dimensional Lie algebras with $\mathrm{r}=d>1$. ### [15] [Virasoro flow, monodromy, and indecomposable structures in critical AdS$_3$ topologically massive gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03649)
*Yannick Mvondo-She*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文为临界拓扑质量引力（critical topologically massive gravity）在手性点（chiral point）处建立了表示论框架（representation-theoretic framework），统一了渐进对称性演化（asymptotic symmetry evolution）与单值性（monodromy）的关系。作者证明，Virasoro零模$L_0$在该点化为非对角化形式，其幂零分量（nilpotent component）同时驱动连续演化与解析延拓中的混合结构，从而将对数模（logarithmic modes）自然地解释为$L_0$的广义本征态（generalized eigenstates），并给出了状态空间不变子空间（invariant subspaces）与广义不变子空间（generalized invariant subspaces）意义上的代数诠释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在手性点$\mu\ell=1$的临界拓扑质量引力中，渐进对称性的代数结构出现对数模（logarithmic modes）等非平凡特征，但缺乏统一的表示论框架来解释连续演化与单值性（monodromy）之间的内在联系。本文的动机是建立这样一个框架，阐明对数扇区（logarithmic sector）在状态空间中的代数本质。

Method: 作者采用表示论方法，将Virasoro零模$L_0$在手性点处写为$L_0=h\mathbf{1}+N$的形式，其中$N$是幂零算子（nilpotent operator）。随后分析该幂零分量在实参数流（连续演化）与虚参数流（单值性）中产生的混合结构，并结合不变子空间（invariant subspaces）与广义不变子空间（generalized invariant subspaces）的代数分解来刻画对数模的产生机制。

Result: 连续演化产生线性混合（linear mixing），单值性产生对数混合（logarithmic mixing），二者均由同一个幂零分量$N$控制。对数模自然地作为$L_0$的广义本征态出现，状态空间中的扇区分解（sector decomposition）具有不变子空间与广义不变子空间的代数解释。

Conclusion: 本文为临界拓扑质量引力中的对数结构提供了统一的描述，阐明了这些结构在渐进对称性表示论（representation theory of asymptotic symmetries）中的角色，揭示了对数扇区本质上对应于状态空间中一个单一的不可分解结构（indecomposable structure）。

Abstract: We develop a representation-theoretic framework for the relation between asymptotic symmetry evolution and monodromy in critical topologically massive gravity at the chiral point $μ\ell=1$. We show that continuous evolution generated by the Virasoro zero mode $L_0$ and analytic continuation around branch points can be unified as different regimes of a single complex one-parameter flow.
  At the chiral point, $L_0$ becomes non-diagonalizable and takes the form $L_0=h \mathbf{1}+N$, with $N$ nilpotent. We demonstrate that this nilpotent component governs identical mixing structures in both real and imaginary flow parameters, producing linear mixing under continuous evolution and logarithmic mixing under monodromy.
  In this sense, the logarithmic sector is characterized by a single indecomposable structure in state space probed uniformly by both transformations. Logarithmic modes arise naturally as generalized eigenstates of $L_0$, and the sector decomposition admits an algebraic interpretation in terms of invariant and generalized invariant subspaces.
  This provides a unified description of logarithmic structures in critical topologically massive gravity and clarifies their role in the representation theory of asymptotic symmetries.

### [16] [Classical correlation functions at strong coupling from hexagonalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03887)
*Benjamin Basso,Erkan Kaluç,Didina Serban*

TL;DR: 本文研究平面 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超杨-米尔斯（Super-Yang-Mills）在强耦合、大尺度极限下的半BPS算符关联函数，利用六边形形式论（hexagon formalism）证明关联函数在该区域指数化，并由一套热力学贝特假设（Thermodynamic Bethe Ansatz, TBA）方程的自由能所支配。该TBA方程在结构上等价于Gaiotto–Moore–Neitzke方程，作者借助墙穿越（wall-crossing）技术扩展了TBA框架，构建了一个适用于多边形六边形铺砌和闭合几何的$\chi$-系统，并推广了Caetano和Toledo关于$AdS_{2}\times S^{1}$中极小曲面的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究平面 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超杨-米尔斯理论在强耦合、大尺度极限下的半BPS算符关联函数，揭示其指数化行为及与可积系统（integrable system）和BPS谱结构的深层联系。

Method: 采用六边形形式论（hexagon formalism）分析二维运动学对应的关联函数，证明其在强耦合大尺度极限下指数化并由TBA方程自由能控制；利用与Gaiotto–Moore–Neitzke方程的结构等价性，引入墙穿越（wall-crossing）技术扩展TBA框架，构建$\chi$-系统。

Result: 发现关联函数在强耦合大尺度极限下指数化，其行为由一组结构等价于Gaiotto–Moore–Neitzke方程的TBA方程自由能描述；建立的$\chi$-系统同时适用于多边形六边形铺砌和描述单迹算符关联函数的闭合几何，并推广了Caetano和Toledo在$AdS_{2}\times S^{1}$中的极小曲面结果。

Conclusion: 半BPS算符关联函数在强耦合大尺度极限下由TBA方程自由能支配，揭示了与$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称场论中BPS谱的深刻对应关系，墙穿越技术为可积系统中的关联函数计算提供了新框架。

Abstract: We study correlation functions of half-BPS operators in planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ Super-Yang-Mills at strong coupling, in the classical limit where operator dimensions scale with the coupling. We focus on the two-dimensional kinematics corresponding in the dual description to strings propagating in $AdS_{3}\times S^{3}$. Using the hexagon formalism, we show that correlation functions exponentiate in this regime and are governed by the free energy of an associated set of Thermodynamic Bethe Ansatz (TBA) equations. These equations are structurally equivalent to the Gaiotto--Moore--Neitzke equations encoding BPS spectra in $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric field theories. Exploiting this correspondence, we apply wall-crossing techniques to extend the TBA framework and formulate a $χ$-system applicable both to polygonal hexagon tilings and to closed geometries describing correlators of single-trace operators. In particular, for four-point functions, this construction generalizes the results of Caetano and Toledo for minimal surfaces in $AdS_{2}\times S^{1}$.

Conclusion: 该自上而下的F-理论框架对轴子参数空间施加了严格的几何约束，预测了质量极轻、衰变常数较大的QCD轴子，为未来轴子探测实验提供了理论参考。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate axion physics in 4D F-theory MSSM models. We derive the axion coupling term with QCD gauge fields and the axion potential from a top-down perspective, from both IIB superstring and the dual M-theory picture. For the explicit geometric model, we employ the "quadrillion" landscape of 4D F-theory models with the exact Standard Model chiral spectrum, and study simple base threefolds such as $\mathbb{P}^3$, $\mathbb{P}^1\times\mathbb{P}^2$, the generalized Hirzebruch threefold $\tilde{\mathbb{F}}_3$ and $\mathbb{P}^1\times\mathbb{P}^1\times\mathbb{P}^1$. We derive exclusion constraints on the Kähler moduli space of the base threefold from the CP violation angle, the Standard Model gauge coupling constants and the stretched Kähler cone condition. We find stringent constraints on the set of base divisors that should be rigid or rigidified by the inclusion of flux. For the allowed regions of the parameter space, we estimate the typical mass of detectable QCD axions to be around $10^{-9}$eV, and the axion decay constant to be around $f_a\sim 10^{15}$GeV.

### [19] [Late-Time Relaxation from Landau Singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04020)
*Dong-Lin Wang,Shi Pu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过朗道奇点分析（Landau singularity analysis）系统提取了有效场论（effective field theory）中由非线性相互作用引发的松弛模式，揭示了从指数衰减到幂律衰减（power-law decay）的晚期时间行为转变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性流体力学相互作用（nonlinear hydrodynamic interactions）会导致涨落（fluctuations）的弛豫从指数衰减转变为晚期时间的幂律衰减。在Schwinger-Keldysh有效场论框架下，这种非线性晚期行为编码在圈图修正（loop corrections）中，但提取该行为需要识别圈积分（loop integrals）的奇点（singularities），而复杂模型中的奇点结构日益精细，亟需系统性方法。

Method: 本文将朗道奇点分析应用于有效场论中的两点关联函数（two-point functions），在不显式计算圈积分的前提下，确定由非线性相互作用诱导的奇点。通过分析频域（frequency-space）奇点，提取出控制晚期时间行为的非线性松弛模式（nonlinear relaxation modes）。

Result: 当系统存在无能隙模式（gapless modes）时，这些松弛模式会在晚期时间产生幂律衰减行为。该方法为一大类宏观有效理论中的非线性晚期弛豫提供了基于奇点的系统性描述。

Conclusion: 朗道奇点分析能够有效地从有效场论圈积分中提取非线性松弛模式的晚期时间行为，无需显式计算积分即可揭示由非线性相互作用引起的幂律衰减机制，适用性广泛。

Abstract: Nonlinear hydrodynamic interactions can change the relaxation of fluctuations from exponential to power-law decay at late times. Schwinger-Keldysh effective field theory provides a standard framework for describing such fluctuation effects, where the nonlinear late-time behavior is encoded in loop corrections. Extracting this behavior requires identifying the singularities of loop integrals, whose structure becomes increasingly intricate beyond simple models. We apply Landau singularity analysis to two-point functions in effective field theories and determine the singularities induced by nonlinear interactions without performing the loop integrations explicitly. From these frequency-space singularities, we extract nonlinear relaxation modes that control the late-time behavior. When gapless modes are present, these modes produce power-law decay at late times. Our results give a systematic singularity-based description of nonlinear late-time relaxation in a broad class of macroscopic effective theories.

### [20] [Holographic Derivation of BPZ-Type Null State Equations in Higher Dimensional CFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04032)
*Kuo-Wei Huang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于 AdS/CFT 对偶，从引力侧推导出高维 CFT 的线性微分方程组，验证了先前提出的四维 CFT 方程（捕获最小扭曲多重应力张量算符的重求和贡献），并通过全息计算获得了超越近光锥区域的额外微分方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维大中心荷 CFT 中的 BPZ 零态方程（null-state equations）已被推广到高维线性微分方程形式，但缺乏引力理论的直接推导。本文旨在通过 AdS/CFT 对偶（AdS/CFT correspondence），从黑洞背景下的引力计算导出这些高维微分方程，并验证其正确性。

Method: 采用近边界展开（near-boundary expansion）分析黑洞背景下的轻标量场方程，利用体时空（bulk）微扰级数中的退耦机制（decoupling mechanism），在特定共形维度（conformal dimensions）下分离出低阶方程。

Result: 引力计算得到的结果与先前提出的四维 CFT 微分方程一致，这些方程捕获了最小扭曲多重应力张量算符（minimal-twist multi-stress tensor operators）的重求和贡献（resummed contributions）。此外，全息计算还可获得延伸至近光锥区域（near-lightcone regime）之外的额外 CFT 微分方程。

Conclusion: 从引力侧成功导出了高维 CFT 的线性微分方程组，验证了其与 BPZ 型方程推广的一致性，并扩展了全息方法在近光锥区域之外的适用性。

Abstract: A set of linear differential equations was recently put forward as higher-dimensional generalizations of the BPZ null-state equations in two-dimensional CFTs at large central charge. In this work, we derive these higher-dimensional equations from gravity, based on the AdS/CFT correspondence. A near-boundary expansion is employed to analyze a light scalar field equation in a black hole background. There is a decoupling mechanism in the bulk perturbative series at certain conformal dimensions, resulting in isolated lower-order equations. We find that the results agree with the previously proposed four-dimensional CFT equations, which capture the resummed contributions from minimal-twist multi-stress tensor operators. The holographic calculation also allows one to obtain additional CFT differential equations that extend beyond the near-lightcone regime.

### [21] [Jordan Frame in Supergravity and Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04041)
*Renata Kallosh*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在已有的超引力ξ-吸引子模型中，标量场与引力的耦合形式有限；本文旨在引入更具灵活性的非最小耦合机制，从而扩展吸引子模型的构造空间，并探索Palatini引力与超引力之间的兼容性边界。

Method: 通过规范固定（gauge-fixing）超共形作用量（superconformal action），分别导出由Kähler势（Kähler potential）$\mathcal{K}(z, \bar z)$定义的Einstein框架超引力，以及由框架函数（frame function）$Ω(z, \bar z)$与$\mathcal{K}(z, \bar z)$共同定义的Jordan框架超引力；在此基础上构造包含指数型和多项式型两类新型ξ-吸引子模型。

Result: 新模型中，指数型与多项式型ξ-吸引子展现出与Palatini吸引子相似的特征，但进一步分析表明，Palatini引力中的非最小标量耦合与独立仿射联络结构无法在超引力框架下实现嵌入。

Conclusion: 新型超引力ξ-吸引子模型在非最小耦合框架下具有结构优势，但Palatini引力无法作为超引力的有效推广，从而限定了超引力吸引子模型的构造路径。

Abstract: The superconformal action can be gauge-fixed in a gauge where is leads to the Einstein frame supergravity defined by a \K potential $\mathcal{K}(z, \bar z)$, or in a gauge where it leads to a Jordan frame supergravity defined by the frame function $Ω(z, \bar z)$, in addition to $\mathcal{K}(z, \bar z)$. We present {\it new supergravity $ξ$-attractor models with non-minimal coupling to gravity}, which offer some advantages over the previously known $ξ$-attractors.
  New attractors include exponential and polynomial $ξ$-attractors and have some features similar to those of the Palatini attractors. However, we show that the Palatini gravity with nonminimal scalar coupling and an independent affine connection has no supergravity embedding.

### [22] [Statistical analysis of virion-cell interactions mediated by peptide nanofibrils and peptide amphiphiles using STEM tomography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02934)
*Philipp Rieder,Julia La Roche,Orkun Furat,Annalena Kuhn,Lena Rauch-Wirth,Kübra Kaygisiz,Fabian Zech,Jan Münch,Clarissa Read,Rüdiger Groß,Volker Schmidt*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于扫描透射电子显微镜断层扫描（STEM tomography）的定量分析框架，用于客观量化肽纳米纤维（PNFs）和肽两亲物（PAs）在病毒转导增强过程中的超分子结构与病毒-细胞相互作用之间的关系。通过分析四种转导增强肽，发现所有肽都能有效捕获病毒，但在病毒空间受限程度上存在差异，这些差异反映了不同的空间组织策略，可能决定转导增强效果。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 所有四种肽均能高效捕获病毒粒子，导致游离病毒极少；但不同肽在病毒粒子被空间限制在细胞表面附近的严格程度上存在差异。

Conclusion: 肽间病毒空间组织的差异反映了不同的空间组织策略，这些策略可能是影响转导增强效果的关键因素。该框架为评估感染增强型纳米材料提供了一种新的通用方法，并为合理设计用于治疗性病毒递送的下一代肽组装体提供指导。

Abstract: Peptide nanofibrils (PNFs) and peptide amphiphiles (PAs) are promising tools for enhancing viral transduction and gene transfer. However, quantitative insight into how their supramolecular architecture governs virion-cell interactions is limited. Here, we introduce a framework for the acquisition, processing, and statistical analysis of scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM) tomograms to objectively quantify peptide-virion-cell interactions. Using four transduction-enhancing peptides (D4, Vectofusin-1, palmitic acid-PA (pal-PA), and eicosapentaenoic-PA (eic-PA)), peptide aggregate morphology, interfacial contact areas, and the spatial organization of virions with respect to peptides and cells were analyzed using advanced geometric descriptors. All peptides efficiently captured virions, resulting in few free virions, but they differ in how strictly virions were spatially confined near the cell surface. These differences reflect alternative spatial organization strategies, which are likely crucial factors influencing transduction-enhancing efficacy. Our approach provides a novel, generalizable method to evaluate infection-enhancing nanomaterials and guides the rational design of next-generation peptide assemblies for therapeutic viral delivery.

### [23] [Do Venture Capitalists Beat Random Allocation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03980)
*Max Sina Knicker,Jean-Philippe Bouchaud,Michael Benzaquen*

Main category: econ.GN

TL;DR: 本文通过将风险投资组合与约束随机基准（constrained random benchmark）进行对比，发现风险投资组合的回报分布与随机分配结果高度一致，在高回报右尾区域无显著差异，表明在厚尾分布（heavy-tailed distribution）环境中难以区分投资者技能与随机运气。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 风险投资回报由少数极端成功案例主导，高度偏斜的回报分布使得区分投资者技能（skill）与有利实现值（favorable realizations）极为困难。现有研究对VC投资组合是否真正体现专业能力存在争议，亟需系统性方法进行甄别。

Method: 研究通过构建约束随机基准（constrained random benchmark），在保留投资组合的时间（timing）、地理（geography）、行业构成（sector composition）和规模（portfolio size）等关键特征的前提下，随机化单个公司选择，从而对比实证VC组合与随机基准的分布差异。此外，还引入基于排名的基准分布（rank-based benchmark distribution）来评估每一横截面位置上的超额表现。

Result: 实证VC组合的回报分布与随机基准惊人地接近：高倍数回报（high-multiple outcomes）的右尾在统计上无法与随机分配区分；低端分布的偏差微小且对零回报的处理敏感，最多仅能提供关于下行风险改善的微弱证据。即使表现最好的VC组合，其回报也未超过随机抽样中相同排名的预期结果。

Conclusion: 风险投资组合的回报结果在很大程度上与约束随机分配一致，凸显在厚尾投资环境中识别总体技能（aggregate skill）的困难性。类似的结论同样适用于金融分析师预测未来盈利的表现。

Abstract: Venture capital outcomes are dominated by a small number of extreme successes, making it difficult to distinguish investor skill from favorable realizations in a highly skewed return distribution. We study this question by comparing empirical VC portfolios to a constrained random benchmark that preserves key portfolio characteristics, including timing, geography, sector composition, and portfolio size, while randomizing individual company selection. Across funding stages, empirical portfolio distributions appear remarkably close to their random benchmarks. We find no evidence that portfolio construction increases the probability of high-multiple outcomes: the right tail remains statistically indistinguishable from random allocation. Deviations in the lower part of the distribution are small and sensitive to the interpretation of zero outcomes, suggesting at most weak evidence of downside improvement. We further introduce a rank-based benchmark distribution to evaluate outperformance at each position in the cross-section. This analysis shows that even the best-performing portfolios do not exceed the outcomes expected for their rank under random sampling. Our results suggest that VC portfolio outcomes are largely consistent with constrained random allocation, highlighting the difficulty of identifying aggregate skill in heavy-tailed investment environments. A similar conclusion holds for the performance of financial analysts in predicting future earnings.

</details>

### [24] [Solution of second-order hyperbolic quasilinear systems with spatio-characteristic initial data in weighted Sobolev-type spaces under finite differentiability assumptions on the data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03122)
*Louokdom Tamto Paul Giscard,Duplex Elvis Houpa Danga,Kouakep Tchaptchie Yannick*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文旨在建立带权重的Sobolev型空间中时空特征二阶拟线性双曲问题解的存在唯一性定理，以澄清和完善H. Muller Zum Hagen与H.J. Seifert于1977年的工作；该结果被用于后续研究中建立二阶拟线性Goursat问题的半全局存在唯一性结果，并最终应用于调和规范真空爱因斯坦方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清和完善H. Muller Zum Hagen与H.J. Seifert（Gen. Rel. and Gravit., 1977）关于带权重的Sobolev型空间中时空特征二阶拟线性双曲问题的已有工作。

Method: 在带权重的Sobolev型空间（weighted Sobolev-type spaces）中，对时空特征（spatio-characteristic）二阶拟线性双曲问题（second-order quasilinear hyperbolic problems）建立解的存在唯一性理论；该结果进一步被用于处理二阶拟线性Goursat问题（second-order quasilinear Goursat problems），其中二阶导数的系数对未知函数呈线性依赖。

Result: 建立了时空特征二阶拟线性双曲问题在带权重Sobolev型空间中的存在唯一性解；在此基础上，得到了二阶拟线性Goursat问题的半全局存在唯一性（semi-global existence and uniqueness）结果。

Conclusion: 该理论结果将被应用于调和规范（harmonic gauge）下的真空爱因斯坦方程（vacuum Einstein equations），为广义相对论中的相关偏微分方程分析提供严格的数学基础。

Abstract: The aim of this work is to establish an existence and uniqueness solution for spatiocharacteristic second-order quasilinear hyperbolic problems in Sobolev type spaces with weights to clarify and complete the previous work done by H. Muller Zum Hagen and H.J. Seifert, Gen. Rel. and Gravit. 1977. We use this result in P. G. Louokdom tamto, PhD thesis ongoing, 2026 to establish a semi-global existence and uniqueness result for second-order quasilinear Goursat problems where the coefficients of the second derivatives depend linearly on the unknown in weighted Sobolev-type spaces, which we will apply to the harmonic gauge vacuum Einstein equations

</details>


### [25] [Late-time tails for linear waves on radially symmetric stationary spacetimes of two space dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03220)
*Onyx Gautam*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了在(2+1)维闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）的径向对称平稳扰动上，线性波动方程解的晚期渐近行为的主阶项正比于$u^{-1/2}v^{-1/2}$，该形式恰好是闵可夫斯基时空上波动方程的解。证明改编了Gajic关于Schwarzschild时空中反平方势波动方程的物理空间技术，并将Dafermos–Rodnianski的$r^p$加权能量估计（weighted energy estimates）推广至二维空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弯曲时空或扰动时空背景下，理解线性波动方程解的长时间渐近行为（long-time asymptotics）是广义相对论（general relativity）和双曲型偏微分方程理论的重要问题。本文旨在确定(2+1)维闵可夫斯基时空在径向对称稳态扰动下，波动方程解在晚期的主导衰减率及其具体形式。

Method: 方法核心是改编Gajic在Schwarzschild时空中处理反平方势（inverse-square potential）波动方程的物理空间技术（physical space techniques），并将其应用至二维径向对称扰动时空。具体而言，将Dafermos–Rodnianski提出的$r^p$加权能量估计（$r^p$-weighted energy estimates）从三维推广至二维空间，以捕获解的晚期衰减行为。

Result: 得到的主要结果是：在(2+1)维闵可夫斯基时空的径向对称稳态扰动上，线性波动方程解的晚期渐近主阶项为$u^{-1/2}v^{-1/2}$（其中$u$和$v$为双零坐标（double null coordinates）），该形式与闵可夫斯基时空上的波动方程解一致。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了对闵可夫斯基时空进行径向对称稳态扰动后，波动方程解的晚期主导衰减率在形式上保持不变，仍为$u^{-1/2}v^{-1/2}$。这一结论证实了在该类扰动背景下，解的渐近行为具有某种稳定性，并展示了$r^p$加权能量估计方法在低维扰动时空中的适用性。

Abstract: We show that the leading-order term in the late-time asymptotics of solutions to the linear wave equation on radially symmetric stationary perturbations of $(2 + 1)$-dimensional Minkowski space is proportional to $u^{-1/2}v^{-1/2}$ (which solves the wave equation on Minkowski space), where $u$ and $v$ are double null coordinates. Our proof adapts the physical space techniques in the work of Gajic (arXiv:2203.15838) on the wave equation with an inverse-square potential on the Schwarzschild spacetime. In particular, we extend the $r^p$-weighted energy estimates of Dafermos--Rodnianski (arXiv:0910.4957) to two space dimensions.

</details>


### [26] [Stability of de Sitter Space and Expansion at the Conformal Boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03481)
*Maurus Leimbacher*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文利用类似arXiv:2409.15460的方法，对德西特时空（de Sitter space）作为爱因斯坦真空方程（带正宇宙常数）解的非线性稳定性给出了新证明，并建立了其共形边界处扰动的精确展开与散射数据之间的一一对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前人工作的基础上，提供德西特时空在$n+1$维（$n\geq3$）爱因斯坦真空方程中非线性稳定性的新证明，并阐明扰动时空在共形边界处的精确展开结构，以建立与散射数据之间的对应关系。

Method: 利用方程中的规范自由度（gauge freedom），对扰动时空在将来共形边界（future conformal boundary）处证明一个精确的展开；依赖Fefferman和Graham（1985）以及arXiv:0710.0919、arXiv:1705.09674和arXiv:2311.02739的结果来建立展开结构与散射数据之间的对应。

Result: 在奇数空间维数（$n$为奇数）下，共形重缩放度规（conformally rescaled metric）在将来共形边界处是光滑的；在偶数空间维数（$n$为偶数）下，光滑性等价于边界度规的阻碍张量（obstruction tensor）为零，否则该度规是对数光滑的（log smooth）。这些结果同样适用于渐近德西特空间（asymptotically de Sitter spaces）。

Conclusion: 建立了在一般维度下，接近德西特空间的爱因斯坦真空方程解与定义在共形边界上的散射数据（scattering data）之间的一一对应关系。

Abstract: Using an approach similar to arXiv:2409.15460, we give a new proof of the nonlinear stability of de Sitter space as a solution to the Einstein vacuum equations with positive cosmological constant in $n+1$ dimensions, with $n\geq3$. Using the gauge freedom of the equations, we are able to prove a precise expansion of the perturbed spacetime at the conformal boundary. In $n=$ odd spatial dimensions, the conformally rescaled metric is smooth up to the future conformal boundary and in $n=$ even spatial dimensions it is smooth if and only if the obstruction tensor of the boundary metric vanishes; if not, then the conformally rescaled metric is log smooth at the boundary. These results also hold for asymptotically de Sitter spaces. Using the results of Fefferman and Graham (1985, Conformal invariants), arXiv:0710.0919, arXiv:1705.09674 and arXiv:2311.02739, the structure of our expansion allows us to establish a 1-1 correspondence between solutions to the Einstein vacuum equations close to de Sitter space and scattering data prescribed on the conformal boundary in general dimension.

</details>

### [27] [Improved muon energy estimation using a detailed model of multiple Coulomb scattering in the MicroBooNE LArTPC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03048)
*P. Abratenko,D. Andrade Aldana,J. Asaadi,A. Ashkenazi,S. Balasubramanian,B. Baller,A. Barnard,G. Barr,D. Barrow,J. Barrow,V. Basque,J. Bateman,B. Behera,O. Benevides Rodrigues,S. Berkman,A. Bhat,M. Wongjirad,K. Wresilo,W. Wu,E. Yandel,T. Yang,L. E. Yates,H. W. Yu,G. P. Zeller,J. Zennamo,C. Zhang,Y. Zhang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出一种改进的基于多次库仑散射（multiple Coulomb scattering, MCS）的μ子能量估计技术，在MicroBooNE探测器中通过测量径迹偏转来估算能量。该技术相比此前方法在分辨率、偏差和数据-模型一致性方面均有显著提升：对全包含事例，偏差<1%，分辨率在4.3%–10%之间；对出射事例（μ子能量<2 GeV），偏差<2%，分辨率在7%–17%之间，远优于此前方法（分辨率大一倍，偏差达20%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于多次库仑散射（multiple Coulomb scattering, MCS）的μ子能量估计方法在MicroBooNE探测器中性能有限，存在分辨率较差和偏差较大的问题，亟需一种能够更好处理探测器非理想效应的改进技术。

Method: 通过测量μ子路径在MicroBooNE探测器内部由多次库仑散射（multiple Coulomb scattering, MCS）引起的偏转来估计能量，并在方法中引入多项创新以更好捕捉探测器的非理想效应（detector non-idealizations）。

Result: 对全包含（fully contained）事件，估计偏差<1%，分辨率在μ子能量从0.1 GeV增至2 GeV时从4.3%变化至10%。对出射事例（μ子能量<2 GeV，且重建径迹长度≥1米），估计偏差<2%，分辨率在7%–17%之间。此前方法在同一能量区间分辨率大一倍，偏差达20%。数据-模型拟合优度（goodness-of-fit）检验表明估计器性能与模型不确定性吻合良好。

Conclusion: 提出的改进MCS能量估计技术在分辨率、偏差和数据-模型一致性方面均显著优于此前MicroBooNE采用的同类方法，验证了该方法在低能μ子能量估计中的有效性。

Abstract: We present an improved technique for estimating a muon's energy by measuring the deflections along its path inside the MicroBooNE detector from multiple Coulomb scattering (MCS). This approach implements several innovations that better capture detector non-idealizations compared to previous MCS-based muon energy estimators. As a result, it achieves improved resolution, reduced bias, and better data-model agreement. Using model simulation, for fully contained events the estimated bias is within 1% and the estimated resolution varies from 4.3% to 10% as muon energy increases from 0.1 GeV to 2 GeV. For events with particles exiting the detector volume, at least a meter of reconstructed muon track, and a muon energy below 2 GeV, the estimated bias is less than 2% and the estimated resolution varies from 7% to 17% over muon energy. These demonstrate significant improvements over the performance of previous work using an MCS-based energy estimator at MicroBooNE, which achieves twice as large a resolution as well as a bias of 20% over the same energy region. Data-model goodness-of-fit studies are used to validate the estimator's performance on data, showing good agreement within model uncertainties.

Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,J. Zhao,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于5.8 fb⁻¹ 数据样本，利用B±→DK±和B±→Dπ±衰变道及D→KS⁰π⁺π⁻/KS⁰K⁺K⁻过程，首次使用升级后的LHCb探测器测量CKM角γ，测得γ=(68.1±6.7)°。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CKM角γ（Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa angle γ）是描述夸克混合与CP破坏（CP violation）的关键标准模型参数，其精确测量对于检验标准模型和寻找新物理具有重要意义。利用升级后的LHCb探测器进行首次测量，旨在验证探测器性能并提高γ角的测量精度。

Method: 利用B±→DK±和B±→Dπ±衰变道，其中D介子衰变至KS⁰π⁺π⁻或KS⁰K⁺K⁻，基于综合亮度（integrated luminosity）为5.8 fb⁻¹的数据样本。通过分析B⁺和B⁻介子中D衰变过程的Dalitz图（Dalitz plot）分布差异来观测CP破坏，从而导出CKM角γ。

Result: CKM角γ被测定为γ=(68.1±6.7)°。此外，所研究的B介子衰变模式相关的其他参数也被同时测量。

Conclusion: 这是利用升级后LHCb探测器对CKM角γ的首次测量，成功观测到CP破坏现象，并为后续更高精度的测量奠定了基础。

Abstract: A measurement of the CKM angle $γ$ using the decay channels $B^{\pm}\rightarrow DK^{\pm}$ and $B^{\pm}\rightarrow Dπ^{\pm}$, where the $D$ meson decays to $D\rightarrow K_{\rm S}^{0}π^{+}π^{-}$ or $D\rightarrow K_{\rm S}^{0}K^{+}K^{-}$, is performed with a data sample corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 5.8 fb$^{-1}$, collected during 2024 by the upgraded LHCb experiment. $C\!P$ violation is observed through a difference in the distributions of the Dalitz plot of the $D$ decay between the $B^{+}$ and $B^{-}$ mesons. The CKM angle $γ$ is determined to be $γ=(68.1\pm 6.7)^{\circ}$. Other parameters related to the examined $B$ meson decay modes are also measured. This is the first measurement of the CKM angle $γ$ using the upgraded LHCb detector.

</details>


### [29] [The LHCb Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03745)
*Marcel H. M. Merk,Niels Tuning*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文系统回顾了LHCb实验的历史动机、设计原理与实验方法，详述了从专门研究B介子CP破坏和稀有衰变的实验到LHC前向区通用实验的演变过程、探测器升级、实验技术、主要物理成果，并展望了高亮度LHC时代的第二次升级计划。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHCb实验最初是为研究B介子（B-meson）系统中的CP破坏（CP violation）和稀有衰变（rare decays）而设计的专用实验，后演变为LHC前向区（forward direction）的通用实验，其动机在于利用LHC的高亮度和前向区域独特的运动学覆盖，拓展对味物理（flavour physics）及其他前沿物理的探测能力。

Method: 文章通过介绍原始LHCb装置及其升级版的关键探测器组件，强调了前向区域事件高效重建的设计特征，并讨论了前向谱仪（forward spectrometer）特有的实验技术，说明如何将详细的探测器信息转化为用于物理分析的事例级观测量（event-level observables）。

Result: LHCb在CP破坏、稀有衰变、谱学（spectroscopy）、长寿命粒子（long-lived particles）、W和Z玻色子物理以及重离子物理（heavy ion physics）等领域取得了重要物理成果。文章还将其性能与其他实验进行了比较。

Conclusion: 本文在总结LHCb现有成就的基础上，简要提出了在高亮度LHC（High Luminosity LHC）时代进行第二次升级的未来规划。

Abstract: We present an overview including the historical motivation, design principles, and experimental methodology of the LHCb experiment. Originally conceived as a dedicated experiment for CP violation and rare decays in the B-meson sector, LHCb evolved into a general-purpose experiment for physics in the forward direction at the LHC, while maintaining its core optimization on flavour physics. We review the key detector components for both the original LHCb set-up as well as its upgrade, with emphasis on design features that enable efficient reconstruction of forward-region events. Experimental techniques specific to the forward spectrometer are discussed, highlighting how detailed detector information is translated into event-level observables used in physics analyses. We present an overview of LHCb's major physics results on CP violation, rare decays, spectroscopy, long-lived particles, W- and Z-boson physics and heavy ion physics. In all cases we focus on the conceptual methods, while referring to the literature for detailed discussions. We end this review by comparing LHCb's performance to other experiments and shortly present the concept for a future, second upgrade of LHCb at the High Luminosity LHC.

</details>


### [30] [Searching for long-lived particles with the ILD experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03908)
*Jan Klamka,Aleksander Filip Żarnecki*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于国际大型探测器（International Large Detector, ILD）的全模拟研究，探讨了未来正负电子对撞机（e⁺e⁻ colliders）上利用时间投影室（time projection chamber, TPC）进行长寿命粒子（long-lived particle, LLP）搜索的潜力，分析了位移顶点（displaced vertices）和扭结径迹（kinked tracks）两种信号特征，给出了模型无关分析以及希格斯玻色子衰变到LLP场景下的预期排除极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来正负电子对撞机为长寿命粒子（long-lived particle, LLP）搜索提供了独特机遇，但LLP信号通常涉及复杂拓扑结构，需要高精度探测器进行有效识别。本文旨在利用国际大型探测器（ILD）中基于气体时间投影室（TPC）的主跟踪系统，探索其对LLP搜索的潜力。

Method: 采用全模拟（full simulation）方法，基于ILD探测器开展LLP搜索研究。利用气体TPC作为主跟踪装置，分析了位移顶点（displaced vertices）和扭结径迹（kinked tracks）两种特征信号。研究涵盖了包含极软位移径迹以及高能近似共线径迹的挑战性末态，并考虑了束流诱导相互作用和其他标准模型（Standard Model）过程产生的背景。

Result: 对于模型无关分析以及希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）衰变到LLP的场景，在多种LLP寿命范围内给出了预期的排除极限（expected exclusion limits）。

Conclusion: ILD由于TPC作为主跟踪设备，在LLP搜索方面具有优越前景，能够有效处理复杂信号拓扑并给出有竞争力的排除极限。

Abstract: Future e$^+$e$^-$ colliders provide a unique opportunity for long-lived particle (LLP) searches. We present a full simulation study of LLP searches using the International Large Detector (ILD), where a gaseous time projection chamber as the main tracking device provides excellent prospects for LLP searches. Signatures of displaced vertices and kinked tracks are explored. We study challenging final states involving both very soft displaced tracks and boosted, nearly collinear tracks. Backgrounds from beam-induced interactions and other Standard Model processes are considered. We present expected exclusion limits for a model-independent analyses, as well as for Higgs boson decays to LLPs, for a range of LLP lifetimes.

</details>

### [31] [Predicting Euler Characteristics and Constructing Topological Structure Using Machine Learning Techniques](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02947)
*Gyunghun Yu,Seong Min Park,Han Gyu Yoon,Tae Jung Moon,Jun Woo Choi,Hee Young Kwon,Changyeon Won*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种仅使用单张几何图像，通过神经网络生成自旋构型并计算斯格明子数（skyrmion number）来预测图像欧拉示性数（Euler characteristic）的方法，无需大型数据集；同时引入磁性哈密顿量作为物理信息损失函数，约束自旋构型的非唯一性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统提取拓扑性质（如欧拉示性数）的方法通常依赖大型数据集或标注，本文受固体物理学（solid-state physics）中从自旋场分析推导磁结构拓扑性质的启发，探索仅用单张几何图像预测拓扑属性的可能性。

Method: 模型首先从输入图像生成单位向量场（unit vector field），将其解释为自旋构型（spin configuration）；然后通过计算该自旋构型的斯格明子数（skyrmion number）来预测欧拉示性数。为约束自旋构型的非唯一性，额外引入包含交换相互作用（exchange interaction）、Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya（DM）相互作用和磁各向异性（anisotropy）的磁性哈密顿量（magnetic Hamiltonian）作为物理信息损失函数。

Result: 网络能够在没有真实手性自旋构型（ground-truth chiral spin configurations）的情况下，仅依赖单张简单几何图像和直接的斯格明子数计算，学会构造手性磁纹理（chiral magnetic textures）。模型在复杂几何形状上验证了有效性，并展示了在实际任务中的适用性。

Conclusion: 该方法无需大规模数据集即可从图像中提取拓扑性质，且通过物理约束解决了自旋构型的非唯一性问题，为拓扑特征提取与物理启发式深度学习的结合提供了新思路。

Abstract: This study proposes a novel approach to extract topological properties, specifically the Euler characteristic, from input images using neural networks without relying on large pre-existing datasets but with a single geometric image. Inspired by solid-state physics, where topological properties of magnetic structures are derived from spin field analysis, our model generates a unit vector field from an image, interpreted as a spin configuration. The Euler characteristic is then predicted by computing the skyrmion number of this generated spin configuration. Remarkably, the network learns to construct chiral magnetic textures without access to ground-truth chiral spin configurations, relying instead on only a single, simple geometric image and the straightforward skyrmion number computation. Furthermore, spin configurations generated by independently trained networks can be non-unique due to inherent degrees of freedom. To constrain these degrees of freedom and further refine the spin configuration, we incorporate a magnetic Hamiltonian, comprising exchange interaction, Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya (DM) interaction, and anisotropy, as an additional, physics-informed loss function. We validate the model's efficacy on complex geometrical shapes and demonstrate its applicability to practical tasks.

</details>


### [32] [Analytic Bridge Diffusions for Controlled Path Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02961)
*Michael Chertkov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出LQ-GM-PID方法，将经典线性-二次-高斯（LQG）随机控制结构重构为路径积分扩散（PID）类型的传输问题，在保留线性-二次骨干的同时，将终端状态调控替换为预设终端概率密度，并允许初始与终端律为高斯混合（GM），从而在无需神经网络或随机模拟的情况下实现桥扩散的闭式求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有桥扩散（bridge-diffusion）方法通常依赖神经网络学习得分（score）或漂移场（drift field），需要内部随机模拟循环，计算成本高且缺乏解析可解释性。本文旨在识别一类足够广泛且可解析求解的桥扩散子类，以提供精确参考模型。

Method: 将经典LQG随机控制框架重新诠释为路径积分扩散（Path Integral Diffusion, PID）类型的传输问题；保留线性动力学、高斯噪声与二次代价的LQG骨架，但将终端状态调控目标替换为预设的终端概率密度，并允许初始与终端分布为高斯混合（Gaussian Mixture, GM），形成LQ-GM-PID框架。

Result: 在2D走廊任务、2D多入口传输任务以及d=32、M=16个高斯混合终端模态的高维扩展实验中，该方法均可在笔记本电脑上以低于50毫秒的解析预计算时间完成。该方法将桥扩散从仅用于终端目标匹配扩展为路径塑形（path shaping）工具。

Conclusion: LQ-GM-PID可定位为现有先进神经桥扩散与生成传输方法的解析可解参考模型，为检验神经近似、得分估计、路径塑形目标及协议学习过程提供可控的精确对照基准。

Abstract: Most modern bridge-diffusion methods achieve finite-time transport by specifying an interpolation, Schrödinger-bridge, or stochastic-control objective and then learning the associated score or drift field with a neural network. In contrast, we identify a restricted but sufficiently broad and analytically solvable class in which the score, intermediate marginals, and protocol gradients are available in closed form without inner stochastic simulation loops and without neural networks in the optimization loop. We recast the classical linear--quadratic--Gaussian (LQG) stochastic-control structure as a transport problem of the Path Integral Diffusion (PID) type. In classical LQG control, linear dynamics, Gaussian noise, and quadratic costs lead to Riccati equations and closed-form optimal feedback. In LQ-GM-PID, we retain the linear--quadratic stochastic-control backbone, but replace terminal state regulation by a prescribed terminal probability density and allow both the initial and terminal laws to be Gaussian Mixtures (GM).
  Moreover, LQ-GM-PID turns bridge diffusion from a tool for terminal target matching alone into a tool for path shaping. We demonstrate this on a 2D corridor task, a 2D multi-entrance transport task, and a high-dimensional scaling study with $d=32$ and $M=16$ Gaussian-mixture terminal modes, all with sub-50\,ms analytic precompute on a laptop. We position LQ-GM-PID as an analytically solvable reference model for the state-of-the-art neural bridge-diffusion and generative-transport methods: a controlled setting in which neural approximations, score estimates, path-shaping objectives, and protocol-learning procedures can be tested against exact quantities.

</details>


### [33] [Finite-Size Gradient Transport in Large Language Model Pretraining: From Cascade Size to Intensive Transport Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02968)
*Ping Wang,Yan-Qi Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出一个基于五个可观测量的有限尺寸梯度输运框架，用于分析真实语言模型训练中的级联动力学。通过对Pico-LM和Pythia两个模型家族的原始梯度测量，发现两者共享近统一的级联尺寸骨架，但处于不同的输运区间：Pico-LM表现出正持续时间标度与负密集效率标度，而Pythia接近D=1基线。两个模型家族在幂律可压缩性和性能关联通道上也存在系统性差异，支持一个可复用的输运测量框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型训练研究缺乏一个能够同时捕获级联尺寸、持续时间、绝对输运和密集输运效率的统一测量框架。作者旨在引入一个基于有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）的梯度输运框架，通过五个可观测量的系统测量来区分不同模型家族在训练动力学上的差异，并为神经标度律（neural scaling laws）提供实证基础。

Method: 基于五个可观测量的有限尺寸梯度输运框架：D（级联尺寸）、z（持续时间）、β（绝对输运）、δ与v_rel（密集输运效率）。对Pico-LM的原始梯度在四个尺度与125个对齐步长（aligned steps）上进行直接分析，同时构建基于153个对齐检查点差分更新场（checkpoint-difference update fields）的五尺度Pythia配套数据集。两种模型家族均采用相同的代数闭包（algebraic closure）进行分析，并引入随机化场控制（randomized-field controls）作为零假设基准。

Result: 两种模型家族共享近统一的级联尺寸骨架（near-unity cascade-size backbone），但处于不同的输运区间：Pico-LM表现出正持续时间标度与负密集效率标度，而Pythia接近D=1基线且仅具有弱正效率尺度依赖性。随机化场控制显示两者在密集通道和持续时间通道上几乎匹配的零基底（null floors），表明差异源自对共享零骨架的不同真实偏离。在步进幂律可压缩性（stepwise power-law compressibility）方面，Pico-LM保持清晰的持续时间和效率幂律，而Pythia保留尺寸骨架但在这些通道上表现出较弱的单斜率可压缩性。外部性能关联呈通道级别分布，主要由v_rel和归一化级联持续时间承载，D(t)仅作为共享尺寸骨架。

Conclusion: 该研究支持一个可复用的输运测量框架，但并未声称存在普适固定点（universal fixed point）或从第一性原理导出神经标度律。梯度输运框架能够有效区分不同模型家族的训练动力学特征，为后续理解语言模型训练中的有限尺寸效应和级联行为提供了可量化的分析工具。

Abstract: We introduce a finite-size gradient-transport framework for real language-model training, based on five observables $(D,z,β,δ,v_{\mathrm{rel}})$ that separate cascade size, duration, absolute transport, and intensive transport efficiency. We analyze direct raw-gradient measurements from Pico-LM across four scales and 125 aligned steps, together with a five-scale Pythia companion dataset built from 153 aligned checkpoint-difference update fields. The same algebraic closure holds in both families, and both share a near-unity cascade-size backbone, but they occupy distinct transport regimes: Pico-LM shows positive duration scaling and negative intensive-efficiency scaling, whereas Pythia remains near the $D=1$ baseline with only weak positive efficiency scale dependence. Randomized-field controls give nearly matched null floors in the intensive and duration channels, indicating that the contrast reflects different real departures from a shared null skeleton rather than different null calibrations. The families also differ in stepwise power-law compressibility: Pico-LM retains clean duration and efficiency power laws, whereas Pythia preserves the size backbone but shows weaker one-slope compressibility in those channels. External performance associations are correspondingly channel-level, carried mainly by $v_{\mathrm{rel}}$ and normalized cascade duration, while $D(t)$ acts as a shared size backbone without a significant exponent-level performance association. These results support a reusable transport measurement framework without claiming a universal fixed point or a first-principles derivation of neural scaling laws.

### [34] [Higher categories of bordisms with geometric structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03453)
*Daniel Grady,Dmitri Pavlov*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个公理系统，唯一地定义了携带几何数据的配边（bordisms）的(∞,d)-范畴，并基于“流形上的场”（field on a manifold）的一般概念，构建了一个对称幺半（symmetric monoidal）的(∞,d)-配边范畴，证明其满足所提公理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为携带几何数据的配边范畴建立一个公理化的唯一性描述，并统一涵盖光滑流形（smooth manifolds）、复流形（complex manifolds）、超流形（super manifolds）、形式光滑流形（formal smooth manifolds）等多种底流形类别，以及黎曼度量、主丛联络、共形结构等多种场结构。

Method: 引入一组公理系统；定义“流形上的场”的一般概念，将黎曼度量（Riemannian metrics）、带联络的主丛（principal bundles with connection）、共形结构（conformal structures）及传统切触结构（tangential structures）等作为特例纳入统一框架；在此基础上构造对称幺半(∞,d)-配边范畴并验证公理。

Result: 成功构造了一个对称幺半的(∞,d)-配边范畴，该范畴适用于多种指定底流形和场结构，且证明此范畴满足所提出的公理系统。

Conclusion: 该公理系统为携带几何数据的配边范畴提供了唯一的范畴论刻画，为后续在量子场论（quantum field theory）和拓扑序（topological order）等领域的应用奠定了严格的数学基础。

Abstract: We introduce a system of axioms that uniquely defines an (infinity,d)-category of bordisms equipped with geometric data. The underlying manifolds of these bordisms may be smooth, complex, super, or formal smooth manifolds, as well as any class of manifolds satisfying conditions specified in this paper. We develop a general notion of a field on a manifold, encompassing structures such as Riemannian metrics, principal bundles with connection, conformal structures, and traditional tangential structures. Using this framework, we construct a symmetric monoidal (infinity,d)-category of bordisms with prescribed underlying manifolds and fields, and prove that it satisfies our axioms.

### [35] [Multistable energy landscapes for adaptive microscopic machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03077)
*Melody Xuan Lim,Zexi Liang,Gabriel Alkuino,Jason Z. Kim,Itay Griniasty,Teng Zhang,Paul L. McEuen,Itai Cohen*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文展示了通过设计具有多稳态（multistability）的能量景观（energy landscape），使微型机器在相同外部驱动场下实现多种构型与动态响应，从而提升其自主性。通过三个实验案例逐步验证：双稳态机械构型、双自由度动态响应驱动环境位移、以及具有连续对称性的微型机器自主实现运动（locomotion）并自适应响应外力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前合成微型机器（synthetic microscopic machines）的功能通常由外部场直接决定，缺乏对环境变化的自适应能力。为实现自适应响应，亟需在相同外部驱动场下编程多种功能，使机器内部状态决定具体执行何种功能。

Method: 论文采用设计具有多稳态的能量景观的方法，使微型机器在相同外部驱动场（如磁场）下呈现多种构型与动态响应。通过三个递进式实验展示：双稳态能量景观写入微型器件、引入第二自由度实现不同动态响应、以及利用连续对称性实现自主运动与自适应行为。

Result: 三个实验示例均成功实现：1) 双稳态微型器件在相同外部磁场下呈现两种稳定机械构型；2) 增加第二自由度后，器件对相同磁场产生不同动态响应，并驱动环境净位移；3) 具有连续对称性的微型机器将单自由度磁驱动自主转化为运动，并自适应响应其他机器施加的力。

Conclusion: 通过设计多稳态能量景观，能够在相同外部驱动场下实现多种构型与动态响应，从而赋予微型机器更高层次的自主性（autonomy），为构建具备自适应能力的合成微型机器提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The past few years have seen great strides in our ability to build synthetic microscopic machines. However, the function of such machines is often controlled directly by externally applied fields that deterministically specify the instantaneous machine dynamics. A crucial step towards machines that can respond adaptively to changes in their environment is the ability to program multiple functions that actuate under the same external driving field, so that their internal state dictates which function is executed. Here, we demonstrate that energy landscapes with designed multistability enable the same externally applied field to drive multiple configurations and dynamic responses in microscopic machines, enabling increasing levels of autonomy. We show three examples. First, we write a bistable energy landscape into a microscopic device, enabling the device to exhibit two stable mechanical configurations under the same external magnetic field. Next, adding a second degree of freedom enables differing dynamic responses to the same external magnetic field, which we direct into net displacement of the environment. Finally, we demonstrate how a microscopic machine with a continuous symmetry autonomously channels a single degree-of-freedom magnetic actuation into locomotion and adaptively responds to forces induced by other machines.

</details>


### [36] [Equilibrium fluctuations of a quasi-spherical vesicle: role of the membrane dissipation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03201)
*Petia M. Vlahovska,Rony Granek*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文理论研究了准球形囊泡（quasi-spherical vesicle）上热驱动的曲率和脂质密度涨落，考虑了单层粘度（monolayer viscosity）和层间摩擦（intermonolayer friction）导致的耗散。理论预测膜曲率使得长波起伏对膜粘度敏感，并加速了脂质密度涨落的弛豫。与平面膜中预测的2/3反常扩散指数不同，亚微米脂质体在纳秒时间尺度上可能不存在清晰的拉伸指数（stretched-exponential）弛豫行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的平面膜涨落理论（如Zilman和Granek提出的2/3反常扩散指数）在准球形囊泡体系中是否仍然适用尚不明确，特别是曲率效应和层间耗散机制对动态粗糙度（dynamic roughness）和动态结构因子（Dynamic Structure Factor）的影响有待澄清。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，研究准球形囊泡的热致曲率涨落和脂质密度涨落动力学，在模型中纳入单层粘度和层间摩擦造成的耗散效应。

Result: 膜曲率使长波长的起伏模式对膜粘度变得敏感；脂质密度涨落的弛豫速率因曲率效应而加快。亚微米脂质体在纳秒时间尺度上的动态结构因子可能不呈现清晰的拉伸指数弛豫行为，这与平面膜体系预测的2/3反常扩散指数不同。

Conclusion: 准球形囊泡的曲率效应从根本上改变了膜涨落的动力学行为，特别是在短时间和亚微米尺度上，经典平面膜理论所预言的拉伸指数弛豫和反常扩散指数不再直接适用。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the thermally-driven curvature and lipid density fluctuations of a quasi-spherical vesicle, accounting for the dissipation due to monolayer viscosity and intermonolayer friction. The theory predicts that membrane curvature makes long-wavelength undulations sensitive to membrane viscosity and speeds up the relaxation of the lipid density fluctuations. Implications for the dynamic roughness and Dynamic Structure Factor measurements of submicron liposomes on nano-second time scales are discussed. Specifically, a clear stretched-exponential relaxation regime may not exist, in contrast to the behavior of planar membranes for which an anomalous diffusion exponent of 2/3 has been predicted [Zilman and Granek, Phys. Rev. Lett. (1996)].

### [37] [Sparkling bubbles in chiral active fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03404)
*Alessandro Petrini,Raphaël Maire,Umberto Marini Bettolo Marconi,Lorenzo Caprini*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 论文研究了由反向粒子通过奇异性相互作用（odd interactions）构成的手性主动流体（chiral active fluid），发现在最佳堆积分数下会出现旋转气泡，并观察到气泡的动态不稳定性——自发破裂与重构，呈现类似过饱和液体的自发闪烁（sparkling-like）行为。粗粒化流体力学理论（coarse-grained hydrodynamic theory）成功预测了这些现象，揭示了其内在非线性本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索手性主动流体中由奇异性相互作用（即横向力）引起的新奇集体行为，特别是非均匀相中旋转气泡的形成机制与动态不稳定性。

Method: 采用排斥性粒子系统模拟，粒子间通过奇异性相互作用传递角动量；同时构建粗粒化流体力学理论（coarse-grained hydrodynamic theory）进行理论预测。

Result: 手性诱导出由旋转气泡组成的非均匀相，其形成在最佳堆积分数下最为显著；气泡在稳态中展现出动态不稳定性（dynamic instability），即自发破裂与重构，呈现类似过饱和液体的自发闪烁行为。

Conclusion: 粗粒化流体力学理论成功预测了气泡及闪烁气泡现象，表明这些集体行为具有内在非线性（intrinsic non-linearity）；研究结果呼吁在颗粒自旋体（granular spinners）或旋转胶体（spinning colloids）中进行实验验证。

Abstract: We study an inertial chiral active fluid, formed by repulsive particles that transfer angular momentum through odd interactions, i.e. transverse forces. Chirality induces an inhomogeneous phase, consisting of rotating bubbles, whose formation is favored at an optimal packing fraction. In this regime, we discover that bubbles may be dynamically unstable, breaking up and reforming in the steady state, thereby showing a spontaneous sparkling-like behavior reminiscent of supersaturated liquids. Bubbles and sparkling bubbles are predicted by a coarse-grained hydrodynamic theory, revealing the intrinsic non-linearity of these collective phenomena, and call for experimental verifications in granular spinners or spinning colloids.

### [38] [Dynamic properties of a confined quasi-two-dimensional granular fluid driven by a stochastic bath with friction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03455)
*David González Méndez,Rubén Gómez González,Vicente Garzó*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于Enskog动力学方程框架，研究受限准二维颗粒流体在中等密度下的动态性质。通过$\Delta$-模型引入能量注入，并考虑间隙气体的粘性阻力和类朗之万随机项；采用Chapman-Enskog方法解析推导了Navier-Stokes输运系数和冷却速率，理论预测与直接模拟蒙特卡洛（DSMC）结果高度吻合，表明外驱动显著改变了输运系数，且线性稳定性分析表明均匀稳态在所探参数空间内稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多忽略颗粒系统中外部驱动（如间隙气体效应）对输运性质的影响，已有假设可能存在偏差。本文旨在修正这一不足，系统分析由非弹性碰撞和外驱动共同作用下的准二维颗粒流体的动力学与输运行为。

Method: 采用Enskog动力学方程框架下的$\Delta$-模型描述系统，引入修正碰撞规则实现能量注入，并通过粘性阻力项和类朗之万（Langevin-like）随机项刻画间隙气体影响。运用Chapman-Enskog方法结合Sonine多项式展开的首项近似，解析推导Navier-Stokes输运系数和冷却速率；数值验证采用直接模拟蒙特卡洛（DSMC）方法。

Result: 解析推导了粘度和热导率等Navier-Stokes输运系数。稳态温度和峰度（kurtosis）的理论预测与DSMC模拟结果高度一致。外驱动显著改变了输运系数，与无气相（dry）颗粒系统存在明显差异。线性稳定性分析表明，均匀稳态在所探索的参数范围内是稳定的。

Conclusion: 外驱动对受限准二维颗粒流体的输运性质有重要影响，否定了先前忽略这些效应的假设。该模型在中等密度下能准确描述系统行为，为描述含间隙气体的颗粒系统提供了可靠的理论框架。

Abstract: This paper investigates the dynamic properties of a confined quasi-two-dimensional granular fluid at moderate densities, modeled within the framework of the Enskog kinetic equation. The system is described using the so-called $Δ$-model, which incorporates energy injection through modified collision rules, and is further extended to account for the influence of an interstitial gas via a viscous drag force and a stochastic Langevin-like term. By applying the Chapman-Enskog method, the Navier-Stokes transport coefficients and the cooling rate are derived analytically considering the leading terms in a Sonine polynomial expansion. The study focuses on steady-state conditions and examines how the combined effects of inelastic collisions and external driving influence transport properties such as the viscosity and the thermal conductivity. Theoretical predictions for the steady temperature and the kurtosis are validated against direct simulation Monte Carlo (DSMC) results, showing excellent agreement. The findings reveal that the external driving significantly alters the transport coefficients compared to dry (no gas phase) granular systems, challenging previous assumptions that neglected these effects. Additionally, a linear stability analysis demonstrates that the homogeneous steady state is stable across the explored parameter space.

</details>


### [39] [Adhesion-controlled sliding and the Stribeck curve in hydrophobic soft contacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03607)
*Ruibin Xu,Charlotte Spies,Michele Scaraggi,B. N. J. Persson*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验与理论相结合的方法，研究了干摩擦和甘油润滑条件下聚甲基丙烯酸甲酯（PMMA）圆柱与聚二甲基硅氧烷（PDMS）橡胶之间的疏水软接触滑动行为，发现对于光滑且具有粘附性的表面，粘附力不仅改变真实接触面积，还会改变滑动模式本身，使得Stribeck曲线无法仅用经典流体力学和载荷分担理论解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在疏水软接触（hydrophobic soft contact）系统中，润滑剂存在时粘附力（adhesion）如何影响真实接触面积（real contact area）和滑动响应（sliding response），并检验经典混合润滑理论在软接触条件下的适用性。

Method: 采用实验测量干摩擦和甘油润滑条件下不同表面粗糙度PMMA圆柱在PDMS橡胶上的滑动行为，结合包含粘附效应的接触面积计算建立基线，并使用均场混合润滑理论（mean-field mixed-lubrication theory）对Stribeck曲线进行拟合分析。

Result: 对于喷砂粗糙表面，Stribeck曲线可由均场混合润滑理论较好描述，需引入与速度无关的有效界面剪切应力（effective interfacial shear stress）。光滑表面则表现出定性不同的行为，归因于低速下粘附控制的滑动模式及宏观Schallamach波（Schallamach-wave）类不稳定性，该模式随速度增加逐渐被抑制。

Conclusion: 在软疏水接触中，粘附力不仅改变真实接触面积，还会改变滑动模式本身。对于足够光滑和具有粘附性的表面，Stribeck曲线无法仅从经典流体力学和载荷分担（load sharing）角度完全理解。

Abstract: We present an experimental and theoretical study of dry and glycerol-lubricated sliding for polymethyl methacrylate (PMMA) cylinders with different surface roughness sliding on polydimethylsiloxane (PDMS) rubber. This system represents a hydrophobic soft contact, where adhesion may persist even in the presence of the lubricant and thereby modify both the real contact area and the sliding response. Dry-friction measurements, combined with contact-area calculations that include adhesion, provide a baseline for the lubricated study. For the two sandblasted surfaces, the measured Stribeck curves are described reasonably well by a mean-field mixed-lubrication theory with a fitted velocity-independent effective interfacial shear stress. In contrast, the smooth surface exhibits qualitatively different behavior. We attribute this to an adhesion-controlled sliding mode involving macroscopic Schallamach-wave-like instabilities at low sliding speeds, which are progressively suppressed as the sliding speed increases and forced wetting reduces direct solid-solid contact. The results show that, for soft hydrophobic contacts, the Stribeck curve cannot always be understood from classical fluid flow and load sharing alone. For sufficiently smooth and adhesive surfaces, adhesion changes not only the real contact area but also the sliding mode itself.

</details>


### [40] [Linear and Non-Linear Rheology of Single and Double Cross-Linked Biopolymer Networks under Viscous Shear Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03728)
*Nasrollah Hajaliakbari,David Head,Oliver Harlen*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究基于细长体理论（Slender Body theory）构建并改进数值工具，模拟单交联与双交联生物聚合物网络（水凝胶）在振荡剪切流（oscillatory shear flow）下的力学行为。研究发现：双网络在非线性区（100%应变幅值）不会出现文献中报道的双峰（两步屈服）；单网络在非线性区反而可观察到双峰；线性区无法通过单网络结果叠加预测双网络应力-应变曲线，但非线性区可以；非线性效应与初始结构形态（种子数）相关。这些结果有助于设计用于伤口愈合或组织工程的增强纤维材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了更深入地理解单交联与双交联生物聚合物网络（水凝胶）在振荡剪切流作用下的微观力学行为，特别是揭示双网络材料是否普遍存在两步屈服（double peaks/two-step yielding）现象，以及线性与非线性区应力响应与网络结构之间的关系。

Method: 基于一种细长体理论（Slender Body theory）的数值工具，进行修改后用于模拟单交联与双交联生物聚合物网络在振荡剪切流下的力学行为；考虑了交织纤维之间的流体动力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions）；通过计算应力和傅里叶系数（Fourier coefficients），即剪切模量（shear moduli），评估了线性区与非线性区的响应。

Result: 在100%最大应变幅值（非线性区）下，双网络并未出现文献中曾报道的双峰（两步屈服）；反而单网络在该非线性区观察到了双峰。线性区（5%应变幅值）中，双网络的应力-应变曲线无法通过叠加对应单网络的结果进行预测，但在非线性区（100%应变幅值）下可以实现该预测。双网络在非线性区的傅里叶系数及其幅值（非线性效应指标）从零模到五模均相当可观，而线性区仅零模和一模足够。单网络的非线性效应与初始结构形态——即种子数（seed number）——相关，而非流动条件。

Conclusion: 研究表明，双交联网络的力学响应并非单交联网络的简单叠加，其非线性行为与初始网络形态（种子数）密切相关。这些发现有助于科学家更好地设计用于伤口愈合或组织工程等领域的增强纤维材料（enhanced fibrous materials）。

Abstract: In this research study, a numerical tool, which is based on a version of Slender Body theory, has been used and also modified to simulate the mechanical behaviour of single- and double-cross-linked biopolymer networks (hydrogel) under oscillatory shear flow. The hydrodynamic interactions among fibres of intertwined networks were considered. Then, the stress and Fourier coefficients (i.e. shear moduli) were evaluated for both linear and nonlinear regimes. It was found that the double peaks (two-step yielding) of two double network at 100% maximum strain amplitude (nonlinear regime) cannot happen due to changes in fibre alignments and seed numbers, although the crosslinkers between two subnetworks present, which was previously reported in the literature. In fact, we also observed two peaks for single network in nonlinear regime. Furthermore, it was shown that the stress-strain curve of double network is not predicted by just superimposing the results from the corresponding single networks at 5% maximum strain amplitude (linear regime), but this prediction can be provided at 100% maximum strain amplitude (nonlinear regime). The Fourier coefficients and corresponding amplitude (an indication of nonlinearity effects) for double network were quite considerable from zero to fifth modes in nonlinear regime, despite enough zero and first modes in linear regime. It was also shown that the nonlinearity effects can be related to the morphology of the initial structure, i.e. the seed number rather than the flow condition for the single network. These results can help scientists to better design enhance fibrous materials used in wound healing or tissue engineering.

</details>

### [41] [Formal moduli and the splitting theory of supermanifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03166)
*Mauricio Corrêa,Simone Noja*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文为复超流形的分裂问题发展了一套形式模理论（formal moduli theory），通过构造有限步过滤微分分次李代数（filtered dg Lie algebra）和最小过滤 $L_\infty$ 模型，统一了Green阻碍、Atiyah类与Kuranishi关系，并给出了显式非分裂超几何实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复超流形（complex supermanifold）的分裂问题（splitting problem）——即判定超流形是否同构于其分裂模型——是超几何理论的核心问题之一。已有Green阻碍塔（obstruction tower）提供了逐级阻碍类，但缺乏一个统一的代数框架来描述整个阻碍序列及其与Atiyah类的内在联系，同时家庭参数化情形下的形式模理论尚不完善。

Method: 以Green阻碍塔为起点，构造一个有限步过滤的微分分次李代数（filtered dg Lie algebra），通过过滤Maurer-Cartan理论（filtered Maurer-Cartan theory）控制分裂问题；将经典逐级阻碍类恢复为适配Maurer-Cartan代表元的首项；将理论转移至最小过滤$L_\infty$模型，其高括号给出阻碍坐标间的内禀Kuranishi关系；在精确过滤意义上证明仿射Atiah类（affine Atiyah class）包含整个Green阻碍塔；构造固定收缩形式模问题（fixed-retract formal moduli problem），在标准有限性、基变换和下降假设下得到相对切-阻碍与Kuranishi表示。

Result: 建立了将复超流形分裂问题完全纳入过滤$L_\infty$形式模理论的统一框架；证明了Donagi-Witten分量对应主阻碍，高阻碍依次作为同一Atiyah上循环的投射缺陷和剩余类出现；识别出分裂截形的形式邻域等价于分裂模型的纤维形变理论；给出了具有残留高阻碍和第一个非线性Kuranishi关系的具体非分裂超几何实例。

Conclusion: 本文构建的代数框架统一了复超流形分裂问题的若干经典不变量（Green阻碍、Atiyah类、Kuranishi关系），并通过构造性实例验证了理论的有效性，为超流形分类和模空间研究提供了新的工具。

Abstract: We develop a formal moduli theory for the splitting problem of complex supermanifolds. Starting from Green's obstruction tower, we construct a finite-step filtered dg Lie algebra which controls splittings by filtered Maurer-Cartan theory. We prove that the classical successive obstruction classes are recovered as the leading terms of adapted Maurer-Cartan representatives, and we transfer the theory to a minimal filtered $L_\infty$-model whose higher brackets give the intrinsic Kuranishi relations among the obstruction coordinates. We also prove that, in a precise filtered sense, the affine Atiyah class contains the entire Green obstruction tower: the Donagi-Witten component gives the primary obstruction, while the higher obstructions arise as successive projected defects and residual classes of the same Atiyah cocycle. We then pass to families, by constructing the fixed-retract formal moduli problem with prescribed split model and by identifying the formal neighbourhood of the split section with the fibrewise deformation theory of the split model; under standard finiteness, base-change, and descent hypotheses this yields relative tangent-obstruction and Kuranishi presentations. Finally, we work out explicit examples of non-split supergeometries, including cases with residual higher obstructions and a first nonlinear Kuranishi relation. These examples illustrate the interaction between Green obstructions, Atiyah classes, and higher $L_\infty$-operations.

</details>
