### [42] [Potential Hessian Ascent III: Sampling the Sherrington--Kirkpatrick Model at Beta < 1/2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03718)
*Ewan Davies,Holden Lee,Juspreet Singh Sandhu,Jonathan Shi*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文提出一个多项式时间算法，能够在逆温度 β<1/2 范围内，以可忽略的全变差距离（total-variation distance, TVD）误差对 Sherrington–Kirkpatrick 模型的 Gibbs 测度进行采样。该工作将此前仅能保证 Wasserstein 距离误差的完整复制对称（replica-symmetric）区间 β<1 的结果，改进为 TVD 意义上的高精度保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sherrington–Kirkpatrick（SK）模型是自旋玻璃理论中的核心模型，其 Gibbs 测度的高效采样是统计物理与计算机科学交叉领域的重要问题。此前算法要么仅能在较低温度（β≈0.295 以下）保证 TVD 误差，要么在整个复制对称相（β<1）仅能保证较弱的 Wasserstein 距离误差，缺乏在更大温度范围内实现强误差（TVD）可控的高效采样算法。

Method: 算法核心是将先前用于优化的势能黑塞上升（potential Hessian ascent）方法改造为采样算法，具体通过实现高温下的算法随机定位（algorithmic stochastic localization）。方法包括：利用高斯分部积分、重叠浓度（overlap concentration）和精确空穴估计（cavity estimates）来估计倾斜 Gibbs 分布的协方差；借助自由概率论（free probability）控制黑塞矩阵的对角子代数，将 Wasserstein 误差改进为 KL 散度下的 O(1) 保证；最后结合 Jarzynski 等式与拒绝采样（rejection sampling），以及时间 T 定位分布上的限制对数 Sobolev 不等式（restricted log-Sobolev inequality），将误差精细化为 TVD 意义上的 o(1)。

Result: 在逆温度 β<1/2 的条件下，算法实现了多项式时间内以可忽略的全变差距离误差对 SK 模型的 Gibbs 测度进行采样。具体地，有限时间定位过程给出 Wasserstein 距离的 O(1) 误差保证（优于此前的 o(n)），并通过进一步的自由概率论证将其改进为 KL 散度下的 O(1) 保证，最终通过 Jarzynski 等式和限制对数 Sobolev 不等式将 TVD 误差降低至 o(1)。

Conclusion: 本研究首次将 SK 模型 Gibbs 测度的高精度（TVD）采样算法从较低温度扩展至 β<1/2 的更大范围，填补了复制对称区间内强误差保证的空白。该工作同时展示了优化算法（势能黑塞上升）在采样问题中的新用途，并为统计物理模型的算法随机定位方法提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: We give a polynomial-time algorithm to sample from the Gibbs measure of the Sherrington--Kirkpatrick model with negligible total-variation distance (TVD) error up to inverse temperature $β< 1/2$. Prior work obtained TVD error guarantees only up to $β\approx 0.295$, while results covering the entire replica-symmetric regime $β< 1$ gave guarantees only in Wasserstein distance. Our approach demonstrates that the same potential Hessian ascent previously developed for optimization also functions as a sampling algorithm by implementing algorithmic stochastic localization at high temperature. By estimating the covariance of the tilted Gibbs distribution via Gaussian integration by parts, overlap concentration, and precise cavity estimates, we show that a Hessian-ascent process achieves an $O(1)$ Wasserstein error guarantee for finite-time localization, improving on the previous $o(n)$. A careful comparison of stochastic localization with the Hessian ascent process and a free probability argument controlling the diagonal sub-algebra of the Hessian improves this to $O(1)$ in KL divergence. We then use Jarzynski's equality with rejection sampling, along with a restricted log-Sobolev inequality on the time-$T$ localized distribution, to refine the error to $o(1)$ in TVD up to a constant time $T$ and to complete the sampling with Glauber dynamics.

</details>


### [43] [Dimer models on astroidal zig-zag graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03896)
*Tomas Berggren,Alexei Borodin,Terrence George*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文针对任意最小周期平面二分图，构造了一族有限子图（AZ图），并显式给出了其Kasteleyn逆矩阵的双围道积分表达式；对于周期加权情形，建立了大AZ图中的相分离现象，给出了arctic曲线的显式参数化，并证明了高度函数的极限形状与局部二聚体关联收敛到对应的平移不变的吉布斯测度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在平面二分图的二聚体模型（dimer model）中，Kasteleyn矩阵的逆矩阵是计算关联函数的核心工具，但迄今为止仅对少数特例如Newton多边形为三角形或四边形的图有显式结果。本文旨在突破这一限制，对任意牛顿多边形（Newton polygon）的周期平面二分图构造一类有限子图，使得其逆Kasteleyn矩阵能够显式表达。

Method: 构造了名为“星形锯齿图”（astroidal zig-zag graphs，简称AZ图）的有限子图族，其边界由锯齿路径（zig-zag paths）构成，整体形状类似星形线（astroid）。对于任意Fock加权（Fock weighting），通过对应的谱曲线（spectral curve）上的双围道积分（double contour integral）给出逆Kasteleyn矩阵。

Result: 对于任意边数为n的牛顿多边形，AZ图构成一个(n-3)维的子图族；当牛顿多边形为单位正方形时，AZ图退化为经典的Aztec菱形（Aztec diamond）。在周期加权下，大AZ图中出现三相分离：渐近冻结区（frozen）、粗糙液体区（rough/liquid）和平滑气体区（smooth/gaseous），并得到了arctic曲线（arctic curve）的显式参数化。还得到了高度函数（height function）的确定性极限——极限形状（limit shape），并证明了局部二聚体关联（local dimer correlations）收敛到极限形状所预测的平移不变的吉布斯测度（translation-invariant Gibbs measure）。

Conclusion: 本文首次对任意牛顿多边形（不限于三角形或四边形）的周期平面二分图给出了显式可解的二聚体模型子图族，并建立了完整的相分离分析和极限形状理论，将经典的Aztec菱形结果推广到了更一般的几何情形。

Abstract: On a finite weighted graph, the dimer model is a probability measure on its dimer covers, that assigns to any cover a probability proportional to the product of the weights of its edges. For planar bipartite graphs, dimer correlations are encoded by the inverse of the so-called Kasteleyn matrix; for a large graph, typically taken as a finite domain in a periodic graph, this inverse matrix is known explicitly only for a handful of examples. In all previously known examples, the Newton polygon -- a convex lattice polygon that classifies periodic graphs up to local moves -- is either a triangle or a quadrilateral.
  Our main results are the following.
  For any (minimal) periodic planar bipartite graph, we construct an $(n-3)$-dimensional family of finite subgraphs for which we obtain an explicit inverse Kasteleyn matrix; here $n$ is the number of sides of the Newton polygon. Their boundaries are formed by zig-zag paths and their overall shape is reminiscent of an astroid; we call them astroidal zig-zag graphs (AZ graphs). If the Newton polygon is the unit square then the corresponding AZ graph is the celebrated Aztec diamond with its size as the parameter.
  Our inverse Kasteleyn matrices are given by a double contour integral on the corresponding spectral curve for any Fock weighting of the graph. This includes, in particular, all periodic weightings.
  For periodic weightings, we asymptotically analyze the resulting inverse Kasteleyn matrices. We establish a phase separation in large AZ graphs into asymptotically frozen, rough (liquid), and smooth (gaseous) regions, and obtain an explicit parametrization of the `arctic curve'.
  We also compute the deterministic limit of the height function, known as the limit shape, and prove the convergence of the local dimer correlations to the translation-invariant Gibbs measure of the slope predicted by the limit shape.

</details>

### [44] [Selecting optimal unrestricted Hartree-Fock trial wavefunctions for phaseless auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo: Accuracy and limitations in modeling three iron-sulfur clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03981)
*Don Danilov,Brad Ganoe,Leon Otis,Zhi Gong,Zixiang Lu,James Shee*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本论文研究了无符号辅助场量子蒙特卡洛（ph-AFQMC）方法对铁硫簇（[2Fe-2S]²⁺、[4Fe-4S]²⁺、[4Fe-4S]⁴⁺）活性空间模型的适用性，发现化学性质和物理对称性比变分能量更适合指导试探波函数选择，并揭示了由于随机波函数与UHF试探之间重叠迅速消失导致的采样偏差问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无符号辅助场量子蒙特卡洛（ph-AFQMC）是一种有前景的电子结构方法，但其预测质量高度依赖于试探波函数（trial wavefunction）的选择，尤其在强关联大体系中如何做出最优选择并不明确。平均场试探波函数虽然计算成本低（$O(N^4)$）且与化学概念直接对应，但在强关联区域面临对称性困境（symmetry dilemma）和多个近简并解的问题。

Method: 研究者选取[2Fe-2S]²⁺、混合价[4Fe-4S]²⁺和[4Fe-4S]⁴⁺的活性空间模型（active space models），系统探究ph-AFQMC对非限制性哈特里-福克（unrestricted Hartree-Fock, UHF）试探波函数选择的敏感性。

Result: 化学性质和物理对称性比变分能量（variational energy）更适合指导平均场试探波函数或耦合簇（coupled cluster）参考态的选择，基于此可获得惊人的精确基态能量。然而，在所有情况下，随机波函数与UHF试探之间的重叠迅速消失，表明这些试探是次优的重要性函数（suboptimal importance functions）。这种采样偏差将ph-AFQMC推向人为的负能量，但在某些情况下可被无符号偏差（phaseless bias）补偿。

Conclusion: 应依据化学性质和物理对称性而非变分能量选择ph-AFQMC的平均场试探波函数。通过与拉伸氦二聚体阳离子的类比，揭示采样偏差导致ph-AFQMC产生人为负能量的机制，说明这种偏差在某些情况下可被无符号偏差抵消。

Abstract: Phaseless auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo (ph-AFQMC) has emerged as a promising electronic structure method for correlated electronic systems. However, the quality of its predictions depends critically on the choice of trial wavefunction, and it is not obvious how to make an optimal choice especially for strongly correlated states of large systems. Mean-field wavefunctions are compelling trial wavefunction candidates as they map directly to chemical concepts and can be obtained with $O(N^4)$ cost. Yet in the strongly correlated regime one faces a symmetry dilemma and the existence of multiple nearly-degenerate solutions. In this work we investigate active space models of [2Fe-2S]$^{2+}$, mixed-valent [4Fe-4S]$^{2+}$, and [4Fe-4S]$^{4+}$ and explore the sensitivity of ph-AFQMC to the choice of unrestricted Hartree-Fock trial wavefunction. We find that chemical properties and physical symmetries, rather than the variational energy, ought to guide the choice of mean-field trial for ph-AFQMC (or reference state for coupled cluster models), and show that surprisingly accurate ground-state energies for these systems can be obtained. However, in all cases we find a rapidly vanishing overlap between the stochastic wavefunction and the UHF trial, indicating that the trials are suboptimal importance functions. By analogy to a similar situation in the stretched helium dimer cation, we show how this sampling bias pushes ph-AFQMC towards artificially negative energies, which evidently can be compensated for by the phaseless bias in certain cases.

</details>

### [45] [Comparing Hemispheres: Anisotropy in the deceleration parameter $q_0$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03004)
*Mauricio Lopez-Hernandez,Josue De-Santiago*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用Pantheon+ Ia型超新星样本对减速参数q₀进行半球比较分析，检验宇宙加速的各向同性及红移修正的稳健性。研究发现即使在经CMB偶极子和本动速度修正后的z_HD参考系中，q₀仍存在残余偶极各向异性，该各向异性与CMB偶极方向一致；通过超新星数据推断的偶极子与Planck CMB偶极子存在~1.9σ的轻度不一致；当将此推断偶极子纳入红移修正流程后，各向异性被抑制，残余涨落与统计噪声一致，表明部分信号源于局域速度场建模的残余不匹配，提示存在未被密度场模型完全捕捉的残余体流（bulk flow）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验宇宙加速是否各向同性，以及现有的红移修正（包括CMB偶极子和本动速度修正）是否充分消除了运动学效应造成的系统偏差。当前低红移超新星宇宙学中，红移修正依赖于基于密度场的本动速度重建，但其完备性尚未得到充分验证。

Method: 采用半球比较（hemispherical comparison）方法，利用Pantheon+ Ia型超新星样本，在三种红移参考系（z_hel、z_CMB、z_HD）中分别计算减速参数q₀的半球间差异，并结合超新星数据直接推断偶极子方向与幅值，将其纳入红移修正流程进行交叉验证。

Result: 在z_HD参考系中探测到残余偶极各向异性，Δq₀=0.112，最大信噪比S/N=2.155，方向与CMB偶极对齐；随最小红移截断增大而减弱。z_hel和z_CMB参考系中各向异性更强。超新星推断的偶极子速度v_⊙=307.26 km/s，方向(RA,DEC)=(156.40°, -3.38°)，与Planck CMB偶极子存在~1.9σ偏差。将超新星推断偶极子纳入修正后，各向异性消失，S/N降至≤1.75。

Conclusion: 现有基于密度场的本动速度重建未能完全捕捉局域体流，导致低红移超新星宇宙学中存在未被充分校正的系统不确定性（systematic uncertainty）。部分观测到的各向异性信号来源于红移修正流程中局域速度场建模的残余不匹配。

Abstract: We present a hemispherical comparison analysis of the deceleration parameter $q_0$ using the Pantheon+ sample of Type Ia supernovae to test the isotropy of cosmic acceleration and the robustness of redshift corrections. We detect directional variations in $q_0$ across redshift frames. Even in the $z_{\mathrm{HD}}$ frame, where corrections for the CMB dipole and peculiar velocities are applied, a residual dipolar anisotropy persists with $Δq_0 = 0.112$ and a maximum signal to noise $S/N = 2.155$, aligned with the CMB dipole direction and decreasing with increasing minimum redshift cut. The anisotropy is stronger in the $z_{\mathrm{hel}}$ and $z_{\mathrm{CMB}}$ frames, where kinematic corrections are incomplete, while the transition to $z_{\mathrm{HD}}$ reduces but does not remove the signal. Inferring the dipole from the supernovae data yields $v_{\odot} = 307.26^{+32.00}_{-22.28},\mathrm{km \, s^{-1}}$ toward $(\mathrm{RA},\mathrm{DEC}) = (156.40^{+4.72}_{-4.71}, -3.38^{+5.54}_{-8.23})^\circ$, mildly discrepant with the Planck CMB dipole at the $\sim 1.9σ$ level. When this SNe inferred dipole is incorporated into the redshift correction pipeline, the hemispherical anisotropy is suppressed, with the dipolar pattern disappearing and the maximum signal reduced to $S/N \lesssim 1.75$, while the remaining fluctuations become consistent with statistical noise, suggesting that part of the signal arises from residual mismatches in the modeling of the local velocity field. Since current redshift corrections rely on peculiar velocity reconstructions based on the density field, our results suggest a residual bulk flow not fully captured by these models, highlighting a source of systematic uncertainty in low redshift supernova cosmology.

</details>


### [46] [Primordial Black Hole contribution to the stochastic background of Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03156)
*D. Martín-González*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出原初黑洞（Primordial Black Holes, PBHs）通过动力学摩擦下沉至暗物质晕中心，经层次合并与气体吸积形成超大质量黑洞（Supermassive Black Holes, SMBHs），其产生的随机引力波背景（Stochastic Gravitational Wave Background, SGWB）幅度与脉冲星计时阵列（Pulsar Timing Arrays, PTAs）的观测一致；该模型同时解释了詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜（James Webb Space Telescope, JWST）发现的高红移早期超大质量黑洞，仅需约0.1%的暗物质以PBH形式存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星计时阵列探测到的随机引力波背景幅度以及詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜发现的高红移早期过大质量中心黑洞，对现有超大质量黑洞形成模型提出了挑战。本研究旨在探讨含有大量原初黑洞的暗物质晕是否能解释上述两方面的观测矛盾。

Method: 研究提出原初黑洞通过动力学摩擦（dynamical friction）下沉至晕中心，并通过层次合并与气体吸积通道共同驱动中心黑洞增长；基于该模型计算了引力波幅度，并利用NANOGrav 15年数据集进行了贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）分析。

Result: 模型预测的引力波背景幅度与观测一致。仅需暗物质晕总质量的0.09%-0.12%下沉至中心即可解释结果，对应原初黑洞占暗物质的比例f_pbh ~ 0.1，且星际质量范围内的下沉PBHs约占总PBH群体的1%。

Conclusion: 解释詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜发现的新超大质量黑洞群体的原初黑洞模型，同样可以解释随机引力波背景的观测幅度，表明该模型能统一解释高红移超大质量黑洞形成与引力波背景这两类独立观测。

Abstract: The amplitude of the detected stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB) measured by pulsar timing arrays (PTAs) and the discovery of early and over-massive central black holes at high redshift by the James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) challenge current models of supermassive black hole (SMBH) formation. We study if halos containing a significant population of primordial black holes (PBHs) would increase the amplitude of the PTA signal. PBHs add an iso-curvature component to the matter power spectrum, accelerating the formation and merger of dark matter halos at all redshifts. We propose that black holes in the halo sink to the center via dynamical friction. The central black hole grows through hierarchical merging in addition to the gas accretion channel. We computed the resulting GW amplitude and performed a Bayesian inference analysis using the NANOGrav 15-year dataset. We show that the predicted amplitude of the gravitational wave background agrees with the observations. Our model only requires $0.09\%-0.12\%$ of the total mass of the halo to fall to the center, compatible with a fraction $f_{\rm pbh}\sim 0.1$ of PBHs as dark matter, if the in-falling PBHs in the stellar mass range are about a $1\%$ of the total population, as found in our previous estimation of the formation of SMBHs at $z\sim 6-10$. The PBH model that explains the JWST new found populations of SMBHs also explain the amplitude of the stochastic background of gravitational waves.

### [47] [The consecutive lifting-projection flow as an approximation of Boltzmann and Landau flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03273)
*Kun Huang*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出连续提升-投影（LP）流，作为空间均匀玻尔兹曼（Boltzmann）和朗道（Landau）方程的一种新型近似框架。核心思想是将非线性碰撞算子提升到高维线性Kac主方程，在球面上演化后再投影回低维速度空间。LP流保质量、动量、能量，满足熵耗散性质，收敛至正确麦克斯韦平衡态，并为构建可靠数值求解器提供了统一方法论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间均匀玻尔兹曼和朗道方程中的非线性碰撞算子给数值求解和理论分析带来了根本性困难。现有方法在守恒性、正性与数值稳定性之间存在权衡，亟需一种既能消除非线性又保持物理约束的近似框架。

Method: 提出了连续提升-投影（lifting-projection, LP）流：将非线性碰撞算子提升到高维线性Kac主方程（master equation），在球面上进行时间演化，再将解投影回原始低维速度空间。该流具有切向流（tangent flow）性质和清晰半群（semigroup）结构。针对麦克斯韦分子（Maxwell molecules）情形给出了有限时间区间上的误差估计。

Result: LP流保留了质量、动量和能量，满足熵耗散性质，并渐近收敛至正确的麦克斯韦平衡态（Maxwellian equilibrium）。提升操作移除了碰撞算子的内在非线性，使得解具有显式解析表示。此外，该框架统一了已有的显式离散化方案，并在此基础上提出了格林函数法（Green's function method），该方法既无条件稳定又与快速谱离散化（fast spectral discretizations）完美兼容。

Conclusion: 该框架为动理学理论（kinetic theory）中构建可靠数值求解器提供了一种简洁且通用的方法论。它有助于理解数值稳定性，厘清守恒性与正性之间的权衡，并为开发新数值格式（如无条件稳定的格林函数法）开辟了路径。

Abstract: We introduce the consecutive lifting-projection (LP) flow as a novel approximation framework for the spatially homogeneous Boltzmann and Landau equations. The key idea is to lift the nonlinear collision operator to a higher dimensional linear Kac master equation on spheres, evolve this lifted equation in time, and project the solution back to the lower dimensional velocity space. The resulting LP flow is a tangent flow to the original kinetic dynamics and admits a clear semigroup structure. We show that the consecutive LP flow preserves mass, momentum, and energy, satisfies an entropy dissipation property, and converges to the correct Maxwellian equilibrium. In addition, the lifting removes the intrinsic nonlinearity of the collision operator and enables explicit analytical representations of the solution. For Maxwell molecules, we provide an error estimate quantifying the accuracy over finite time intervals. The framework provides a concise and general methodology for constructing reliable numerical solvers in kinetic theory. It unifies existing explicit discretizations, which helps understanding numerical stability and clarifying the trade-off between conservation and positivity. More importantly, it enables the development of new schemes. In particular, we propose the Green's function method, which is not only unconditionally stable, but also perfectly compatible with fast spectral discretizations.

</details>

### [48] [Two Regularized Determinants of Laplacian through Resurgence theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03960)
*Wen Shen,Shanzhong Sun*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文从复现理论（resurgence theory）视角出发，研究了黎曼流形上拉普拉斯算子行列式的两种正则化方法——形式对数导数正则化与指数变形正则化。通过Borel-Laplace重求和（Borel-Laplace resummation）建立了两种正则化行列式的闭式公式，并揭示了它们之间的内在关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在从复现理论的角度系统研究黎曼流形上拉普拉斯算子（Laplacian）行列式的正则化问题，为理解两种正则化方式（形式对数导数与指数变形）的数学结构提供统一框架。

Method: 利用Borel-Laplace重求和技术，结合Theta级数$\hatΘ_{D_X}$沿解析延拓路径上奇点贡献的分析，分别建立两种正则化行列式的闭式公式。该Theta级数类似于热核的迹（trace of the heat kernel），但基于拉普拉斯算子平方根的谱定义。

Result: 在$S^1$和高亏格（genus $\geq2$）紧黎曼曲面（compact Riemann surface）上，分别利用泊松求和公式（Poisson summation formula）和Selberg迹公式（Selberg trace formula）重新审视了形式对数导数正则化。此外，得到了指数变形正则化在无穷远处的1-Gevrey渐近行为（1-Gevrey asymptotic behavior），其系数由热核的迹决定。

Conclusion: 两种正则化行列式之间存在明确关系：在指数变形正则化中，当变形参数趋于$0$时，两者具有相同的导数。

Abstract: We study two types of regularizations of the determinant of Laplacian on Riemann manifold from the viewpoint of resurgence theory. One is the formal logarithmic derivative of the determinant, and the other is its exponential deformation. Under appropriate conditions, the close formulas for both regularized determinant are established through Borel-Laplace resummation which takes into account the contribution of the singularities along the analytic continuation of Theta series $\hatΘ_{D_X}$. The series resembles the trace of the heat kernel, but is defined via the spectrum of the square-root of the Laplacian. As applications, we revisit the well known formal logarithmic derivative of determinant on $S^1$ and compact Riemann surface with higher genus ($\geq2$) corresponding to the Poisson summation formula and Selberg trace formula respectively. Furthermore, the 1-Gevrey asymptotic behavior of the exponential deformation regularization at infinity is considered whose coefficients are determined by the trace of the heat kernel. In the end, we establish the relationship between the two regularized determinants. In fact, they have the same derivatives when the deformation parameter tends to $0$ in exponentially deformed regularization.

### [49] [Pade Approximants for Geodesy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04027)
*Ovidiu Costin,Gerald V. Dunne,Crichton Ogle*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了帕德近似（Padé approximants）在球谐展开（spherical harmonic expansions, SHEs）收敛半径之外进行向下延拓（downward continuation）以及识别引力势复数奇点（complex singularities）中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 球谐展开本质上是以无穷远点为展开点的1/r展开，其收敛域通常限于布洛伊万球（Brillouin sphere）外部；然而，对于具有解析地形和密度的人造模型，收敛域可能更大，且随行星结构复杂性增加而偏差减小。本文旨在探索帕德近似能否突破这一收敛半径限制。

Method: 采用帕德近似对球谐展开进行解析延拓（analytic continuation），以逼近收敛半径之外的引力势行为，并利用该方法定位引力势的复数奇点。

Result: 帕德近似能够有效外推至球谐展开原始收敛域之外；对于具有解析性地形与密度分布的合成模型，收敛域的扩展程度随行星结构复杂度增加而下降。

Conclusion: 帕德近似是一种可行的工具，可用于球谐展开的向下延拓及引力势复数奇点的识别，但其有效性受模型结构复杂性制约。

Abstract: In this note we analyze the use of Padé approximants for downward continuation beyond the radius of convergence of spherical harmonic expansions (SHEs), and for identifying the complex singularities of the gravitational potential. SHEs are, in essence, expansions in 1/r, i.e., expansions about the point at infinity. Their domain of convergence is generically the exterior of the Brillouin sphere. However, for synthetic models with analytic topography and density the region of convergence may be larger, with the deviation decreasing as the structural complexity of the planet increases.

### [50] [Quantum Geometric Quadrupole of Cooper Pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03133)
*Wenqin Chen,Kaijie Yang,Ting Cao,Shi-Zeng Lin,Jiabin Yu,Di Xiao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文发展了基于库珀对四极矩（Cooper pair quadrupole moment）的统一框架，用以描述超导配对大小的几何起源；在时间反演对称性破缺时，贝里曲率（Berry curvature）通过配对波函数的相位结构对配对尺寸产生关键贡献，并与量子度量（quantum metric）共同给出几何下界；在菱方石墨烯（rhombohedral graphene）中的应用表明，贝里曲率贡献可占主导，所得配对尺寸与实验推断的相干长度（coherence length）可比拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导中库珀对（Cooper pair）的尺寸定义了基本长度尺度，传统理论由能带色散和超导能隙决定；但在平带（flat bands）体系中，色散被抑制使得量子几何（quantum geometry）变得至关重要，现有理论仍缺乏统一描述，尤其忽略了贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的贡献。

Method: 基于库珀对四极矩（Cooper pair quadrupole moment）构建一般性计算框架，其迹（trace）给出配对尺寸；该框架同时适用于色散能带和平带情况，并纳入时间反演对称性破缺时贝里曲率通过配对波函数相位结构产生的贡献。

Result: 贝里曲率与量子度量共同对配对尺寸施加几何下界；在菱方石墨烯中，贝里曲率诱导的贡献可占主导，所得配对尺寸与实验推断的相干长度可比拟。

Conclusion: 贝里曲率（Berry curvature）是控制超导微观长度尺度的核心几何要素，该框架为理解超导配对尺寸的几何起源提供了统一描述。

Abstract: The size of Cooper pairs defines a fundamental length scale of superconductivity, conventionally set by band dispersion and the superconducting gap. This picture breaks down in flat bands, where quenched dispersion makes quantum geometry essential. Here we develop a general framework based on the Cooper pair quadrupole moment, whose trace gives the pair size. The framework holds for both dispersive and flat-band cases, and provides a unified description of the geometric origin of this length scale. In particular, when time-reversal symmetry is broken, Berry curvature enters through the phase structure of the pair wavefunction and gives an essential contribution absent from previous quantum-metric theories. Together, Berry curvature and quantum metric impose a geometric lower bound on the pair size. Applying this framework to rhombohedral graphene, we find that the Berry-curvature-induced contribution can dominate and yields pair sizes comparable to experimentally inferred coherence lengths. These results identify Berry curvature as a central geometric ingredient controlling the microscopic length scale of superconductivity.

</details>


### [51] [Nb$_3$Sn Thin Films Using a Cu-Sn Route for Dark Matter Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03171)
*Andre Juliao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出两种在铜基底上通过固态扩散制备Nb3Sn超导薄膜的工艺路线，成功将Tc提升至16K并涂覆六边形谐振腔。零场下品质因子Q达77,000（优于裸铜的55,000），但在多特斯拉磁场下Q急剧下降，表明该方案在轴子暗物质探测中具有初步潜力但仍需改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子暗物质（axion dark matter）探测需要铜基底上的超导射频（superconducting radio-frequency, SRF）谐振腔，在多特斯拉磁场中品质因数Q > 10^5。铜可降低热噪声并支持复杂几何结构，但传统~1100°C气相法制备Nb3Sn薄膜不适用于铜基底，因此需开发低温固态扩散工艺。

Method: 利用高锡Cu-Sn合金中的Sn通过固态扩散进入Nb层，在650-750°C（铜兼容温度）下形成Nb3Sn薄膜，替代传统~1100°C气相法。通过优化Cu-Sn合金成分维持高Sn活度，并结合Nb和蓝宝石衬底的对比实验分离铜基底应变效应。开发了两条工艺路线：(1) 在Ta涂层铜基底上热溅射Nb并扩散；(2) 先在Ta/Cu基底上蒸发Cu-Sn再沉积Nb并异位反应。采用路线(2)涂覆六边形谐振腔，测试至50 mK和9 T。

Result: 组成与热膨胀分析表明，铜基底应变将Tc抑制在18 K以下。路线(1)获得Tc=16 K；路线(2)得到均匀Nb3Sn薄膜，被选用于腔体涂覆。涂覆后的六边形腔在零场下Q=77,000（比裸铜的55,000提高40%），但磁场中Q急剧下降。

Conclusion: Nb3Sn涂层铜腔在零场下优于裸铜，为改进轴子探测器提供了可行的工艺路线，但多特斯拉磁场下Q值下降的问题仍需解决。

Abstract: Axion dark matter searches require superconducting radio-frequency (SRF) cavities on copper (Cu) substrates with quality factors Q > 10^5 in multi-tesla magnetic fields. Copper reduces thermal noise and allows complex geometries. Nb3Sn is a strong candidate due to its superior superconducting properties. However, uniform high-Tc Nb3Sn thin films on Cu are challenging due to Sn loss and substrate strain.
  This work uses solid-state diffusion of Sn from high-Sn Cu-Sn alloys into Nb layers to form Nb3Sn at Cu-compatible temperatures (650-750°C), avoiding the traditional ~1100°C vapor method. Varying Cu-Sn composition yielded an optimal alloy that maintains high Sn activity. Compositional and thermal expansion analyses showed Tc is suppressed below 18 K by Cu substrate strain. Experiments on Nb and sapphire substrates isolated the strain effects. Two routes were developed: (1) Cu-Sn on Ta-coated Cu with hot Nb sputtering (Tc = 16 K), and (2) Nb on Ta/Cu with Cu-Sn evaporation and ex-situ reaction. Route 2 gave uniform Nb3Sn and was chosen for cavity coating. A hexagonal cavity combining designs from the University of Washington and Center for Axion and Precision Physics was coated using Route 2 and tested to 50 mK and 9 T. At zero field it reached Q = 77,000 (40% above bare Cu's Q = 55,000), but Q dropped sharply in field. Nb3Sn coatings on Cu cavities outperform bare Cu at zero field and provide practical routes for improved axion detectors.

</details>


### [52] [First-Order Transitions in Weak Ising Spin-Orbit-Coupled Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03774)
*Xusheng Wang,Gaomin Tang,Shuai-hua Ji*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过自由能方法证明，在弱伊辛自旋轨道耦合（Ising spin-orbit coupling, ISOC）且大交换场条件下，超导体可发生一级相变；传统能隙方程仅能给出过冷场。同时发现准粒子谱中存在双内隙相干峰，揭示了弱ISOC区间特有的光谱特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为伊辛自旋轨道耦合（Ising spin-orbit coupling, ISOC）会强烈保护超导免受交换场退配对效应，通常导致远超泡利极限（Pauli limit）的临界场及连续二级相变。本文旨在探索弱ISOC大交换场条件下是否会出现一级相变（first-order transitions），并解决传统能隙方程在此区间失效的问题。

Method: 采用自由能方法（free-energy approach）进行分析，并与传统的基于能隙方程（gap equation）的理论方法进行对比。通过计算自由能确定热力学临界场，并分析准粒子谱（quasiparticle spectra）中的相干峰结构。

Result: 在弱ISOC且大交换场条件下，超导体中会涌现一级相变；传统能隙方程无法给出热力学临界场，只能得到过冷场（supercooling field）。准粒子谱中观测到两个显著的内隙相干峰（in-gap coherence peaks），这些是弱ISOC区间中先前报道的幻影间隙态（mirage-gap states）的表现形式。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了自由能分析在描述伊辛超导体（Ising superconductors）一级相变中的关键重要性，并揭示了弱ISOC区间独特的光谱学特征（spectroscopic signatures）。

Abstract: Ising spin-orbit coupling (ISOC) can strongly protect superconductivity against exchange-field-induced depairing, typically leading to critical fields far exceeding the Pauli limit and continuous (second-order) phase transitions. Here, using a free-energy approach, we demonstrate that first-order transitions can emerge in superconductors with weak ISOC under large exchange fields. In this regime, conventional theoretical approaches based on the gap equation fail to determine the thermodynamic critical field and instead yield only the supercooling field. Moreover, we identify two pronounced in-gap coherence peaks in the quasiparticle spectra, which represent the weak-ISOC manifestation of the previously reported mirage-gap states. Our results establish the importance of free-energy analysis in describing the first-order phase transitions in Ising superconductors and reveal distinct spectroscopic signatures of the weak-ISOC regime.

</details>


### [53] [Nonuniform superconducting states from Majorana flat bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03859)
*Sushanth Varada,Aksel Kobiałka,Ankita Bhattacharya,Patric Holmvall,Annica M. Black-Schaffer*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过自洽计算研究拓扑超导体中马约拉纳边界态平板带（flat band）导致的竞争有序相，发现边缘局域的配对密度波（pair density wave）和相位晶体（phase crystal）两种非均匀超导相，并揭示了其随化学势和温度的相图特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导能隙内的零能平板带可能引发竞争有序相，理解其在拓扑超导体（topological superconductor）中的涌现行为对揭示马约拉纳态（Majorana state）的物理性质至关重要。

Method: 基于磁性吸附原子平台（magnetic adatom platform）的拓扑超导体模型，对超导序参量（superconducting order parameter）进行自洽计算（self-consistent calculation），并利用绕数（winding number）分析平板带打开能隙的机制，化学势（chemical potential）作为主要调控参数。

Result: 零温下均匀超导解不存，相图由配对密度波主导；当振幅调制不足以杂化所有马约拉纳态时，序参量转变为相位晶体，两者之间存在宽泛的中间区域。有限温下配对密度波可存活至约80%体超导转变温度，相位晶体仅出现在更低温度，中间区域被强烈抑制。

Conclusion: 研究确立了拓扑超导体中非均匀超导相及其温度依赖行为的普适性，为理解马约拉纳平板带诱导的竞争序提供了重要理论依据。

Abstract: Zero-energy flat bands within the superconducting gap can give rise to competing ordered phases. We investigate such phases in topological superconductors based on the magnetic adatom platform hosting a flat band of Majorana edge states. Our self-consistent calculations of the superconducting order parameter show the emergence of both a pair density wave with edge-localized amplitude modulations and a phase crystal characterized by edge-localized phase modulations. These two phases lower the free energy of the system by gapping out the Majorana flat band, as dictated by winding numbers, which are primarily tuned by the chemical potential. In fact, at zero temperature the uniform superconducting solution with Majorana flat band never survives and the phase diagram features a pair density wave, while the order parameter transitions into a phase crystal when amplitude modulations are insufficient to hybridize all the Majorana states. A broad intermediate region connects these two phases with comparable modulations in both amplitude and phase. At finite temperatures, the pair density wave survives up to around 80% of the bulk superconducting transition temperature, while the phase crystal only appears at lower temperatures and the intermediate region is strongly suppressed. Our findings establish the ubiquity of emergent nonuniform superconducting phases and their temperature-dependent behavior in topological superconductors.

### [54] [Page Curve for Local-Operator Entanglement from Free Probability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02995)
*Neil Dowling,Silvia Pappalardi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用自由概率（free probability）工具解析计算了Haar随机动力学下局域算符纠缠（LOE）的所有Rényi指数，发现它渐近复制了无迹算子下随机态的Page曲线，并存在指数级微小修正。基于此结果，论证混沌系统中LOE熵的长时间值仅依赖于初始算子的自关联函数，高阶结构并不必要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域算符纠缠（local-operator entanglement, LOE）被用来衡量Heisenberg算子的经典可模拟性，并被推测为局域相互作用系统中多体混沌（many-body chaos）的见证者。然而，其具体行为及与现有混沌诊断手段（如out-of-time ordered correlators）的关系尚不清晰。

Method: 采用自由概率（free probability）理论工具，解析计算了Haar随机动力学下LOE在所有Rényi指数下的精确值；并与高阶out-of-time ordered correlators（OTOCs）通过自由累积量（free cumulants）依赖算子关联的方式进行了对比。

Result: 对于无迹（traceless）算子，LOE渐近地重现了随机态（random states）的Page曲线，并包含指数级微小修正。与高阶OTOCs不同，LOE的主导阶行为与初始算子无关。

Conclusion: 混沌系统中LOE熵的长时间值仅依赖于初始算子的自关联函数（autocorrelation functions），修正呈指数小；这意味着描述LOE并不需要完整版的本征态热化假说（Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis, ETH）的高阶结构。

Abstract: The local-operator entanglement (LOE) measures the classical simulability of a Heisenberg operator and is conjectured to witness many-body chaos in locally interacting systems. Using tools from free probability, we analytically compute its value for Haar random dynamics for all Rényi indices. We find that it asymptotically reproduces the Page curve for random states in the case of traceless operators, with exponentially deviating corrections. In contrast to higher-order out-of-time ordered correlators, which depend on operator correlations via free cumulants, the leading-order LOE is independent of the initial operator. Guided by our Haar result, we therefore argue that the long-time value of the LOE entropies in chaotic systems will depend only on autocorrelation functions of the initial operator up to exponentially small corrections, suggesting that the higher-order structure of the full Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis is not necessary to describe it.

</details>


### [55] [Completely-positive non-signalling non-Markovian dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03197)
*Serhii Kryhin,Vivishek Sudhir*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文严格定义了非马尔可夫量子动力学（non-Markovian quantum dynamics），在完全正性（complete positivity）和无信号传递（non-signalling）假设下刻画了其结构，导出了带记忆积分项的 integro-differential 主方程，并建立了无需回归定理（regression theorem）的多时关联函数计算框架。以受驱动二能级系统的发射光谱为例，展示了非马尔可夫浴引起的频率依赖线宽对 Mollow 三重态的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子动力学框架大多局限于马尔可夫近似，无法描述当前状态依赖所有历史状态的非马尔可夫过程；同时缺乏一种严格而普适的非马尔可夫量子态演化理论及相应的多时测量关联计算方法。

Method: 在完全正性和无信号传递的物理约束下，将非马尔可夫量子动力学定义为当前状态依赖于全部过去状态的演化，推导出带有记忆积分项的 integro-differential 方程，该方程是对 Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL) 方程的推广。在此基础上，建立了一套无需回归定理的多时关联函数（multi-time correlations）计算形式。

Result: 得到了一个能够描述任意可积功率谱密度（integrable power spectral density）噪声下量子系统演化的连续时间动力学方程。以受驱动二能级系统与非马尔可夫浴耦合为例，推导出其发射光谱：经典的 Mollow 三重态（Mollow triplet）出现了频率依赖的线宽，该线宽编码了浴的记忆效应。

Conclusion: 该工作为非马尔可夫量子系统提供了一个严格而透明的量子态描述框架，为突破马尔可夫近似的量子态估计（state estimation）和量子控制（state-based quantum control）开辟了道路。

Abstract: We define non-Markovian quantum dynamics as evolution in which the current state depends on all past states, and completely characterize its structure under the assumptions of complete positivity and non-signalling. The resulting continuous-time dynamics is an integro-differential equation that augments the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad equation with a memory integral, and is capable of describing the quantum state of systems exposed to noise with any integrable power spectral density with no further approximations. We then establish a formalism to evaluate multi-time correlations of measurement outcomes in this general setting, obviating the need for a regression theorem. As an application, we derive the emission spectrum of a driven two-level system coupled to a non-Markovian bath: the familiar Mollow triplet acquires a frequency-dependent linewidth that encodes the memory of the bath. Our work provides a rigorous yet transparent description of the quantum state of non-Markovian systems, opening the door for state estimation and state-based quantum control beyond the Markovian regime.

</details>


### [56] [Preparing High-Fidelity Thermofield Double States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03017)
*Brian J. J. Khor,Nadie LiTenn,Martin Sasieta,Brian Swingle*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于父哈密顿量（parent Hamiltonian）的绝热演化方案，用于制备满足本征态热化假说（ETH）的多体量子系统的热场双态（TFD），并通过数值实验验证了该方法在混合场伊辛模型（mixed field Ising model）和自旋Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev模型中的有效性。研究展示了两种变体方案，其中第二种通过引入惩罚项（penalty term）有效抑制了随系统尺寸增长的保真度衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子计算机的一个核心承诺是能够受控制备超越经典计算能力范围的多体量子态，其中热混合态及其热场双态（TFD）纯化在量子多体物理和量子引力中具有核心地位。现有方法在温度或几何局域性方面存在局限，因此需要一种更具普适性的TFD态制备方案。

Method: 针对能量谱有界且满足本征态热化假说（ETH）的目标系统，构造一个由两份目标哈密顿量（target Hamiltonian）及两者之间的超局域耦合（ultra-local couplings）组成的父哈密顿量（parent Hamiltonian）。通过从强耦合区进行绝热演化（adiabatically evolving down），制备高保真度的TFD态。研究采用数值方法在混合场伊辛模型（一维和二维）以及非局域的自旋Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）模型中测试了两种变体方案。

Result: 较简单的变体方案中，父哈密顿量的基态与TFD态在近量子设备可访问的系统尺寸下具有高重叠，但全局重叠随量子比特数呈指数衰减，每个自由度的误差较小。第二种变体引入可调惩罚项（penalty term），能够减少甚至消除重叠随系统尺寸的衰减现象。

Conclusion: 结合基于ETH的一般性分析，这些结果表明该方法具有广泛适用性，不受特定温度或几何局域性的限制，为TFD态制备提供了一种通用途径。

Abstract: A major promise of quantum computers is the controlled preparation of many-body quantum states beyond the reach of efficient classical computation. Among the most important targets are thermal mixed states and their thermofield double (TFD) purifications, which play central roles in quantum many-body physics and quantum gravity. For target systems with a bounded energy spectrum that obey the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (ETH), we present a parent Hamiltonian built from two copies of the target Hamiltonian and ultra-local couplings between the copies, which we argue is gapped with a ground state that approximates a TFD state of the target Hamiltonian. By adiabatically evolving down from strong coupling, we can thus prepare a high-fidelity TFD state. We study two variants of the parent Hamiltonian using numerical methods in two classes of models: mixed field Ising models in one and two dimensions and non-local "spin Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev'' models. In the simpler variant, the parent Hamiltonian ground state has high overlap with a TFD for system sizes accessible to near-term quantum devices. However, the global overlap decays exponentially with the number of qubits, with a small error per degree of freedom. The second variant introduces an additional penalty term which can be tuned to reduce or remove the decay of the overlap with system size. Together with a general ETH-based analysis, these results suggest a broadly applicable method for TFD preparation that is not limited to particular temperatures or geometric locality.

</details>


### [57] [Strong Locality as a Tetrahedron: A Symmetry-Reduced Geometric Representation of the (3,3,2,2) Bell Scenario](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03104)
*Marek Gazdzicki,Francesco Giacosa,Pawel Piesowicz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对(3,3,2,2)贝尔场景（Bell scenario）提出了强局域模型（strongly-local models）的几何表征，通过引入三维混合矩空间（mixed-moment space），发现强局域区域呈现为正四面体（regular tetrahedron）形式——即“金字塔”（pyramid），并证明仅需三个线性不等式（pyramid inequalities）即可刻画该区域。该表示法将原本684个面定义不等式的36维条件概率空间（conditional-probability space）大幅降维，并直观展示了强局域模型、量子模型（quantum models）与无信号模型（no-signalling models）之间的层次包含关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维贝尔场景（如(3,3,2,2)）中强局域模型的几何结构复杂，完整刻画需684个面定义不等式，缺乏直观的几何解释。本文旨在通过对称性约化与投影降维，寻找一种简洁的几何表征，以更好地理解强局域性（strong locality）及其与量子关联（quantum correlations）和无信号关联（no-signalling correlations）的层次关系。

Method: 通过将参与者视为不可区分的（indistinguishable sites），引入三维混合矩空间，其中混合矩（mixed moments）在非对角测量设置（off-diagonal measurement settings）下计算。在此基础上，利用对称性约化（symmetry reduction）、归一化（normalisation）和投影至混合矩空间（projection）等步骤，将原本36维条件概率空间中的684个面定义不等式降至三个线性不等式。

Result: 强局域区域在该降维表示中呈现为规则正四面体，称为“金字塔”。仅需三个线性不等式（pyramid inequalities）即可将强局域模型（SL）与非强局域模型（非SL）区分开来。在金字塔表示中，层次关系 SL ⊊ Q ⊊ NS 几何上表现为：四面体嵌入一个较大的弯曲体（量子模型Q），该弯曲体再嵌入一个立方体（无信号模型NS）。

Conclusion: 金字塔表示法在定性和定量层面相对于(2,2,2,2)情形的标准CHSH表示（CSHS representation）具有明显优势。该工作为高维贝尔非局域性（Bell nonlocality）的几何理解提供了一种更简洁、直观的框架。

Abstract: We present a geometric characterisation of strongly-local models in the bipartite Bell scenario with three measurement settings per site and binary outcomes, i.e.\ the (3,3,2,2) case. Restricting attention to indistinguishable sites, we introduce a three-dimensional mixed-moment space in which the mixed moments are calculated under off-diagonal measurement settings.
  In this reduced representation, the strongly-local region assumes the remarkably simple form of a regular tetrahedron - the 'pyramid'. We prove that only three independent linear inequalities are required to characterise this region. We call them the pyramid inequalities that separate strongly-local ($\mathcal{SL}$) models from their complement, non-strongly-local ($\mathcal{\overline{SL}}$) models. We also clarify the relation between the symmetry-reduced pyramid representation and the full (3,3,2,2) Bell polytope in the 36-dimensional conditional-probability space, which possesses 684 facet-defining inequalities. The reduction from 684 to three reflects normalisation, symmetry reduction, and projection to the mixed-moment space.
  In the pyramid representation, the hierarchy $\mathcal{SL} \subsetneq \mathcal{Q} \subsetneq \mathcal{NS}$ appears geometrically as a tetrahedron embedded in a somewhat larger curved body of quantum models, $\mathcal{Q}$, which in turn is embedded in a cube of no-signalling models, $\mathcal{NS}$. The qualitative and quantitative advantages of the pyramid representation over the standard CSHS representation for the (2,2,2,2) case are discussed.

</details>


### [58] [Rigorous error bounds for dissipative thermal state preparation from weak system-bath coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03011)
*Christopher Ong,S. A. Parameswaran,Benedikt Placke,Dominik Hahn*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于耗散林德布拉德演化（dissipative Lindbladian evolution）的热态制备（thermal state preparation）协议，证明其中附加的幺正动力学（unitary dynamics）能收紧不动点误差界，其误差以系统-浴耦合强度J的平方标度，并分析了随机化实现（randomized implementation）对共振抑制及可观测量方差的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热态制备是量子多体系统模拟中的核心挑战，尽管近期出现了可证明高效的算法，但基于数字量子模拟的实现仍超出当前量子硬件的能力。后续研究转向了通过碰撞模型（collision model）进行类比模拟，但现有严格方法未利用这些构造天然产生的附加幺正演化对收敛的帮助。

Method: 本研究从理论上分析了由系统-浴相互作用产生的附加幺正项（即“兰姆位移”（Lamb shift）项）对不动点误差界的影响，建立了误差与耦合强度J之间的平方标度关系。同时，明确了随机化实现在抑制驱动与多体能谱间共振中的作用，并界定了该随机化对可观测量引入的额外方差。

Result: 证明了附加幺正贡献确实能收紧不动点误差界，且该误差严格受控于系统-浴耦合强度J，标度为J²。澄清了随机化实现抑制共振的机制，并给出了随机化对可观测量方差的界。此外，对混合时间（mixing time）等实验相关方面进行了数值研究。

Conclusion: 通过调控耦合强度J可以控制系统-浴相互作用产生的虚假兰姆位移项的影响，这为热态制备的物理实现提供了理论保障。随机化实现有助于避免多体谱共振效应，但其代价是增加了可观测量方差。

Abstract: Thermal state preparation is a central challenge in the simulation of quantum many-body systems. Yet, provably efficient algorithms for this task were only introduced recently [Chen et al. Nature 646, 561 (2025)]. These algorithms are based on dissipative Lindbladian evolution which exactly fixes the thermal state. Controlled and efficient digital simulation of this evolution, although possible in principle, remains out of reach for present-day quantum hardware. Subsequent work has therefore focused on analog approximations of the proposed Lindbladians via `collision models' with relatively modest requirements -- a resettable bath of ancilla qubits whose couplings to the system can be tuned in time-dependent fashion -- while still admitting rigorous fixed-point error bounds. Existing rigorous approaches, however, do not exploit the fact that these constructions generically implement not only the desired Lindblad dynamics, but also an additional unitary evolution generated by the system Hamiltonian which may aid convergence to the thermal state [Lloyd and Abanin arXiv:2506.21318 (2025)]. Here, we show that this unitary contribution does indeed tighten the fixed-point error bound and demonstrate that it is rigorously controlled by the system-bath coupling strength $J$, scaling as $J^2$. This demonstrates that the effect of the spurious `Lamb shift' term generated by the system-bath interaction can be controlled by tuning $J$. We clarify the role, previously observed, of a randomized implementation in suppressing possible resonances of the drive with the many-body spectrum, and bound the additional variance that this randomization imposes on observables. Finally, we numerically study aspects of the protocol which are relevant for its practical realization, such as the mixing time.

</details>


### [59] [Exact Quantum Many-Body Scars by a generalized Matrix-Product Ansatz](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03020)
*Sascha Gehrmann,Fabian H. L. Essler*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文基于Derrida-Evans-Hakim-Pasquier方法的思想，提出了一种局域误差抵消（local error cancellation）拟设，用于构造非无怨哈密顿量（non-frustration-free Hamiltonian）下量子多体系统的精确本征态（exact eigenstates），并以矩阵乘积形式（matrix product form）给出显式构造，在一维和二维空间中均提供了具体实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有精确本征态构造方法多局限于无怨哈密顿量（frustration-free Hamiltonians）系统，而对于更一般的非无怨哈密顿量系统缺乏有效的精确解构造手段。作者希望借鉴非对称简单排斥过程（asymmetric simple exclusion process, ASEP）中稳态构造的Derrida-Evans-Hakim-Pasquier方法，将其推广到量子多体系统。

Method: 提出一种基于局域误差抵消（local error cancellation）的拟设方案，借鉴Derrida-Evans-Hakim-Pasquier方法的思想，将精确本征态的构造转化为矩阵乘积形式（matrix product form）下的局域方程求解问题。该方法不要求哈密顿量具有无怨（frustration-free）性质。

Result: 在一维（one spatial dimension）和二维（two spatial dimensions）空间中均给出了显式的构造实例，验证了所提方法的可行性与普适性。

Conclusion: 该工作为非无怨哈密顿量量子多体系统提供了一种全新的精确本征态构造框架，拓展了矩阵乘积态（matrix product state, MPS）方法的适用范围，并从统计力学（statistical mechanics）的非平衡稳态构造问题中汲取了有效的数学工具。

Abstract: We construct exact eigenstates of quantum many-body systems with Hamiltonians that are not frustration-free in matrix product form, based on a local error cancellation ansatz motivated by the Derrida-Evans-Hakim-Pasquier method for finding the stationary state of the asymmetric simple exclusion process. We demonstrate the approach with explicit examples in both one and two spatial dimensions.

</details>


### [60] [Robust spin-squeezing on quantum networks: the lesson from universality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03032)
*Andrea Solfanelli,Augusto Smerzi,Peter Zoller,Nicolò Defenu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文建立了在任意非均匀网络几何（inhomogeneous network geometries）中实现可扩展自旋压缩（scalable spin squeezing）的条件，识别出两种压缩形式——OAT类压缩和临界压缩，并揭示了自旋压缩临界点标度行为由XY铁磁普适性与逾渗普适性之间的非平凡相互作用决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对于量子网络中的自旋压缩研究多集中于均匀系统，而非均匀网络几何结构下的可扩展自旋压缩条件尚未被系统建立。作者旨在填补这一空白，为通用非均匀结构上的可扩展量子计量增益提供统一的理论框架。

Method: 通过分析相互作用图（interaction graph）的谱维数（spectral dimension）这一普适性质，将自旋压缩区分为两种类型：OAT类可扩展压缩和临界压缩。对于OAT类压缩，谱维数直接控制标度行为；对于临界压缩，谱维数仅提供必要条件，充分条件还需系统处于对称性破缺转变（symmetry breaking transition）之下。进一步揭示了自旋压缩临界点的标度行为来自于XY铁磁普适性（xy-ferromagnetic universality）与逾渗普适性（percolation universality）之间的非平凡相互作用。

Result: 建立了可扩展自旋压缩在任意非均匀网络几何中的实现条件，识别了两种不同的压缩形式及其各自的标度控制机制，并将该理论框架应用于若干实验场景。

Conclusion: 该工作为在多种量子模拟平台上设计可扩展量子传感器提供了统一的视角，给出了在通用非均匀结构上实现鲁棒计量增益的清晰且与实验相关的条件。

Abstract: We establish the conditions under which scalable spin squeezing can be achieved in interacting spin ensembles embedded in arbitrary, inhomogeneous network geometries. We identify two different forms of squeezing: OAT-like scalable squeezing is governed solely by the universal properties of the interaction graph and is controlled by its spectral dimension. In critical squeezing, on the other hand, the value of the spectral dimension only furnishes the necessary condition for scalable metrological gain, while the sufficient condition requires the model to lie below the symmetry breaking transition. Therefore, in quantum networks, the scaling of the spin-squeezing critical point emerges from a nontrivial interplay between xy-ferromagnetic universality and percolation universality. We apply this general theoretical framework to several experimental scenarios and discuss sharp and experimentally relevant conditions for achieving robust metrological gain on generic inhomogeneous structures, giving a unifying perspective for designing scalable quantum sensors across diverse quantum simulation platforms.

</details>


### [61] [Information in Many-body Eigenstates: A Question of Learnability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03043)
*Maksymilian Kliczkowski,Jarosław Pawłowski,Masudul Haque*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过机器学习工具，引入一种称为“可学习性（learnability）”的新量化指标，利用编码器-解码器神经网络（encoder-decoder neural network）从单个本征态（eigenstate）重建哈密顿量（Hamiltonian），从而区分谱边缘本征态与谱中段本征态在信息含量上的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多体量子系统（many-body quantum systems）中单个本征态在多大程度上编码了其底层哈密顿量的信息，以及这种编码如何依赖于本征态在能谱中的位置。以往研究已从纠缠结构的角度对谱边缘与谱中段本征态加以区分，但缺乏一种直接的、基于信息含量（information content）的量化方式。

Method: 利用机器学习工具，构建一个编码器-解码器神经网络架构，并设计一个具有物理学启发性质的损失函数（physics-inspired loss function），从单个本征态出发反向预测哈密顿量。将这一预测精度定义为“可学习性”，用以量化本征态中包含的哈密顿量信息。

Result: 对于谱边缘（spectral-edge）本征态，预测精度显著优于谱中段（mid-spectrum）本征态；且学习谱边缘本征态所需的样本数量远少于谱中段本征态。两种类型本征态之间的差异在可学习性这一指标上得到了清晰的体现。

Conclusion: 可学习性可作为衡量本征态信息含量的一个新替代指标；机器学习方法能够有效揭示多体量子系统本征态与其哈密顿量之间的信息关联，并区分谱边缘与谱中段本征态在信息编码上的本质差异。

Abstract: To what extent do individual eigenstates encode information of their underlying Hamiltonian, and how does this depend on their spectral position? For many-body quantum systems, this issue is widely understood in terms of the differing nature of the eigenstates near the spectral edges (low-entanglement, highly-structured eigenstates) and those far from the spectral edges (high-entanglement, near-random eigenstates). Utilizing the availability of machine learning tools, we introduce a new way to quantify the information contained in eigenstates: for a particular learning architecture, how precisely can the Hamiltonian be reconstructed from a single eigenstate? We refer to this property as learnability; it serves as a new, alternative measure of the information content of eigenstates, made possible by machine learning. Using an encoder-decoder neural network and a physics-inspired loss function, we demonstrate how the distinction between two types of eigenstates is manifested as a difference in learnability. For spectral-edge eigenstates, the prediction accuracy is much better, and fewer eigenstates are required to learn the Hamiltonian, compared to mid-spectrum eigenstates.

</details>


### [62] [Operating a bistable qubit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03187)
*Fabrizio Berritta,Jan A. Krzywda,Tom Dvir,Paul Buttles,Stanislav Eilhart,Jeroen Danon,Ferdinand Kuemmeth*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文实验展示了一种基于FPGA经典控制器的自适应协议（1-bit反馈协议），用于对具有双稳态特性的超导量子比特进行高保真度操控。该协议通过单次单次测量（single-shot measurement）估计量子比特的双稳态频率，达到了量子比特内禀熵所设定的信息极限。实验证明该方法能有效抑制由寄生两能级系统（TLS）缺陷引起的Ramsey拍频，使门保真度随时间稳定，并减少约77%的误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寄生两能级系统（two-level-system, TLS）缺陷与量子比特的相互作用会导致量子比特频率发生离散、随机漂移，使量子比特呈现双稳态（bistable）行为，从而限制固态量子处理器的稳定性和性能。现有方法难以高效应对这种由强耦合TLS引起的退相干误差，因此需要一种简单且信息效率高的自适应操控策略。

Method: 采用基于现场可编程门阵列（field-programmable gate array, FPGA）的经典控制器驱动1-bit反馈协议：仅通过一次单次测量（single-shot measurement）即可估计量子比特的双稳态频率，从而在信息层面达到量子比特内禀熵所设定的极限。

Result: 在超导量子比特实验中，该协议有效抑制了TLS诱导的Ramsey拍频（Ramsey beating）；实现了约136 kHz的估算带宽，并将门保真度误差降低了77%。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种简洁且信息效率最优的策略，用于减轻由强耦合TLS缺陷引起的退相误差（dephasing errors），并有望推广至存在少量离散不稳定缺陷的大型量子比特阵列。

Abstract: Parasitic two-level-system (TLS) defects limit the stability and performance of solid-state quantum processors. Their interaction with a qubit can cause discrete, stochastic shifts of the qubit frequency, making the qubit bistable. We experimentally demonstrate an adaptive protocol for operating a bistable qubit with high fidelity using a classical controller powered by a field-programmable gate array (FPGA). Our "1-bit feedback" protocol estimates the qubit's bistable frequency from only one single-shot measurement, reaching the information limit set by the qubit's intrinsic entropy. We validate the protocol in a superconducting qubit by suppressing TLS-induced Ramsey beating, and deploy it to stabilize gate fidelities over time with approximately 136 kHz estimation bandwidth and a 77% error reduction. Our approach provides a simple, yet fundamentally efficient strategy for mitigating dephasing errors induced by strongly coupled TLS defects, and may enable the operation of large future qubit arrays suffering from few remaining, discrete instabilities.

</details>


### [63] [Finite-frequency fluctuation-response bounds for open quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03340)
*Jie Gu,Kangqiao Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文为输入-输出框架下的马尔可夫开放量子系统推导了有限频率的涨落-响应不等式，将测量的锁相响应-噪声矩阵约束为输出场量子Fisher信息率的上界，并进一步在耗散振幅调制情形下将其关联至频率无关的信号通道活性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在开放量子系统的输入-输出设定中，关于下游测量（downstream measurement）的响应与噪声之间的基本量化关系尚不明确。该工作旨在推导一个适用于有限频率（finite-frequency）的涨落-响应不等式，以建立响应矩阵与量子Fisher信息率（quantum Fisher information rate）之间的严格上界关系。

Method: 采用输入-输出理论（input-output theory），针对马尔可夫开放量子系统（Markovian open quantum systems）进行分析。通过将下游测量锁相响应-噪声矩阵与输出场的量子Fisher信息率相联系，分别考虑耗散振幅调制（dissipative amplitude modulation）和动力学调制（kinetic modulation）两种情形，并将不等式推广至多信号通道（multiple signal channels）和实际有限频率正交分量（real finite-frequency quadratures）。

Result: 对于真空输入的耗散振幅调制，输出场量子Fisher信息率被频率无关的信号通道活性（signal-channel activity）所界定；对于动力学调制，该活性退化为稳态通道流（stationary channel fluxes）。该不等式具有“面向探测器但非定迹无关”（detector-facing but unraveling-independent）的性质：上界由量子场本身设定，与具体探测方案或轨迹表示无关。

Conclusion: 研究为单边腔（single-sided cavity）、共振荧光（resonance fluorescence）以及截断Kerr参量猫谐振器（truncated Kerr-parametric cat resonator）等典型系统提供了有限频率涨落-响应不等式的实例验证，揭示了噪声与响应之间的量子信息论约束。

Abstract: We derive a finite-frequency fluctuation-response inequality for Markovian open quantum systems in an input-output setting. For any downstream measurement of the emitted field, the measured lock-in response-to-noise matrix is bounded by the output-field quantum Fisher information rate. For dissipative amplitude modulation with vacuum inputs, this information rate is further bounded by a frequency-independent signal-channel activity, which reduces for kinetic modulation to the stationary channel fluxes. The result is detector-facing but unraveling-independent: it applies after choosing a measurement record, while the information ceiling is set by the quantum field before any detection scheme or trajectory representation is selected. We formulate the bound for multiple signal channels and real finite-frequency quadratures, and illustrate it with a single-sided cavity, resonance fluorescence, and a truncated Kerr-parametric cat resonator.

</details>


### [64] [Interplay of Nonstabilizerness and Ergotropy in Quantum Batteries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03600)
*Tanoy Kanti Konar,Jakub Zakrzewski*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了非稳定化子特性（nonstabilizerness）在量子电池（quantum batteries）背景中的作用，揭示了在U(1)对称性保持的相互作用下，电池中存储的功（ergotropy）与复合系统的总非稳定化子之间存在一一对应关系；而在更一般的相互作用下，这种对应关系通常消失。此外，当电池初始处于非稳定化子态并通过克利福德演化（Clifford evolution）充电时，最大平均充电功率与初始非稳定化子量呈非单调依赖，且最优功率可在初始态不含任何魔法（magic）时实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非稳定化子特性（nonstabilizerness）是量子计算机上高效模拟量子系统的关键要素，但其在量子电池（quantum batteries）这一新兴能量存储框架中的作用尚未被充分探索。本文旨在通过研究充电器与电池之间的不同相互作用类型，定量揭示非稳定化子与功存储能力之间的关联。

Method: 考虑一个由N个自旋-1/2粒子组成的系统，左半部分作为充电器（charger），右半部分作为电池（battery）。分别研究了保持U(1)对称性和打破该对称性的两类充电器-电池相互作用，并量化了在量子电池中存储功所需的非稳定化子量。此外，还考察了电池初始化为非稳定化子态、通过克利福德演化（Clifford evolution）充电的互补情景。

Result: 当相互作用哈密顿量保持U(1)对称性时，电池中存储的功（ergotropy）与复合系统的总非稳定化子之间存在一一对应关系；对于不保持该对称性的更一般相互作用，该对应关系通常消失。在电池初始处于非稳定化子态的互补情景中，最大平均充电功率与初始非稳定化子量呈非单调依赖关系。

Conclusion: 最高平均充电功率可以在初始态不含任何魔法（magic）时实现，表明在该协议下，初始魔法并非产生最优充电功率的必要资源。

Abstract: Nonstabilizerness plays an essential role in an efficient simulation of quantum systems on quantum computers. In this work, we investigate its role in the context of quantum batteries (QBs). To this end, we consider a system of N spin-1/2 particles, where the left half serves as the charger and the right half acts as the battery. By studying different classes of interactions between the charger and the battery, we quantify the amount of nonstabilizerness required to store work in the QB. Our results reveal that a one-to-one correspondence between the ergotropy stored in the battery and the total nonstabilizerness of the composite system emerges whenever the interaction Hamiltonian preserves a U(1) symmetry. In contrast, this correspondence is generally lost for more generic interactions that do not respect this symmetry. Finally, we examine the complementary scenario in which the battery is initialized in a nonstabilizer state and subsequently charged through Clifford evolution. In this case, we find that the maximum average charging power exhibits a non-monotonic dependence on the initial nonstabilizerness. Remarkably, the highest average power can be achieved even when the initial state carries no magic (nonstabilizerness), demonstrating that the initial magic is not a necessary resource for generating an optimal charging power in this protocol.

</details>


### [65] [A Berry-Esseen Bound for Quantum Lattice Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03829)
*Marcus Cramer,Fernando G. S. L. Brandão,Mădălin Guţă,Álvaro M. Alhambra,Matteo Scandi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了量子晶格系统（quantum lattice systems）中的 Berry-Esseen 定理，给出了局部可观测量的统计涨落（statistical fluctuations）趋近正态分布（normal distribution）的严格收敛速率估计，误差上界为 $\mathcal{O}(N^{-1/2} \text{polylog}(N))$，在忽略对数因子意义下达到最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大量子系统中局部可观测量（local observables）的统计涨落通常预期服从中心极限定理（central limit theorem），但已有结果缺乏对有限系统尺寸下收敛速度的严格刻画。本文旨在为量子晶格系统提供一种强化的中心极限定理，即 Berry-Esseen 定理，以给出一个严格的收敛估计。

Method: 针对具有有限关联长度（finite correlation length）的量子态以及作用于 $N$ 粒子的局域量子哈密顿量（local quantum Hamiltonian），推导了局部可观测量（如能量）的测量结果分布与正态分布之间的误差上界。

Result: 证明该误差上界为 $\mathcal{O}(N^{-1/2} \text{polylog}(N))$，并且该标度在忽略对数因子的意义下是渐进最优的。

Conclusion: 该结果严格确立了量子晶格系统中局部可观测量的正态逼近速率，为量子统计力学（quantum statistical mechanics）中涨落行为的理解提供了理论基础。

Abstract: It is expected that the statistical fluctuations of local observables in large quantum systems obey the central limit theorem, and approximate a normal distribution as their size grows. Here, we prove a version of the Berry-Esseen theorem for quantum lattice systems, which strengthens that central limit theorem by providing a rigorous convergence estimate towards the normal distribution for large but finite system size. Given a local quantum Hamiltonian on $N$ particles and a quantum state with a finite correlation length, the result states that the measurement of local observables such as the energy follows a normal distribution, up to an error scaling as $\mathcal{O}\left(N^{-\frac{1}{2}} \text{polylog}(N)\right)$, which is optimal up to logarithmic factors.

</details>


### [66] [Entanglement transitions in translation-invariant tensor networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04026)
*Yi-Cheng Wang,Samuel J. Garratt,Ehud Altman*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究近似收缩平移不变张量网络（translation-invariant tensor networks）的计算复杂度，发现其与转移矩阵（transfer matrix）本征谱及行状态纠缠熵之间存在相变关联，并在体积律（volume-law）与面积律（area-law）纠缠相之间建立了清晰联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解平移不变张量网络近似收缩的计算复杂度，特别是在混沌弗洛凯（chaotic Floquet）与强非幺正（non-unitary）极限之间的行为，以及其与纠缠结构的关系。

Method: 分析一族插值于混沌Floquet与强非幺正极限之间的转移矩阵，研究其本征谱在复平面上的分布，以及行状态（row state）在时间演化下的纠缠熵行为。

Result: 发现了体积律与面积律纠缠之间的相变：在体积律相中，转移矩阵本征谱在复平面上呈现密集环形分布且具有尖锐外缘，类似于非幺正随机矩阵行为；在面积律相中，则存在一个主导本征值。

Conclusion: 建立了张量网络收缩复杂度、转移矩阵谱性质与非幺正动力学下的纯化（purification）之间的关联。

Abstract: We study the complexity of approximately contracting translation-invariant tensor networks. The computational cost of row-by-row tensor network contraction, which defines a discrete time evolution governed by a fixed transfer matrix, is associated with the entanglement of the state of a row. By analyzing a family of tensor networks whose transfer matrices interpolate between chaotic Floquet and strongly non-unitary limits, we uncover a transition between volume- and area-law entanglement in states evolved under the transfer matrix. We show that deep in the volume-law phase the spectrum of the transfer matrix in the complex plane consists of a dense ring with a sharp outer edge, reminiscent of behavior identified for non-unitary random matrices. At late times an evolving row state therefore has significant contributions from many eigenvectors with nearly degenerate eigenvalue magnitudes. In the area-law phase, there is instead a distinct leading eigenvalue. Our results establish connections between contraction complexity, spectral properties of the transfer matrix, and purification under non-unitary dynamics.

</details>

### [67] [Building a physics-aware AI ecosystem for solid-state hydrogen storage materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03081)
*Seong-Hoon Jang,Yiwen Yao,Chuanyu Liu,Linda Zhang,Di Zhang,Xue Jia,Hung Ba Tran,Eric Jianfeng Cheng,Ryuhei Sato,Yusuke Ohashi,Toyoto Sato,Yusuke Hashimoto,Mark Allendorf,Nongnuch Artrith,Marcello Baricco,Andreas Borgschulte,Darren P. TL;DR: 本文针对储氢材料（HSM）发现中多尺度热力学、动力学与微观结构演化耦合的瓶颈问题，提出了一个整合连贯数据基础设施、物理约束建模与AI驱动逆向设计的闭环发现框架，通过嵌入物理约束和实验反馈实现自适应的物理一致性优化，为自主、数字孪生驱动的储氢材料发现奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢能系统的规模化应用受限于储氢材料中热力学、动力学与微观结构演化的多尺度耦合问题。现有AI加速材料发现方法存在数据碎片化、物理一致性不足以及与实验验证整合薄弱等局限。

Method: 提出一个统一框架，在闭环发现范式（closed-loop discovery paradigm）中整合连贯数据基础设施（coherent data infrastructure）、物理约束建模（physics-grounded modeling）与AI驱动的逆向设计（AI-driven inverse design），并通过嵌入物理约束和实验反馈实现自适应优化。

Result: 该方法能够实现自适应的、物理一致的优化，从而建立通往自主化、数字孪生驱动（digital-twin-enabled）的储氢材料发现路径。

Conclusion: 通过将物理约束与实验反馈有机结合于AI驱动的发现循环中，该框架有望克服当前材料发现中数据碎片化和物理一致性不足的瓶颈，最终实现储氢材料的自主化数字化发现。

Abstract: Hydrogen storage remains a central bottleneck for scalable hydrogen energy systems due to the multiscale and coupled nature of the thermodynamics, kinetics, and microstructural evolution of hydrogen storage materials (HSMs). Although artificial intelligence (AI) has accelerated materials discovery, current approaches remain constrained by fragmented data, limited physical consistency, and weak integration with experimental validation. Here, we propose a unified framework that integrates coherent data infrastructure, physics-grounded modeling, and AI-driven inverse design within a closed-loop discovery paradigm. By embedding physical constraints and experimental feedback, this approach enables adaptive, physically consistent optimization, thereby establishing a pathway toward autonomous, digital-twin-enabled discovery of HSMs.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（large language models, LLMs）正在迅速改变材料科学和化学领域的研究方式，但缺乏对其应用模式的系统化梳理，本文旨在识别这些系统在整个科学生命周期中的新兴使用模式。

Method: 本文分析了一组广泛的社区开发的LLM应用，将其分为两个互补类别：知识基础设施（Knowledge Infrastructure），即对科学信息进行结构化、检索、综合和验证的系统；以及行动系统（Action Systems），即在计算和实验环境中执行、协调或自动化科学工作的系统。

Result: 提交的应用案例显示出从单一用途LLM工具向集成式多智能体工作流（integrated multi-agent workflows）的转变，这些工作流结合了检索（retrieval）、推理（reasoning）、工具使用（tool use）和领域特定验证。突出主题包括：作为基石基础设施的检索增强生成（retrieval-augmented generation）、持久的结构化知识表示（persistent structured knowledge representations）、多模态（multimodal）和多语言科学输入，以及实验室集成闭环系统（laboratory-integrated closed-loop systems）的早期进展。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型正从通用型助手演变为用于科学推理和行动的可组合基础设施（composable infrastructure）。本文提供了这一转型过程的社区快照，以及一个实用的分类体系（taxonomy），用以理解材料科学和化学领域新兴的LLM驱动工作流。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are rapidly changing how researchers in materials science and chemistry discover, organize, and act on scientific knowledge. This paper analyzes a broad set of community-developed LLM applications in an effort to identify emerging patterns in how these systems can be used across the scientific research lifecycle. We organize the projects into two complementary categories: Knowledge Infrastructure, systems that structure, retrieve, synthesize, and validate scientific information; and Action Systems, systems that execute, coordinate, or automate scientific work across computational and experimental environments. The submissions reveal a shift from single-purpose LLM tools toward integrated, multi-agent workflows that combine retrieval, reasoning, tool use, and domain-specific validation. Prominent themes include retrieval-augmented generation as grounding infrastructure, persistent structured knowledge representations, multimodal and multilingual scientific inputs, and early progress toward laboratory-integrated closed-loop systems. Together, these results suggest that LLMs are evolving from general-purpose assistants into composable infrastructure for scientific reasoning and action. This work provides a community snapshot of that transition and a practical taxonomy for understanding emerging LLM-enabled workflows in materials science and chemistry.

### [69] [Coupled phase transitions in crystalline solids with extreme chemical disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03444)
*Subha Dey,Rukma Nevgi,Suresh Chandra Joshi,Sourav Chowdhury,Nandana Bhattacharya,Kashish Kapoor,Tinku Dan,Subhadip Chowdhury,Sabyasachi Karmakar,S. D. Kaushik,Shibabrata Nandi,Christoph Klewe,Manuel Valvidares,Moritz Hoesch,George E. Sterbinsky,Srimanta Middey*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过设计成分复杂氧化物（CCOs），证明了在高熵氧化物（HEOs）这类高度化学无序的体系中，依然可以发生耦合的结构相变，并以尖晶石型材料[Mn$_{0.2}$Co$_{0.2}$Ni$_{0.2}$Cu$_{0.2}$Zn$_{0.2}$]Cr$_2$O$_4$为例，展示了先后由轨道驱动和磁性驱动的两次连续结构相变，提出了“通过竞争实现合作”（cooperation via competition）的局域畸变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高熵氧化物（HEOs）通常稳定在高度对称的立方相中，由于极端化学无序，结构相变被认为十分罕见，类似高熵合金中的行为。这引发了一个基本问题：在如此无序的体系中，耦合相变的丰富物理是否依然可以存在。

Method: 本文通过靶向设计成分复杂氧化物（CCOs）触发对称性降低的相变，以尖晶石型材料为代表性案例。具体对[Mn$_{0.2}$Co$_{0.2}$Ni$_{0.2}$Cu$_{0.2}$Zn$_{0.2}$]Cr$_2$O$_4$进行冷却实验，并通过系统替换A位阳离子探究Ni和Cu的必要性，结合元素特定的局域结构（local structure）研究揭示不同离子的局域畸变特征。

Result: 含有两种Jahn-Teller（J-T）活性离子的[Mn$_{0.2}$Co$_{0.2}$Ni$_{0.2}$Cu$_{0.2}$Zn$_{0.2}$]Cr$_2$O$_4$在冷却时发生两次连续耦合结构相变：100 K处的轨道驱动（orbital-driven）相变和40 K处的磁性驱动（magnetism-driven）相变。系统替换A位阳离子表明Ni和Cu对相变必不可少；局域结构研究显示Ni和Cu周围存在截然相反（opposing）的局域畸变，而Mn、Co、Zn基本未畸变。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了CCOs可以通过化学无序晶格中局域畸变的“通过竞争实现合作”（cooperation via competition）机制来承载耦合相变。这一发现拓展了复杂氧化物的设计原理，引入了一种超越传统对称性约束、在高熵体系中调控结构和功能性质的新范式。

Abstract: Structural phase transitions often couple to magnetic and electronic degrees of freedom, enabling emergent phenomena in solids. In high-entropy oxides (HEOs), which typically stabilize in highly symmetric cubic phases, such transitions are considered rare due to the extreme chemical disorder-analogous to the behavior observed in high-entropy alloys. This raises a fundamental question: can the rich physics of coupled phase transitions persist in such disordered systems? Here, we show that targeted design of compositionally complex oxides (CCOs) can trigger symmetry-lowering transitions, with spinel-type materials serving as a representative case. For instance, [Mn$_{0.2}$Co$_{0.2}$Ni$_{0.2}$Cu$_{0.2}$Zn$_{0.2}$]Cr$_2$O$_4$, having two Jahn-Teller (J-T) active ions, undergoes two successive coupled structural transitions upon cooling: an orbital-driven transition at 100 K and a magnetism-driven transition at 40 K. Systematic substitution of $A$-site cations reveals that both Ni and Cu are essential for these transitions. Element specific local structure investigations uncover distinct and opposing local distortions around Ni and Cu, while Mn, Co, and Zn remain largely undistorted. These results establish that CCOs can host coupled phase transitions through `cooperation via competition' among local distortions in a chemically disordered lattice. This discovery expands the design principles for complex oxides, introducing a new paradigm for tuning structural and functional properties in high-entropy systems beyond conventional symmetry constraints.

</details>


### [70] [Energy dissipation at the atomic scale explains how fracture energy depends on crack velocity in silica glass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03457)
*Marthe Grønlie Guren,Sigbjørn Løland Bore,François Renard,Henrik Andersen Sveinsson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过第一性原理机器学习势函数的分子动力学模拟，发现二氧化硅玻璃的结构断裂能（fracture energy）在低于分叉阈值（branching threshold）时即可上升最多33%，表明断裂能并非恒定材料属性。该上升大致等分归因于本征表面能密度（intrinsic surface energy density）的增加和纳米尺度粗糙化（nanoscale roughening）导致的真实断裂表面积增大。结果表明，动态断裂（dynamic fracture）不仅通过增加表观表面来提升断裂能，更通过在纳米尺度上形成根本不同的表面来实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脆性材料的断裂能随裂纹速度（crack velocity）增加而上升，此前通常归因于路径失稳造成的表面粗糙化（surface roughening）。作者旨在探究，在低于分叉阈值的条件下，断裂能是否仍会发生显著变化，并厘清其微观机制究竟是单纯的表面面积增加，还是涉及表面性质的根本改变。

Method: 采用第一性原理机器学习势函数（first-principles machine learned interatomic potential）对二氧化硅玻璃进行分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations），研究裂纹速度对结构断裂能的影响，并定量分解断裂能上升的贡献来源。

Result: 在低于分叉阈值时，结构断裂能上升最多33%；该上升大致等分地来自本征表面能密度的增加和纳米尺度粗糙化导致的真实表面积增加。

Conclusion: 断裂能并非恒定材料属性；动态断裂在二氧化硅玻璃中提升断裂能的机制，除了产生更多表观表面外，更关键的是在纳米尺度上创造了一种根本不同的表面。

Abstract: The fracture energy of brittle materials rises with crack velocity, and this effect is typically attributed to surface roughening from path instabilities. Here we show, using molecular dynamics simulations of silica glass with a first-principles machine learned interatomic potential, that the structural fracture energy rises by up to 33 % already below the branching threshold, showing that fracture energy is not a constant material property. This rise in fracture energy is roughly equally partitioned between an increase in the intrinsic surface energy density and nanoscale roughening that increases the real fracture surface area. Results demonstrate that dynamic fracture in silica glass increases the fracture energy not merely by creating more apparent surface, but also by creating a fundamentally different surface at the nanoscale.

</details>


### [71] [Influence of twist angle on ultrafast charge separation in WS2-graphene heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03480)
*Niklas Hofmann,Leonard Weigl,Johannes Gradl,Stiven Forti,Domenica Convertino,Camilla Coletti,Isabella Gierz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究利用时间分辨与角分辨光电子能谱（trARPES）直接探测了外延生长的WS₂-石墨烯范德华异质结（vdW heterostructure）中超快电荷转移过程，发现扭转角（twist angle）为0°时电荷分离效率高，而30°时电子与空穴转移速率相近，表明扭转角对电荷分离效率具有关键调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管扭转角对莫尔条纹（moiré pattern）、能带结构（band structure）及关联态（correlated states）的影响已有充分研究，但其对超快电荷转移（ultrafast charge transfer）的影响仍存在争议，亟待实验澄清。

Method: 采用时间分辨与角分辨光电子能谱（trARPES）技术，直接探测了扭转角分别为0°和30°的外延生长WS₂-石墨烯范德华异质结中的超快电荷转移过程，光激发能量为ħω=3.1 eV。

Result: 在0°扭转角下观测到高效的电荷分离；而在30°扭转角下，电子与空穴的转移速率接近，电荷分离效率显著降低。

Conclusion: 扭转角是调控范德华异质结中电荷分离效率的关键参数，这一发现为设计光伏（photovoltaics）和光电子（optoelectronics）器件中的vdW异质结提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Van der Waals (vdW) heterostructures, formed by stacking two-dimensional materials, offer highly tunable electronic and optical properties, with the twist angle between layers acting as a critical tuning parameter. While its impact on moiré patterns, band structure, and correlated states is well-established, the influence of twist angle on ultrafast charge transfer remains controversial. Here, we employ time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (trARPES) to directly probe ultrafast charge transfer in epitaxially grown WS\textsubscript{2}-graphene heterostructures with twist angles of 0$^{\circ}$ and 30$^{\circ}$. Upon photoexcitation at $\hbarω= 3.1\,\mathrm{eV}$, we observe efficient charge separation at 0$^{\circ}$, while at 30$^{\circ}$, electron and hole transfer occur at similar rates. Our results highlight the crucial role of the twist angle in controlling charge separation efficiency, offering valuable insights for designing vdW heterostructures for applications in photovoltaics and optoelectronics.

</details>


### [72] [Scale-Dependent Input Representation and Confidence Estimation for LLMs in Materials Property Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03515)
*Shuichiro Ozawa,Izumi Takahara,Teruyasu Mizoguchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过微调不同规模的Llama模型（1B和8B），系统评估了五种输入表征对无机晶体材料性质预测（形成能和带隙）的影响，发现最优输入表征依赖于模型规模；此外，微调后模型的平均负对数似然（mean negative log-likelihood, mean NLL）可作为有效的预测置信度指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型（large language models, LLMs）在材料科学中的应用日益增多，但预测精度、输入表征与模型规模之间的关系仍不明确，且缺乏可靠的预测置信度评估方法。本研究旨在系统性地填补这些空白。

Method: 采用低秩适配（low-rank adaptation, LoRA）技术微调两个不同规模的Llama模型（1B和8B）；在无机晶体结构数据集上，系统评估五种输入表征（化学成分、晶体摘要、局域环境描述、全文描述和晶体学信息文件）对形成能和带隙预测性能的影响。

Result: 最优输入表征依赖于模型规模：1B模型在紧凑表征下表现更好，8B模型在较长自然语言描述和CIF输入下仍保持高精度。包含空间群信息的晶体摘要始终优于仅含成分的输入。微调后模型的预测误差与平均负对数似然（mean NLL）之间存在一致趋势，即mean NLL越低，预测误差越小。

Conclusion: 输入表征和模型规模在大语言模型驱动的材料性质预测中均起关键作用；平均负对数似然（mean NLL）可作为无需额外训练的有效且计算高效的预测置信度指标。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly applied to materials science. However, the relationship between prediction accuracy, input representation, and model scale remains unclear, and reliable methods for assessing prediction confidence have not yet been established. In this study, we fine-tune two Llama models of different scales (1B and 8B) using low-rank adaptation (LoRA) on an inorganic crystal structure dataset. We systematically evaluate five input representations, namely chemical composition, crystal summary, local environment description, full text description, and crystallographic information files (CIF), for formation energy and bandgap prediction. Our results show that the optimal input representation depends on model scale. The 1B model performs better with compact representations, whereas the 8B model maintains high accuracy even with longer natural-language descriptions and CIF inputs. Across both model scales, crystal summaries that include space-group information consistently outperform composition-only inputs, indicating that symmetry information serves as a robust and informative feature. We further analyze the relationship between prediction error and the mean negative log-likelihood (mean NLL) of tokens corresponding to predicted numerical values. While no clear correlation is observed in base models, fine-tuned models exhibit a consistent trend in which lower mean NLL corresponds to smaller prediction errors. This result suggests that mean NLL can serve as a practical confidence indicator without requiring additional training. These findings demonstrate that both input representation and model scale play critical roles in LLM-based materials property prediction, and that mean NLL provides an effective and computationally efficient measure of prediction confidence.

</details>


### [73] [Adjacent Sink Strengths Used in Multiscale Kinetic Rate Equation Simulations of Defects and Impurities in Solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03529)
*Tommy Ahlgren*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文首次推导了相邻陷阱汇强度（adjacent sink strength）的解析表达式，并将其整合到经典动力学速率方程（kRE）建模中，解决了传统kRE因忽略相邻再捕获效应而导致的热脱附谱（TDS）温度偏移和动力学参数不准确的问题，显著提升了缺陷与杂质演化的多尺度模拟预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统动力学速率方程（kinetic rate equation, kRE）仅包含随机位置汇强度（random-position sink strengths），无法描述缺陷在脱陷或离解事件中从陷阱附近释放时增强的再捕获效应，导致热脱附谱（thermal desorption spectroscopy, TDS）峰温被系统性低估以及与实验数据拟合时得到的动力学参数（如俘获能、脱附频率）物理不一致。

Method: 首次推导了相邻汇强度（adjacent sink strength）的解析表达式，并引入有限杂质扩散跳跃长度（finite impurity diffusion jump length）的修正；提出了将这些表达式集成到kRE模拟中的实际实现策略。

Result: 与动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte Carlo, kMC）基准对比表明，相邻汇强度主导了再捕获概率（retrapping probability），是正确再现TDS释放峰温度依赖性的关键；仅使用随机汇强度的模拟虽可拟合TDS谱，但拟合得到的俘获能（trapping energies）、脱附频率（detrapping frequencies）和扩散参数往往物理上不一致。

Conclusion: 该相邻汇强度公式显著提升了kRE建模的预测能力，实现了缺陷与杂质行为的精确多尺度模拟，并为未来扩展至与位错（dislocations）和晶界（grain boundaries）等扩展缺陷相关的相邻汇强度奠定了基础，有助于解决实验与模拟之间在俘获能量学上的长期不一致问题。

Abstract: Kinetic Rate Equation (kRE) modeling is widely used to simulate defect and impurity evolution in solids over experimentally relevant time and length scales. However, conventional kRE formulations include only random-position sink strengths, which adequately describe trapping of defects created at random lattice sites but fail to capture the enhanced retrapping of defects released directly adjacent to traps during detrapping or dissociation events. This omission leads to systematic errors, including underestimated thermal desorption (TDS) peak temperatures and incorrect kinetic parameters when fitting to experimental data. In this work, we derive for the first time analytical expressions for the adjacent sink strength, including correction for finite impurity diffusion jump length. We provide a practical implementation strategy for integrating these expressions into kRE simulations. Comparisons with kinetic Monte Carlo (kMC) benchmarks demonstrate that adjacent sink strengths dominate the retrapping probability and are essential for reproducing the correct temperature dependence of TDS release peaks. Simulations that employ only random sink strengths can still be tuned to match TDS spectra; however, the resulting fitted trapping energies, detrapping frequencies, and diffusion parameters are often physically inconsistent. The adjacent sink strength formulation introduced here significantly improves the predictive capability of kRE modeling, enabling accurate multiscale simulations of defect and impurity behavior in materials. This framework also establishes a foundation for future extensions, including adjacent sink strengths associated with extended defects such as dislocations and grain boundaries, offering new opportunities to resolve persistent discrepancies between experimental and simulated trapping energetics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常将规范场项视为可忽略或仅为规范SOC（canonical SOC）的可加修正；本文旨在验证该规范场项在非平衡自旋-轨道动力学中是否具有不可或缺的定量与定性作用。

Method: 采用实时含时密度泛函理论（real-time time-dependent density functional theory, rt-TDDFT）进行数值计算，针对具有镜面对称（mirror symmetry）、滑移面对称（glide symmetry）及螺旋旋转对称（screw-rotational symmetry）的代表性体系，分析自旋-轨道动力学行为。

Result: 当含时哈密顿量中的规范场项扰乱了规范项的对称性时，自旋态随时间演化逐渐脱离对称性冻结态，形成动态自旋态（dynamical spin state）。

Conclusion: 在非平衡自旋-轨道动力学中，规范不变表述（gauge-invariant formulation）不仅具有形式上的必要性，而且在定量上至关重要——即使外场很弱，也不能忽略规范场项。

Abstract: When a condensed-matter system is subjected to external electromagnetic fields, the gauge-invariant formulation of physical operators must explicitly incorporate the gauge-field contribution. However, in the context of spin-orbit coupling (SOC), this gauge-field term is often regarded as negligible or merely additive compared to the canonical SOC, which is typically localized near atomic cores. Here, we demonstrate that the symmetry breaking and consequent spin dynamics are governed by the gauge-field term, without which the spins remain symmetry-constrained. We perform real-time time-dependent density functional theory calculations to investigate spin-orbit dynamics, focusing on representative cases with mirror, glide, and screw-rotational symmetry. We demonstrate that when the gauge-field term in the time-dependent Hamiltonian perturbs the symmetry of the canonical term, a dynamical spin state gradually develops during the time evolution, beyond the symmetry-frozen states. We suggest that, for nonequilibrium spin-orbit dynamics, the gauge-invariant formulation of SOC is not only formally required but also quantitatively essential, even for a weak external field.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用时间分辨极紫外光电子能谱（time- and angle-resolved extreme-ultraviolet photoemission spectroscopy），并结合含时Lindblad主方程形式（time-dependent Lindblad master-equation formalism）进行理论建模。

Abstract: The quantum geometric properties of Bloch electrons fundamentally govern light-matter interactions and optical selection rules in solids. In semiconducting transition-metal dichalcogenides, circularly polarized excitation near the band edge enables valley-selective interband transitions, providing the basis for valleytronics. While nonlinear optical protocols are being developed to manipulate and probe valley selection rules, they largely rely on band-edge transitions that proceed via virtual intermediate states. Here, we demonstrate a doubly resonant cascaded nonlinear pathway from the valence band to high-lying states, mediated by a real intermediate state whose participation substantially reshapes the valley optical selection rules. Using time- and angle-resolved extreme-ultraviolet photoemission spectroscopy in combination with a time-dependent Lindblad master-equation formalism, we show that this cascaded nonlinear photoexcitation produces a substantially enhanced high-lying valley polarization compared to the conventional linear optical response near the band edge. ### [79] [A Correction Method for Crack Area Overestimation in Phase-Field Fracture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03731)
*M. Castillón,J. Segurado,I. Romero*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文针对相场断裂模型高估裂纹面积的问题，基于能量均分（energy equipartition）原理提出一种网格无关的修正框架：利用梯度项能量的两倍来近似裂纹面积，从而避免了传统网格依赖修正和骨架化算法的缺陷，并在二维与三维基准测试中验证了其准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相场断裂模型（phase-field fracture model）因扩散裂纹表示和数值伪影（如应变局部化）而系统性地高估裂纹面积，降低了断裂预测的精度。现有修正策略（网格依赖因子、骨架化算法）在非结构化网格或复杂裂纹拓扑下可靠性差、复杂度高，亟需一种鲁棒且网格无关的修正方法。

Method: 基于能量均分原理：当长度尺度参数趋近于零时，相场项（phase-field term）与梯度项（gradient term）的能量贡献相等。由于数值伪影主要影响相场项而梯度项几乎不受干扰，因此裂纹面积可近似取梯度依赖能量（gradient-dependent energy）的两倍。该方法无需网格修正，可直接推广至三维全域。

Result: 在具有解析解的基准问题上进行验证，并与骨架化（skeletonization）等方法对比，证明了所提方法的准确性。随后将其应用于含曲线裂纹路径的复杂几何体，并在三维模拟中进行了评估。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于能量均分的裂纹面积修正框架具有网格无关性，能有效克服传统方法的局限性，为相场断裂模型提供了更精确且适用于复杂几何与三维场景的裂纹面积估计方案。

Abstract: Phase-field fracture models are known to overestimate the crack area, a discrepancy that compromises the accuracy of fracture predictions. This issue stems from the diffuse crack representation and numerical artifacts, such as strain localization, where the phase-field variable artificially saturates across finite elements.
  Existing correction strategies, including mesh-dependent factors and skeletonization algorithms, have significant limitations. Mesh-based corrections are often unreliable for unstructured meshes, while skeletonization can be complex and inaccurate for intricate crack topologies, especially in three dimensions.
  This paper introduces a novel and robust framework to correct this overestimation. Our approach is founded on the principle of energy equipartition, where the energy contributions from the phase-field and its gradient are equal as the length-scale parameter approaches zero. Since numerical artifacts primarily affect the phase-field term while leaving the gradient term largely unperturbed, we propose that the crack area can be accurately approximated as twice the gradient-dependent energy. This method is inherently mesh-independent and readily applicable to the entire domain, including 3D simulations.
  The proposed methodology is validated against benchmarks with analytical solutions and compared with established methods like skeletonization to demonstrate its accuracy. It is then applied to complex geometries with curvilinear crack paths and evaluated in a three-dimensional simulation.

</details>
