*Wael Othman,Ibrahim Alghoul,K-F. Aguey-Zinsou,Nacir Tit,Tanveer Hussain*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报告了一种缺陷工程化的二维二氮化铍（BeN₂）单层材料，通过引入铍空位并修饰碱金属（Li、Na、K），实现了高容量、可逆的氢气存储，其储氢容量（最高11.64 wt%）显著超过美国能源部（DOE）设定的最终目标（6.50 wt%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢气（H₂）虽具有最高的质量能量密度，但在标准条件下其体积能量密度极低，给安全、高效、可逆的存储带来了根本性的材料挑战。现有材料难以同时满足高容量和近常温可逆吸附的需求，因此需要开发新型轻质多孔材料。

Method: 利用第一性原理（first-principles）计算和从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics, AIMD）模拟，研究了一种包含两个本征铍空位的2×2超胞BeN₂单层，用于稳定负载Li、Na、K原子；通过计算金属-空位结合能、吸附能以及热稳定性来评估储氢性能。

Result: 该材料中碱金属与空位的平均结合能分别为−3.80 eV（Li）、−2.94 eV（Na）和−3.18 eV（K），有效抑制了金属团聚；在400 K下热稳定性得到验证；每个超胞最多可吸附20个H₂分子，平均吸附能位于−0.17至−0.19 eV的可逆吸附窗口内；相应的质量储氢容量分别为11.64 wt%（Li）、9.82 wt%（Na）和8.49 wt%（K），远超DOE最终目标（6.50 wt%）。

Conclusion: 空位缺陷与碱金属协同修饰的二维BeN₂单层是一种可行的、可扩展的高密度可逆储氢材料设计策略，为工程化极性轻质材料用于能源存储提供了新方向。

Abstract: Hydrogen (H2) possesses the highest gravimetric energy density of any chemical fuel and is the most abundant element in the universe. However, its extremely low volumetric energy density at standard conditions imposes a fundamental materials challenge for safe, efficient, and reversible storage. Here, we report a defect-engineered 2D beryllium dinitride (BeN2) monolayer that enables stable light-metal functionalization for high-capacity H2 storage. A 2 x 2 supercell containing two intrinsic beryllium vacancies accommodates four Li, Na, and K atoms without clustering, exhibiting strong average metal-vacancy binding energies of -3.80, -2.94, and -3.18 eV, respectively. Ab initio molecular dynamics simulations at 400 K confirm the thermal stability of the metal-decorated frameworks and the suppression of metal aggregation. The vacancy-stabilized alkali-metal centers generate localized charge polarization that facilitates the adsorption of up to 20 H2 molecules per supercell, with average adsorption energies of -0.182 eV (Li), -0.191 eV (Na), and -0.171 eV (K), making the adsorption reversible under near-ambient conditions. The corresponding gravimetric H2 storage capacities reach 11.64, 9.82, and 8.49 wt percent, respectively, significantly exceeding the US Department of Energy (DOE) ultimate target of 6.50 wt percent. Moreover, thermodynamic analysis further confirms favorable adsorption-desorption behavior within practical operating windows. These results establish vacancy-defected light-metal decorated BeN2 as a viable design strategy for high-density, reversible H2 storage, providing a scalable framework for engineering polar lightweight materials for energy storage applications.

</details>


### [81] [Spontaneous Topological Locking and Symmetry Restoration of Meron Lattices in Synthetic Antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03755)
*Gülşen Doğan,Ümit Akıncı*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用大规模蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，揭示了合成反铁磁体（synthetic antiferromagnets）双层膜中meron-antimeron晶体的自发拓扑锁定（topological locking）与结构对称性恢复机制：超弱层间反铁磁交换耦合作为结构支架，强制垂直同步、恢复C₄旋转对称性，并在极端各向异性下维持局部拓扑锁定，为分数拓扑织构的稳定与操控提供了理论路线图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成反铁磁体（synthetic antiferromagnets, SAF）为稳定分数拓扑织构（fractional topological textures）提供了鲁棒平台，可有效规避铁磁系统的局限性。本文旨在探究SAF双层膜中meron-antimeron晶体的自发拓扑锁定与结构对称性恢复机制。

Method: 采用大规模蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，对具有易面磁各向异性（easy-plane magnetic anisotropy）的SAF双层膜体系进行数值研究。

Result: 在非耦合单层极限下，增大各向异性引发极端核心收缩效应（core-shrinking effect），物理上扩大芯间距离并触发C₄→C₂对称性破缺；引入超弱层间反铁磁交换（antiferromagnetic exchange）作为活性结构支架，对刚性晶体强制垂直同步，形成鲁棒的反铁磁bimeron偶极子（dipoles）并完全恢复宏观C₄旋转对称性；在高度膨胀的预坍缩晶体中观察到异常层间诱导晶格压缩，主动最大化交换能；在宏观晶序不可逆坍缩的极端各向异性极限下，双层耦合仍对存活的孤立缺陷强制严格的局部拓扑锁定。

Conclusion: 这些发现揭示了局部垂直同步（local vertical synchronization）与全局结构有序（global structural order）之间的基本退耦，为在超越斯格明子（beyond-skyrmion）自旋电子学架构中稳定和操控分数拓扑织构提供了全面的理论路线图。

Abstract: Synthetic antiferromagnets offer a robust platform for stabilizing fractional topological textures, effectively circumventing the limitations of ferromagnetic systems. In this study, we utilize large-scale Monte Carlo simulations to investigate the spontaneous topological locking and structural symmetry restoration of meron-antimeron crystals within SAF bilayers subjected to easy-plane magnetic anisotropy. In the uncoupled monolayer limit, increasing anisotropy induces an extreme core-shrinking effect that physically expands the inter-core distance and triggers a $C_4 \rightarrow C_2$ symmetry breaking. However, the introduction of an ultra-weak interlayer antiferromagnetic exchange acts as an active structural scaffold. For rigid crystals, this coupling strictly enforces vertical synchronization, forming robust antiferromagnetic bimeron dipoles and fully restoring the macroscopic $C_4$ rotational symmetry. Furthermore, in highly expanded, pre-collapse crystals, we observe an anomalous interlayer-induced lattice compression that actively maximizes the exchange energy. At extreme anisotropy limits where macroscopic crystalline order irrecoverably collapses, the bilayer coupling continues to enforce a strict local topological locking of surviving isolated defects. These findings reveal a fundamental decoupling between local vertical synchronization and global structural order, providing a comprehensive theoretical roadmap for stabilizing and manipulating fractional topological textures in beyond-skyrmion spintronic architectures.

</details>


### [82] [The high K anomaly in ScAlN explained](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03765)
*Ilan Shalish*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文解决了氮化钪铝（ScAlN）中介电响应长期存在的理论与实验不一致问题，指出实验观测到的"高介电常数（high K）"行为源于机电膨胀（electromechanical inflation）效应——极性异质结构中的巨大内电场通过逆压电效应诱导宏观晶格应变。通过施加无应力力学边界条件，推导出有效介电常数的解析关系 ε_eff = ε_33^S + e_33²/C_33，该模型定量解释了ScAlN合金范围内的实验数据，并界定了刚性晶格近似在强极性半导体中的根本极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，氮化钪铝（ScAlN）的介电响应存在理论与实验之间的显著不一致：刚性晶格的第一性原理计算预测介电常数约为11.7，而实验一致观测值接近15。本文旨在解决这一分歧，揭示该"高K"行为的物理机制。

Method: 通过将机电膨胀效应——极性异质结构中的巨大内电场经逆压电效应（inverse piezoelectric effect）诱导宏观晶格应变——引入耦合状态方程，并在无应力力学边界条件下推导出有效介电常数的解析表达式 ε_eff = ε_33^S + e_33²/C_33。

Result: 该模型定量解释了ScAlN合金范围内全部实验观测结果，并明确了刚性晶格近似在强极性半导体中的适用极限。

Conclusion: ScAlN中实验观测到的高介电常数并非材料本征性质，而是逆压电效应导致的机电膨胀现象；本文提出的解析框架为理解强极性半导体的介电行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We resolve the long-standing discrepancy between theoretical material constants and experimental observations of the dielectric response in scandium aluminum nitride (ScAlN). While first-principles calculations of the rigid lattice predict a permittivity of about 11.7, experiments consistently report values near 15. We demonstrate that this "high K" behavior is a manifestation of electromechanical inflation, where the enormous internal electric fields of polar heterostructures induce macroscopic lattice strain via the inverse piezoelectric effect. By applying stress-free mechanical boundary conditions to the coupled equations of state, we derive an analytical relation for the effective permittivity: epsilon_eff=epsilon_33^S + e_33^2/C_33. This model quantitatively accounts for experimental observations across the ScAlN alloy range and defines the fundamental limit of the rigid-lattice approximation in highly polar semiconductors.

</details>

*I. Artacho,I. Ramiro,A. Martí*

TL;DR: 本文报道了分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）生长的1×1 mm² InAs热辐射二极管（thermoradiative diodes），重点分析其反向饱和电流（reverse saturation current）和击穿电压（breakdown voltage）。在450°C生长温度、As₂通量约为化学计量比三倍、铟（In）喷射炉尖端温度高于基座温度150°C的条件下，器件实现了高于0.3 V的击穿电压和约为辐射极限（radiative limit）200倍的反向饱和电流密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究InAs热辐射二极管的反向饱和电流与击穿电压特性，以优化器件性能并理解其电流-电压（I-V）行为偏离辐射极限（radiative limit）的机制。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）技术生长InAs p-i-n二极管结构，生长温度为450°C，As₂通量约为化学计量比的三倍，In喷射炉尖端温度设定为高于基座温度150°C。

Result: 在最佳生长条件下，器件击穿电压高于0.3 V，反向饱和电流密度达到辐射极限（radiative limit）的200倍。

Conclusion: 特定的分子束外延生长条件（高温、富As₂气氛、In源尖端高温）可显著提升InAs热辐射二极管的击穿电压，同时反向饱和电流密度远超辐射极限。

Abstract: We describe the development of 1x1 mm2 InAs thermoradiative diodes grown by molecular beam epitaxy with emphasis on their reverse saturation current and break-down voltage. P-i-n diode structures grown at 450 C, with As2 flux around 3 times stoichiometry and an In effusion cell tip temperature 150 C higher than the base temperature, exhibit the best results with breakdown voltages above 0.3 V and reverse saturation current densities 200 times the radiative limit.

### [84] [Magneto Transport and Spin Reorientation in Pt Co78Ho22 Heterostructures Near the Sublattice Compensation Temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03982)
*Rajeev Nepal,Jose Flores,Aurain Seaton,Michael Newburger,John Derek Demaree,Ramesh C Budhani*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文实验研究了Co78Ho22Al薄膜及Pt/Co78Ho22Al异质结的异常霍尔电阻率、直流磁化和自旋霍尔磁电阻（SHMR），发现两类系统在补偿温度（Tcomp）附近均出现霍尔电阻率符号反转和翼状磁滞回线，且Pt层增强了SHMR，这些现象可通过自旋翻转转变、自旋轨道矩及微观相分离等理论加以解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钬（Ho）在镧系元素中拥有最大的轨道角动量（OAM），但其在3d-4f铁磁体系中的磁输运行为研究仍相对不足；本文旨在填补这一空白，探究Ho基非晶铁磁薄膜及其异质结中的磁输运特性。

Method: 采用多靶磁控溅射（multitarget magnetron sputtering）制备Co78Ho22Al薄膜及Pt/Co78Ho22Al异质结，并测量其异常霍尔电阻率、直流磁化强度以及自旋霍尔磁电阻（SHMR）。

Result: 两类系统在补偿温度（Tcomp）附近均观察到霍尔电阻率的符号反转（sign reversal）和翼状磁滞回线，同时饱和磁化强度在Tcomp附近达到最小值；Pt层的引入使SHMR增强。

Conclusion: Ho基非晶铁磁薄膜中靠近补偿温度的磁输运反常现象可由自旋翻转转变（spin flop transition）、自旋轨道矩（spin orbit torque）及微观相分离（microscopic phase separation）理论解释，后者可能导致薄膜中形成3d和4f磁性团簇。

Abstract: Metallic amorphous ferrimagnets of 3d transition metals (TM) and rare earths (RE) with 4f electrons exhibit rich magneto transport behavior due to the interplay between the 3d and 4f magnetic sublattices and their interaction with mobile charges. Tuning the TM and RE concentrations in the alloy can effectively modulate the compensation temperature, where the moments of the two sublattices point in opposite direction leading to a net zero magnetization. Despite extensive magnetotransport studies in Gd and Tb based 3d 4f systems, Ho based alloys remain comparatively underexplored, even though Ho possesses the largest orbital angular momentum (OAM) among the lanthanides. This unquenched OAM can strongly impact magnetic anisotropy and magnetotransport in ferrimagnetic heterostructures. Here, we have investigated the anomalous Hall resistivity , dc magnetization, and spin Hall magnetoresistance (SHMR) of Co78Ho22.Al film and a Pt.Co78Ho22.Al heterostructure deposited using multitarget magnetron sputtering. The Hall resistivity of both systems shows a distinct sign reversal and prominent wing-shaped hysteresis loops in the vicinity of the compensation temperature (Tcomp), which is accompanied by the minimum saturation magnetization near Tcomp. Furthermore, the SHMR in Pt.Co78Ho22.Al film is enhanced due to the Pt layer. These HM interface-induced prominent features of magneto-transport are addressed in the light of the existing theories of spin flop transitions, spin orbit torque, and microscopic phase separation, which may lead to the formation of 3d and 4f magnetic clusters in the film.

</details>

### [85] [Non-Markovian entropy production fluctuation theorem driven by a time-dependent electric field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03191)
*K. S. Rodríguez-Vigil,M. A. Bastarrachea-Magnani,J. I. Jiménez-Aquino*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 利用广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equation）研究带电粒子在谐振势（harmonic potential）与含时电场作用下扩散过程的非马尔可夫熵产生涨落定理（non-Markovian entropy production fluctuation theorem），证明Kubo第二涨落-耗散定理（Kubo's second fluctuation-dissipation theorem, FDT）保持不变，并基于此验证了总熵产生（total entropy production）的细致涨落定理（detailed fluctuation theorem, DFT）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涨落定理（fluctuation theorems）是理解小系统非平衡热力学（non-equilibrium thermodynamics）基础与应用层面的关键工具，本研究旨在将其推广至非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）扩散过程。

Method: 采用广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equation）建模带电粒子在气体中、谐振势内、受含时电场作用的扩散过程；利用Kubo第二涨落-耗散定理（Kubo's second FDT）推导位置的高斯概率密度（Gaussian probability density），进而验证细致涨落定理（DFT）在总熵产生（total entropy production）上的成立性；并以Ornstein-Uhlenbeck型摩擦记忆核（friction memory kernel）与振荡电场为例进行数值分析。

Result: 电场对标记布朗粒子（tagged Brownian particle）与浴粒子（bath particles）的共同影响产生了一种“诱导”电动力（induced electric force），但Kubo第二涨落-耗散定理（FDT）在该情形下保持不变；基于FDT得到的位置高斯概率密度为证明总熵产生的细致涨落定理（DFT）提供了关键条件。

Conclusion: 在非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）背景下，总熵产生的细致涨落定理（DFT）依然成立；在Ornstein-Uhlenbeck型摩擦记忆核与振荡电场条件下，可进一步分析不同参数区域中的平均功（average work）与熵产生（entropy production）行为。

Abstract: Fluctuation theorems are key to understanding both fundamental and applied aspects of non-equilibrium thermodynamics of small systems. We study the non-Markovian entropy production fluctuation theorem for the diffusion process of charged particles in a gas inside a harmonic potential and under the action of a time-dependent electric field, using a generalized Langevin equation. By considering the influence of the electric field on both the tagged Brownian particle and the bath particles, an "induced" electric force arises. Despite the additional force, we demonstrate that Kubo's second fluctuation-dissipation theorem (FDT) remains unchanged. The FDT allows us to obtain the Gaussian probability density for the position along a single stochastic trajectory, which is the key to demonstrating the validity of the detailed fluctuation theorem (DFT) for the total entropy production. We study the specific result of an Ornstein-Uhlenbeck-type friction memory kernel and an oscillating electric field, and analyze the average work and entropy production in different parameter regimes.

</details>


### [86] [Universal criticality of entropy production in chemical reaction networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03192)
*Kyota Tamano,Keiji Saito*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究通过质量作用动力学（mass-action dynamics）局部分岔（local bifurcations）框架，分类了宏观非平衡相变中熵产生涨落与响应的临界标度指数，并推导出通用标度不等式 α - 2β ≥ 0，揭示熵产生涨落是检测非平衡临界性更灵敏的探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）已为微观熵产生（entropy production）建立普适关系，但宏观非平衡相变中的临界行为尚未被系统分类，亟需统一的理论框架。

Method: 采用线性噪声公式（linear-noise formulas）、中心流形规范型（center-manifold normal forms）与Floquet理论（Floquet theory），分析完全混合可逆化学反应网络在宏观极限下的叉形分岔（pitchfork）、跨临界分岔（transcritical）、鞍结分岔（saddle-node）及Hopf分岔（Hopf bifurcation）；并利用轨迹空间Cramér-Rao型界（trajectory-space Cramér-Rao type bound）推导标度不等式。

Result: 获得了上述四种局部分岔类型下熵产生涨落与响应的通用临界指数（generic exponents），并证明标度关系 α - 2β ≥ 0 成立，表明发散响应必然伴随发散涨落，反之则不一定。

Conclusion: 熵产生涨落比响应函数更灵敏地刻画非平衡临界性（nonequilibrium criticality），为宏观非平衡相变的普适分类提供了新判据。

Abstract: Stochastic thermodynamics gives universal relations for microscopic entropy production, yet its critical behavior at macroscopic nonequilibrium transitions remains unclassified. We study well-mixed reversible chemical reaction networks in the macroscopic-first limit, where transitions arise as local bifurcations of mass-action dynamics. Using linear-noise formulas, center-manifold normal forms, and Floquet theory, we obtain generic exponents for entropy-production fluctuations and responses at pitchfork, transcritical, saddle-node, and Hopf bifurcations. Beyond this low-order classification, a trajectory-space Cramér-Rao type bound yields the universal scaling inequality $α- 2β\geq 0$. Hence divergent responses require divergent fluctuations, but not conversely, making entropy-production fluctuations a sharper probe of nonequilibrium criticality.

</details>


### [87] [From Enhanced Sampling to Human-Readable Representations of Protein Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03394)
*Souvik Mondal,Michael A. Sauer,Matthias Heyden*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种全自动框架，将增强采样（enhanced sampling）轨迹转化为人类可读的蛋白质动态表示。该方法结合频率选择性非简谐模式分析（frequency-selective anharmonic mode analysis）导出的集体变量（collective variables, CVs）与加权动态互相关矩阵（weighted dynamic cross-correlation matrices）的后验分析，识别残基对和结构域的关联/反关联运动，提炼出物理可解释的域-域距离作为新CVs。在KRAS和HIV-1蛋白酶等五个蛋白质上的应用表明，该方法无需先验系统知识即可识别生物学相关结构域和运动，生成的低统计不确定性的自由能面（free energy surfaces）能够复现已知构象态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蛋白质构象动力学（protein conformational dynamics）的理解对于阐明生物功能至关重要，但由于涉及广泛的时标和复杂的集体运动，传统分子动力学（molecular dynamics）受限于时标问题。增强采样方法虽能克服时标限制，但其有效性依赖于集体变量（CVs）的选择，而CVs常难以定义且缺乏物理可解释性。特别是机器学习和集体振动模式导出的CVs虽能捕捉慢动力学，但难以映射到直观的结构描述符上。

Method: 该方法是一个全自动框架，包含两个阶段：首先，沿频率选择性非简谐模式分析导出的CVs进行增强采样；其次，对偏置轨迹进行后验分析，利用加权动态互相关矩阵识别表现出协同和反协同运动的残基对与结构域，从中提炼出简单的域-域距离作为物理可解释的CVs。该框架在包括KRAS和HIV-1蛋白酶在内的五个蛋白质上进行了验证。

Result: 该方法能够一致地识别生物学相关的结构域和运动，无需先验的体系特定知识。将轨迹投影到这些域-域距离上得到的自由能面，在保持低统计不确定性的同时，能够复现已知的构象态，并最大化独立动态信息。复杂CVs被系统性地转化为简单的几何描述符，且不损失本质动力学信息。

Conclusion: 该框架的通用性和自动化特性使其可广泛应用于增强采样模拟的解读，能够生成可解释的构象系综（conformational ensembles），便于与新兴的机器学习方法集成。

Abstract: Understanding protein conformational dynamics is essential for elucidating biological function but remains challenging due to the wide range of timescales and the complexity of collective motions. Enhanced sampling methods overcome timescale limitations of conventional molecular dynamics, yet their effectiveness depends on the choice of collective variables (CVs), which are often difficult to define and may lack physical interpretability. In particular, collective variables derived from machine learning or collective vibrational modes can efficiently capture slow dynamics but are not easily mapped onto intuitive structural descriptors. Here, we present a fully automated framework that transforms enhanced sampling trajectories into human-readable representations of protein dynamics. Our approach combines enhanced sampling along CVs derived from frequency-selective anharmonic mode analysis with a post hoc analysis of biased trajectories using weighted dynamic cross-correlation matrices. From these, we identify residue pairs and domains exhibiting correlated and anti-correlated motions, yielding simple domain-domain distances that serve as physically interpretable CVs. We apply this method to five proteins, including KRAS and HIV-1 protease, and show that it consistently identifies biologically relevant domains and motions without prior system-specific knowledge. Projection onto these distances produces free energy surfaces that reproduce known conformational states with low statistical uncertainty while maximizing independent dynamical information. This workflow enables systematic recasting of complex CVs into simple geometric descriptors without loss of essential dynamics. Its generality and automation make it broadly applicable for interpreting enhanced sampling simulations and generating interpretable conformational ensembles for integration with emerging machine learning approaches.

</details>


### [88] [Optimal Navigation in Stochastic and Disordered Gridworlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03568)
*Kévin Bilaï Biloa,Olivier Pierre-Louis*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究通过动态规划（dynamic programming）计算布朗粒子（Brownian particle）在无序能量景观（disordered energy landscape）中的最优导航策略，并引入基于Kullback-Leibler散度的策略变更密度（density of change）来量化无序的影响。结果表明，策略变更在陷阱浓度上呈现非单调依赖，且在弱偏置的涨落主导区域，最大值意外出现在低陷阱浓度处。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序环境下的最优导航问题在生物学和工程学等领域具有关键意义，但现有数值优化方法未能深入揭示无序如何重塑最优导航策略。本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 研究将无序能量景观建模为具有随机分布陷阱的晶格（lattice），采用动态规划（dynamic programming）计算使平均首达时间（mean first-passage time）最小化的最优导航策略，并引入基于Kullback-Leibler散度（Kullback-Leibler divergence）的策略变更密度来量化无序的影响。

Result: 最优策略的变更随陷阱浓度呈现非单调依赖，并在某一浓度处出现显著最大值。在涨落主导（fluctuation-dominated）的弱偏置区域，策略变更密度存在解析表达式，且最大值出现在低陷阱浓度条件下。

Conclusion: 无序对最优导航策略的影响并非简单的单调变化，而是在低浓度下出现意外峰值，这表明即使少量的无序也能显著改变最优导航行为。

Abstract: Navigation in complex and noisy environments is a key issue in diverse fields from biology to engineering. Despite extensive progress in numerical optimization methods for computing navigation policies, insights into how disorder reshapes optimal navigation remain elusive. To address this question, we investigate the navigation of a Brownian particle in a disordered energy landscape, modeled as a lattice with randomly distributed traps. Using dynamic programming, we compute the optimal navigation policies that minimize the mean first-passage time to a target site. To quantify the impact of disorder, we introduce a density of change from a Kullback-Leibler divergence, which captures how the optimal policy is reshaped by either the presence of disorder or the knowledge of its configuration. Our results reveal a non-monotonic dependence of the change of the policy on trap concentration, with a pronounced maximum. In the fluctuation-dominated regime where the navigation bias is weak, we derive an analytical expression for the density of change, and demonstrate that the maximum occurs unexpectedly at low trap concentrations.

</details>


### [89] [Information-Geometric Signatures of Nonconservative Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03757)
*Andrea Auconi,Sosuke Ito*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于信息几何（information geometry）的非保守驱动（nonconservative driving）特征量，利用Kullback–Leibler散度（KL散度）和Fisher信息（Fisher information）检测细致平衡（detailed balance）的破坏。对于满足细致平衡的马尔可夫跳跃过程（Markov jump processes），在近平衡态下，KL散度相对于平衡态的加速度等于Fisher信息的两倍；而对于弛豫到非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady state）的过程，即使在稳态附近该关系也普遍被违反。本文将这种偏差定义为弛豫间隙（relaxation gap），并推导了稳态熵产生率（steady-state entropy production rate）的下界，该下界在具有简单循环拓扑的网络中尤为紧致。类似的关系和界限同样适用于Fokker–Planck动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非保守驱动（nonconservative driving）是远离平衡态系统的重要特征，但缺乏一种基于信息几何的、可直接检测细致平衡破坏程度的通用几何特征量。本文旨在填补这一空白，利用KL散度和Fisher信息构建一种新的信息几何签名（information-geometric signature）。

Method: 论文从信息几何视角出发，针对马尔可夫跳跃过程（Markov jump processes）和Fokker–Planck动力学，分析了KL散度的时间行为与Fisher信息之间的关系。通过比较满足细致平衡与不满足细致平衡两种情况下的关系差异，定义了弛豫间隙（relaxation gap），并将其与稳态熵产生率（steady-state entropy production rate）建立联系，推导出下界。

Result: 在满足细致平衡且近平衡的条件下，KL散度相对于平衡态的加速度等于两倍Fisher信息（时间导数形式）。对于弛豫到非平衡稳态的过程，即使在稳态附近该关系也被违反。基于这一偏差定义的弛豫间隙，可以推导出稳态熵产生率的下界，该下界在简单循环拓扑网络中特别紧致。同样的结论对Fokker–Planck动力学也成立。

Conclusion: 本文提出的信息几何签名（information-geometric signature）能够有效检测非平衡驱动力导致的细致平衡破坏。弛豫间隙（relaxation gap）与稳态熵产生率之间的下界关系为量化非平衡系统的不可逆性提供了新的理论工具，尤其适用于具有简单循环拓扑结构的网络系统。

Abstract: We propose an information-geometric signature of nonconservative driving that detects violations of detailed balance using the Kullback--Leibler divergence and the Fisher information. For Markov jump processes satisfying detailed balance, we show that, near equilibrium, the acceleration of the Kullback--Leibler divergence relative to the equilibrium state is given by twice the Fisher information with respect to time. In contrast, for relaxation toward a nonequilibrium steady state, this relation is generally violated even near the steady state. We refer to the resulting discrepancy as the relaxation gap and derive a lower bound on the steady-state entropy production rate in terms of this gap. We demonstrate that this bound is particularly tight for networks with simple cyclic topologies. Finally, we show that analogous relations and bounds hold for Fokker--Planck dynamics.

</details>

### [90] [Chiral Symmetry and Its Restoration in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27982)
*Teiji Kunihiro*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文系统梳理了手征对称性（chiral symmetry）在量子色动力学（QCD）物质中的角色，从π介子的赝标量特性出发，依次讨论了手征对称性自发破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）、Nambu-Goldstone定理、U(1)A反常、多种手征夸克模型（chiral quark models）以及核子奇偶双重态模型（parity-doublet model），并介绍了在热/密核物质中探索手征对称性恢复（chiral restoration）的相关实验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 借助狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）引入手征性（chirality）概念，类比Bogoliubov-Valatin超导理论说明有质量狄拉克场中手征性的混合；通过Nambu-Jona-Lasinio型手征夸克模型、含行列式项的三味线性sigma模型以及核子奇偶双重态模型进行理论构建。

Result: 阐述了U(1)A反常（U(1)A anomaly）及其物理后果，分析了η'介子质量项的起源；基于Hellmann-Feynman定理给出了手征凝聚（chiral condensate）可能降低的直观解释；报告了当前构建包含奇偶双重态和手征对称性恢复的核物质及中子星物质状态方程（equation of state）的努力。

Conclusion: 手征对称性的恢复是理解高温/高密QCD物质的关键，相关实验（如π介子原子、相对论性重离子碰撞中的轻子对产生、η'介子核尝试）正在探索这一过程。

Abstract: We first note the peculiar property of the pion as the pseudoscalar particle, which play the essential role in realizing the basic properties of the nuclear matter such as the density/energy saturations. Then,
  we introduce the notion of chirality using the Dirac equation, and show how chiralities are
  mixed in the massive Dirac field with an emphasis on the similarity with the Bogoliubov-Valatin theory of superconductivity. After noting the approximate chiral symmetry in QCD in the light quark sector,
  we introduce the notion of the spontaneous symmetry breaking,
  and the Nambu-Goldstone theorem. A remark is given on the U(1)$_A$ anomaly and its physical consequences. Several chiral quark models of the Nambu-Jona-Lasinio type are introduced with an emphasis to the relevance to QCD, and discuss some consequences of the models. A three-flavor linear sigma model with the determinant term is examined, and discuss the origin of the mass term of the $η'$ meson. A parity-doublet model for nucleons is introduced, and the current active effort is described to construct the equation of state of nuclear and neutron-star matter incorporating the parity-doubling in the baryon sector and the occurrence of the restoration of chiral symmetry in the QCD matter. An intuitive account is given on how the chiral condensate may be reduced on the basis of Hellmann-Feynman theorem. We describe some experiments to explore the chiral restoration in hot and/or dense medium, such as the pionic atoms, lepton-pair production in relativistic-heavy-ion collisions, an attempt to produce $η'$-mesonic nuclei, and so on.

### [91] [Chiral symmetry breaking and inhomogeneous phases in thermal anti-de Sitter spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03118)
*Sergio Morales-Tejera*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文利用夸克-介子模型（quark-meson model）研究有限温度反德西特（AdS）时空中手征对称性的自发破缺。通过分析微分间隙方程（differential gap equation），发现AdS中凝聚σ通常是非均匀的，且边界值问题的解具有唯一性。手征对称性在靠近AdS边界处始终被破坏。相图显示，温度倾向于恢复手征对称性，而负曲率（negative curvature）则促进其自发破缺。同时考虑了霍金-佩奇相变（Hawking-Page phase transition）对相图的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索弯曲时空（尤其是负曲率AdS背景）中手征对称性破缺的行为，以及温度与时空曲率对手征对称性恢复或破缺的竞争机制。

Method: 采用夸克-介子模型在有限温度AdS时空中研究手征对称性自发破缺；通过微分间隙方程求解非均匀凝聚σ，并分析正则解（regular solution）的边界值问题。

Result: 正则解中不存在自由积分常数，边界值问题的解具有唯一性；手征对称性在AdS边界附近始终破缺；构建了以AdS曲率和温度为变量的相图，发现温度与负曲率对手征对称性具有相反的作用；考虑霍金-佩奇相变后相图发生修正。

Conclusion: 温度倾向于恢复手征对称性，而负曲率则促进其自发破缺；霍金-佩奇相变会对上述相图产生修正影响。

Abstract: We study the spontaneous breaking of chiral symmetry in an AdS spacetime at finite temperature using the quark-meson model. The condensate $σ$ is typically inhomogeneous in AdS and is determined from the differential gap equation. We demonstrate that there are no free integration constants in the regular solutions to the differential equation and find that the solution to the boundary value problem is unique. We find that chiral symmetry is always broken close to the AdS boundary. We construct the phase diagram of the system as a function of the AdS curvature and temperature. These two parameters have opposing effects: temperature tends to restore chiral symmetry, whereas negative curvature favors its spontaneous breaking. We also consider how the phase diagram is modified when the Hawking-Page phase transition is taken into account.

</details>

### [92] [Epistatic strength, modularity, and locus heterogeneity shape the number of local optima in fitness landscapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03046)
*Mahan Ghafari,Alejandro Castro Cabrera,Alejandro Lage-Castellanos,Guillaume Achaz,Joachim Krug,Luca Ferretti*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本文通过各向同性高斯随机场（isotropic Gaussian random fields）揭示：非结构化适应度景观（fitness landscapes）中局部最优峰（local optima）的预期数量由单一局部上位性（epistasis）度量——适应度效应相关性（correlation of fitness effects）决定；当上位性相互作用具有结构时，如模块化聚类或位点间异质性，峰的数量会相应增加或急剧减少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 适应度景观中局部最优峰的数量决定了进化能否朝向全局最优（global optimum）前进或困于次优峰（suboptimal peaks）。尽管已知多峰现象需要互惠符号上位性（reciprocal sign epistasis），但上位性与峰数量之间的定量关系尚未完全阐明。

Method: 研究采用各向同性高斯随机场（isotropic Gaussian random fields）作为一类广泛非结构化适应度景观的数学模型，推导局部最优峰的预期数量与上位性局部度量之间的解析关系。进一步通过结构化上位性相互作用，分别考察模块化聚类（clustering interactions within blocks of loci）和位点间强异质性（strong heterogeneity between loci）对峰数的影响。

Result: 非结构化景观中预期局部最优峰数量由适应度效应相关性（correlation of fitness effects）单一确定，建立了峰密度与互惠符号上位性之间的直接基线预测。模块化聚类略微增加局部最优峰数量，而位点间强异质性（仅少数位点参与上位性相互作用）导致峰数量急剧下降。

Conclusion: 局部最优峰的数量不仅受上位性的整体强度（overall strength of epistasis）调控，还取决于上位性相互作用在基因型空间（genotype space）中的分布方式。该框架调和了互惠符号上位性的核心作用与具有相似上位性程度的景观可能呈现截然不同粗糙度（ruggedness）这一观察，并为预期典型景观中的峰数范围提供了指导。

Abstract: Fitness landscapes provide a quantitative framework for understanding how natural selection shapes evolutionary trajectories. A central feature of these landscapes is their number of local optima, which determines whether fitness-increasing evolution can proceed towards a global optimum or become trapped on suboptimal peaks. Although multiple peaks are known to require reciprocal sign epistasis, the quantitative relationship between epistasis and number of peaks remains incompletely understood. Here, we show that for a broad class of unstructured fitness landscapes, i.e. isotropic Gaussian random fields, the expected number of local optima is determined by a single local measure of epistasis: the correlation of fitness effects. This provides a baseline prediction for the number of peaks in typical unstructured landscapes and links peak density directly to the amount of reciprocal sign epistasis. This baseline changes when epistatic interactions are structured. We show that clustering interactions within blocks of loci slightly increases the number of local optima. In contrast, strong heterogeneity between loci, where only a small subset of loci participate in epistatic interactions, causes the number of peaks to collapse. These results show that the number of local optima is governed not only by the overall strength of epistasis, but also by how epistatic interactions are distributed across the genotype space. Our framework therefore reconciles the central role of reciprocal sign epistasis with the observation that landscapes with similar amounts of epistasis can differ substantially in ruggedness, and provides a guide to the range of peak numbers expected in typical landscapes.

</details>

### [93] [Parafermionic and decoupled multicritical points in a frustrated $\mathbb{Z}_6$ clock chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03001)
*Andrea Kouta Dagnino,Attila Szabó*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种广义的六态钟模型（generalised six-state clock chain），该模型通过一个由退耦伊辛模型（Ising model）和三态波茨模型（three-state Potts model）描述的多临界点（multicritical point），在钟模型（clock model）与波茨模型（Potts model）之间进行插值。研究表明这种退耦会延伸至仅破缺 ℤ₂ 或 ℤ₃ 对称性的稳定相中，并利用边界共形场论（boundary CFT）分析和能级谱学（level spectroscopy）明确识别出终结钟模型Luttinger液体相（Luttinger-liquid phase）的 ℤ₆  parafermion多临界点。该工作表明parafermion可以远离可积性（integrability）出现，即使在伊辛序与三态波茨序相互交织的系统中也是如此。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索钟模型与波茨模型之间的连续插值过程，并揭示其中由退耦伊辛模型与三态波茨模型描述的多临界点及其延伸的稳定相；同时希望识别并确认钟模型Luttinger液体相的终结多临界点，以验证parafermion是否能在远离可积性的系统中涌现。

Method: 引入一种广义六态钟模型（generalised six-state clock chain），通过调节参数在钟模型与波茨模型之间插值；采用边界共形场论（boundary CFT）分析与能级谱学（level spectroscopy）方法识别多临界点的性质。

Result: 发现了由退耦伊辛模型和三态波茨模型描述的多临界点，且该退耦效应延伸至仅破缺 ℤ₂ 或 ℤ₃ 对称性的稳定相中；通过边界CFT和能级谱学分析，明确识别出一个 ℤ₆  parafermion多临界点，该点终结了钟模型的Luttinger液体相。

Conclusion: parafermion可以在远离可积性（integrability）的系统中涌现，即使在伊辛序与三态波茨序相互交织的情况下也不例外。

Abstract: We introduce a generalised six-state clock chain that interpolates between the clock and Potts models via a multicritical point described by decoupled Ising and three-state Potts models. We find that this decoupling extends into stable phases that break only $\mathbb{Z}_2$ or $\mathbb{Z}_3$ symmetry. We also use boundary CFT analysis and level spectroscopy to conclusively identify a $\mathbb{Z}_6$ parafermion multicritical point terminating the clock model Luttinger-liquid phase. Our work shows that parafermions emerge far from integrability, even in systems with intertwined Ising and three-state Potts orders.

### [94] [Universal Theory of Incoherent Metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03013)
*Aaron Kleger,Nikolay Gnezdilov,Rufus Boyack*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用二维Yukawa-SYK模型（一种费米子与量子临界玻色子具有空间随机耦合的模型），以非微扰方式研究非相干金属的输运性质，成功解释了高温超导体中费米液体理论无法描述的多种反常现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜氧化物、重费米子和扭曲双层石墨烯等非常规超导体在超导临界温度以上表现出非相干金属输运行为，这一现象无法用费米液体理论（Fermi-liquid theory）描述，对理论物理学提出了重大挑战。

Method: 采用二维Yukawa-SYK模型，其中费米子（fermions）与量子临界玻色子（quantum-critical bosons）之间存在空间随机耦合，以非微扰（non-perturbative）方式在耦合强度上研究输运行为。

Result: 该模型提供了一个量子临界非相干金属（quantum-critical incoherent metals）的微观模型，再现了其伴随的多种性质：电阻率与准粒子寿命之间的非玻尔兹曼输运公式（non-Boltzmann transport formula）、莫特-伊夫-雷格尔电阻率界限（Mott-Ioffe-Regel resistivity bound）的违反，以及科夫通-孙-斯塔里内茨剪切粘度与熵密度界限（Kovtun-Son-Starinets shear viscosity to entropy density bound）的违反。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解非常规超导体中量子临界区域的非相干金属输运现象提供了一个微观理论基础，并揭示了超越传统输运理论框架的新物理机制。

Abstract: Numerous unconventional superconductors such as cuprates, heavy-fermions, and twisted-bilayer graphene exhibit incoherent metallic transport above the superconducting critical temperature. This phenomenon cannot be described with Fermi-liquid theory and has presented a significant theoretical challenge to overcome. We utilize the two-dimensional Yukawa-SYK model of fermions with spatially random coupling to quantum-critical bosons to study transport in a manner which is non-perturbative in the coupling strength. Our work provides a microscopic model of quantum-critical incoherent metals and their concomitant properties, including a non-Boltzmann transport formula between resistivity and quasi-particle lifetime, violation of the Mott-Ioffe-Regel resistivity bound, and violation of the Kovtun-Son-Starinets shear viscosity to entropy density bound.

</details>

Abstract: Orbitally degenerate systems provide a promising platform for realizing novel quantum phases driven by spin-orbital exchange interactions, as described by the Kugel-Khomskii model. Here, we combine first-principles calculations with an effective spin-orbital model to address this problem. Using a model that retains only center-of-mass and valley degrees-of-freedom, we find that electrostatic potentials can drive optical valley splitting up to 10meVs and induce valley selective exciton dispersion. For the $1$-parameter family, we show that the $em$-exchange defect is pumped into the bond Hilbert space of a tensor-network representation. Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过中子散射实验解析了常压镍基超导母体相La3Ni2O7的单晶自旋序与自旋动力学，发现其自旋激发呈现约5 meV的自旋隙（spin gap）、各向异性的面内色散以及双层周期性的面外调制，证实了反铁磁层间耦合。通过与双层海森伯模型（bilayer Heisenberg Hamiltonian）对比，确定了条状磁序（stripe-type magnetic order）中的强层间交换与竞争性面内耦合。尽管其自旋波带宽仅为铜氧化物超导体（cuprates）的约25%，但局域动态磁化率显著增强，总波动磁矩相当，表明中能量自旋激发源于强电子关联，构成了区别于铜氧化物超导体的独特磁学框架，对该体系超导电性的理解具有直接意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用中子散射（neutron scattering）技术，对单晶La3Ni2O7样品进行测量，解析其自旋序（spin order）与自旋动力学（spin dynamics）特征。同时利用双层海森伯哈密顿量（bilayer Heisenberg Hamiltonian）对色散关系进行理论拟合。

Result: 在Q = (0, 0.5, 2.5)处观测到清晰的自旋激发，具有约5 meV的自旋隙（spin gap）和各向异性的面内色散，横向方向出现区边界软化（zone-boundary softening），表明存在竞争的交换相互作用。激发呈现出双层周期性的显著面外调制，直接证实了反铁磁层间耦合（antiferromagnetic interlayer coupling）。谱归一化显示，尽管自旋波带宽仅为铜氧化物超导体的约25%，但局域动态磁化率显著增强，总波动磁矩大小相当。

Conclusion: 中能量自旋激发源于显著的电子关联（electronic correlations），构成该家族区别于铜氧化物超导体的关键磁学特征，为该体系中超导电性的理解提供了直接相关的磁性框架。

Abstract: The recent discovery of high-temperature superconductivity in pressurized and thin film nickelates has generated intense interest, yet the nature of magnetism in their ambient-pressure parent phases remains poorly understood, despite its potentially crucial role in pairing. Here we use neutron scattering to resolve the spin order and dynamics of single-crystalline La3Ni2O7, an ambient-pressure parent of this class. Well defined spin excitations are observed at Q = (0, 0.5, 2.5), featuring a~5 meV spin gap and anisotropic in-plane dispersions, with zone-boundary softening along the transverse direction indicative of competing exchange interactions. The excitations exhibit pronounced out-of-plane modulations with bilayer periodicity, providing direct evidence for antiferromagnetic interlayer coupling. Their dispersion is well described by a bilayer Heisenberg Hamiltonian with strong interlayer exchange and competing in-plane couplings within a stripe-type magnetic order. Normalization of the spectra to absolute units reveals that, although the spin-wave bandwidth is only about 25% of that in cuprates, the local dynamic susceptibility at comparable energies is significantly enhanced, yielding a total fluctuating moment of comparable magnitude. These results highlight intense mid-energy spin excitations rooted in substantial electronic correlations as a defining feature of this family, establishing a magnetic framework distinct from cuprates and directly relevant to understanding superconductivity in this system.

Abstract: The intriguing physics and rich application potential of strongly correlated first-row transition metal oxide compounds result from the complex interplay of several factors that influence the electronic structure. ### [100] [Renormalization group analysis for bosonization coefficients in half-odd-integer Kitaev spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03582)
*Jianxun Li,Chao Xu,Wang Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于重整化群（RG）分析，研究了自旋-S（S为半奇整数）Kitaev-Gamma链与Kitaev-Heisenberg-Gamma链在(K<0, Gamma>0, J>0)参数区域的玻色化公式。研究发现，玻色化公式中涌现连续对称性破缺的效应在大量子数极限下按1/S标度，与DMRG数值结果定性一致；同时，对称性分析揭示了十个独立的玻色化系数，其中五个在RG分析下预计不依赖于Heisenberg耦合（至线性阶）。该工作为准一维方法确定二维Kitaev自旋模型中的磁有序倾向提供了有价值的输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用重整化群（renormalization group, RG）分析研究玻色化公式；结合对称性分析（symmetry analysis）提取玻色化系数；通过密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）数值计算进行定性验证。

Result: 在(K<0, Gamma>0, J>0)参数区域，玻色化公式中涌现连续对称性破缺的效应在大量子数极限下以1/S标度衰减，与DMRG结果定性一致；Kitaev-Heisenberg-Gamma链存在十个独立的玻色化系数，其中五个在RG分析下至线性阶不依赖于Heisenberg耦合。

Conclusion: 该工作为准一维（quasi-one-dimensional）方法理解二维Kitaev自旋模型中的磁有序倾向提供了有价值的理论输入。

Abstract: Based on a renormalization group (RG) analysis, we study the bosonization formulas in spin-S Kitaev-Gamma and Kitaev-Heisenberg-Gamma chains in the (K < 0, Gamma > 0, J > 0) parameter region, where S is a half-odd integer. We find that the effects associated with the breaking of emergent continuous symmetries in bosonization formulas scale as 1/S in the large-S limit, which is in qualitative agreement with DMRG numerical results for Kitaev-Gamma chains. In Kitaev-Heisenberg-Gamma chains, symmetry analysis reveals ten independent bosonization coefficients, five of which are predicted by the RG analysis to have no dependence on the Heisenberg coupling up to linear order. Our work may offer valuable input for determining magnetic ordering tendencies in two-dimensional Kitaev spin models within a quasi-one-dimensional approach.

### [101] [Numerical evidence of a critical point in the (2+1)D SO(5) nonlinear sigma model with Wess-Zumino-Witten term](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03700)
*Yuan Da Liao,Bin-Bin Chen,Fakher F. Assaad,Lukas Janssen,Zi Yang Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种优化的连续场量子蒙特卡洛（QMC）算法，将计算复杂度降至 O(βN_q N_φ²)，从而能够模拟尺寸远超前人工作的 SO(5) 非线性 sigma 模型（含 Wess-Zumino-Witten 项），并在其相图中识别出一个多临界点，解决了该模型全局结构的长期悬而未决的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究含 Wess-Zumino-Witten（WZW）项的 SO(5) 非线性 sigma 模型（nonlinear sigma model），该模型描述 2+1 维时空中的半填充狄拉克费米子（如石墨烯）及其与五重态质量项的 Yukawa 耦合。此前工作在系统尺寸上受限，且该模型相图的全局结构（global structure）存在长期未解的问题。

Method: 采用优化的连续场量子蒙特卡洛（continuous-field quantum Monte Carlo, QMC）算法，通过将理论投影到最低朗道能级（lowest Landau level）进行正则化，在球面（sphere）和环面（torus）两种几何上实现模拟。算法复杂度降至 O(βN_q N_φ²)，相比前人工作[1-3]获得了 N_φ（磁通数，即系统尺寸）量级的加速。

Result: 在环面上实现 N_φ=140、球面上实现 N_φ=49 的系统尺寸，远超此前可达到的最大规模。绘制了两种几何下的普适相图，识别出一个将 SO(5) 对称性破缺有序相与 SO(5) 对称无序相分开的临界点（critical point）；该临界点在引入将 SO(5) 对称性破缺至 U(1)×SU(2) 的项时成为多临界点（multicritical point），与量子磁体中 Néel 反铁磁序与价键固体序之间的退禁闭相变相关。

Conclusion: SO(5) 非线性 sigma 模型（含 WZW 项）相图中多临界点的发现解决了其全局结构的长期开放性问题。所提出的 QMC 框架为投影哈密顿量（projected Hamiltonians）的系统研究（从关联平带到分数量子反常霍尔系统）开辟了新途径。无序相在热力学极限下的确切性质仍有待确定，但论证其既非共形（conformal）也非平凡带隙，类似于具有小能隙的手性量子自旋液体（chiral quantum spin liquid）。

Abstract: We develop an optimized continuous-field quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) algorithm to investigate the SO(5) nonlinear sigma model with a Wess-Zumino-Witten term, which describes half-filled Dirac fermions in 2+1 space-time dimensions akin to graphene and Yukawa coupled to a quintuplet of compatible mass terms. To regularize the theory, we project onto the lowest Landau level for both spherical and torus geometries. Our algorithm reduces the computational complexity to $O(βN_{\mathbf{q}} N_φ^2)$, yielding a speedup of a factor of $N_φ$ (the number of magnetic fluxes, i.e., system size) relative to prior works [1-3]. This advance enables us to simulate system sizes up to $N_φ=140$ on torus and $N_φ=49$ on sphere, far exceeding the maximum sizes accessed, and to map out the universal phase diagram of the model on both geometries. Most notably, we identify and characterize a critical point that separates an SO(5)-broken ordered phase at small coupling from an SO(5)-symmetric disordered phase at large coupling. The critical point becomes multicritical upon the inclusion of terms that break the SO(5) symmetry down to $\mathrm{U}(1) \times \mathrm{SU}(2)$, relevant for the deconfined phase transition between Néel antiferromagnetic and valence-bond-solid orders in quantum magnets. While the precise nature of the disordered phase in the thermodynamic limit remains to be determined, we argue that it is neither conformal nor trivially gapped, akin to a chiral quantum spin liquid with a small gap. Our finding of a multicritical point in the phase diagram of the SO(5) nonlinear sigma model with Wess-Zumino-Witten term resolves the long-standing open question of its global structure, and our QMC framework opens a new avenue for systematic studies of projected Hamiltonians, ranging from correlated flat bands to fractional quantum (anomalous) Hall systems.

</details>


### [102] [Gossamer Superconductivity in Moiré WSe$_2$ Bilayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03766)
*Hui-Ke Jin,Guangyue Ji,Zhan Wang,Jie Wang,Fu-Chun Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过将扭曲双层WSe₂中的moire超导映射为三角晶格上的扩展单轨道Hubbard模型，利用重整化平均场理论（renormalized mean-field theory）揭示了半填充零位移场下超导的手性d+id配对本质，并解释了从Mott绝缘体到超导体再到关联金属的转角依赖演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验在特定转角下的moire双层WSe₂中发现了稳健的超导电性，但其微观配对机制尚不明确。本文旨在从强关联理论角度揭示该超导的“gossamer”本质。

Method: 将moire连续模型映射为三角晶格上的扩展单轨道Hubbard模型，并采用重整化平均场理论（renormalized mean-field theory）研究强耦合相图。

Result: 中等强度的库仑排斥（Coulomb repulsion）部分抑制电荷涨落，同时保留有限密度的可移动双占据（doublons）和空穴（holes）；扩展动能与反铁磁超交换（antiferromagnetic superexchange）的竞争稳定了手性d+id超导相。

Conclusion: 该模型自然解释了从Mott绝缘体到超导体再到关联金属的转角依赖演化，且半填充配对态在密度掺杂后迅速消失，与实验观测一致。

Abstract: Moiré transition metal dichalcogenides have served as a versatile platform for simulating Hubbard physics. Recent experiments have identified robust superconductivity in moiré bilayer WSe$_2$ for certain twist angles. Here, we propose the gossamer nature of the superconductivity recently discovered at half-filling and zero displacement field in twisted WSe$_2$. By mapping the moiré continuum system to an effective extended single-orbital Hubbard model on the triangular lattice, we employ renormalized mean-field theory to investigate the strong-coupling phase diagram. We find that a moderate Coulomb repulsion partially suppresses charge fluctuations while preserving a finite density of mobile doublons and holes. In this regime, the interplay between extended kinetic hoppings and antiferromagnetic superexchange stabilizes a chiral $d+id$ superconducting phase. Our results naturally account for the twist-angle-dependent evolution from a Mott insulator to a superconductor and eventually to a correlated metal. Furthermore, the model demonstrates that this half-filled pairing state vanishes rapidly upon density doping, consistent with experimental observations.

### [103] [Plasmons in Holographic Ersatz Fermi Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03865)
*Eli Ismailov,Ulf Gran,Eric Nilsson*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个有限温度下的非费米液体红外有效全息模型，该模型满足Luttinger定理并包含长程库仑相互作用。通过在静态反德西特-史瓦西背景中采用Maxwell-Chern-Simons理论与LU(1)规范场，并选择适当边界条件，得到了一个等离子体频率按Luttinger定理标度的阻尼集体等离激元模式，同时分析了无库仑相互作用时的密度-密度关联函数，识别出与Lindhard连续谱一致的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Reissner-Nordstrom全息金属中缺乏Luttinger计数的费米面（Fermi surface），这促使作者寻找一种能够同时满足Luttinger定理并包含长程库仑相互作用的非费米液体全息模型。

Method: 采用Maxwell-Chern-Simons理论，在静态反德西特-史瓦西（anti-de Sitter-Schwarzschild）背景中，使用LU(1)规范场（而非传统的U(1)规范场）构建红外有效的全息模型，并通过适当选择边界条件来求解。

Result: 得到了一个阻尼的集体等离激元模式（collective plasmon mode），其等离子体频率（plasma frequency）按Luttinger定理预测的方式标度。在无长程库仑相互作用时，密度-密度关联函数（density-density correlator）中存在一个与Lindhard连续谱（Lindhard-like continuum）一致的贡献。

Conclusion: 该全息模型能够描述满足Luttinger定理的非费米液体，并自然地包含长程库仑相互作用，为理解强关联系统中的等离激元激发提供了全息对偶框架。

Abstract: We solve an infrared effective holographic model of a non-Fermi liquid at finite temperature that satisfies Luttinger's theorem and incorporates long-range Coulomb interactions. Motivated by the absence of a Luttinger-counting Fermi surface in standard Reissner-Nordstrom holographic metals, we consider a Maxwell-Chern-Simons theory in a static anti-de Sitter-Schwarzschild background, coupled to an LU(1) gauge field rather than a conventional U(1) gauge field. By an appropriate choice of boundary conditions, we obtain a damped collective plasmon mode whose plasma frequency scales as predicted by Luttinger's theorem. We further analyze the density-density correlator in the absence of long-range Coulomb interactions and identify a contribution consistent with a Lindhard-like continuum.

### [104] [Graph Neural Networks in the Wilson Loop Representation of Abelian Lattice Gauge Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03901)
*Ali Rayat,Gia-Wei Chern*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种规范不变的图神经网络（gauge-invariant graph neural network, GNN）架构，用于处理阿贝尔晶格规范模型（Abelian lattice gauge models）。该架构通过显式强制局域规范对称性（local gauge symmetry），利用规范不变输入（如威尔逊环 Wilson loops）消除冗余规范自由度，并在 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 和 $\mathrm{U}(1)$ 模型上实现了对全局与空间解析观测量（observables）的精确预测，同时作为 $\mathrm{U}(1)$ 量子链模型（quantum link models）的半经典动力学高效代理模型，实现了稳定可扩展的时间演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域规范结构（local gauge structures）在凝聚态系统与合成量子平台中广泛出现，作为强关联相和工程化动力学的有效描述。然而，传统的数值方法在处理规范-物质耦合（gauge-matter coupling）带来的非局域关联时面临挑战，需要一种既能保留物理对称性又能高效学习的计算框架。

Method: 提出一种规范不变的图神经网络架构，通过将局域规范不变性（local gauge invariance）显式编码到输入特征（如威尔逊环）和图消息传递（message passing）过程中，强制对称性约束，从而自动消除冗余的规范自由度，在保持表达力的同时降低计算复杂度。

Result: 在 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 和 $\mathrm{U}(1)$ 两种晶格规范模型上，该方法准确预测了全局观测量和空间分辨的局域量；在 $\mathrm{U}(1)$ 量子链模型的半经典动力学中，学习模型作为高效代理，无需重复进行费米子对角化（fermionic diagonalization）即可实现稳定、可扩展的时间演化，并能忠实再现局域动力学与统计关联。

Conclusion: 规范不变的消息传递（gauge-invariant message passing）为学习和模拟阿贝尔晶格规范系统提供了一个紧凑且基于物理的框架，在保持对称性约束的同时实现了高效且精准的预测与动力学模拟。

Abstract: Local gauge structures play a central role in a wide range of condensed matter systems and synthetic quantum platforms, where they emerge as effective descriptions of strongly correlated phases and engineered dynamics. We introduce a gauge-invariant graph neural network (GNN) architecture for Abelian lattice gauge models, in which symmetry is enforced explicitly through local gauge-invariant inputs, such as Wilson loops, and preserved throughout message passing, eliminating redundant gauge degrees of freedom while retaining expressive power. We benchmark the approach on both $\mathbb{Z}_2$ and $\mathrm{U}(1)$ lattice gauge models, achieving accurate predictions of global observables and spatially resolved quantities despite the nonlocal correlations induced by gauge-matter coupling. We further demonstrate that the learned model serves as an efficient surrogate for semiclassical dynamics in $\mathrm{U}(1)$ quantum link models, enabling stable and scalable time evolution without repeated fermionic diagonalization, while faithfully reproducing both local dynamics and statistical correlations. These results establish gauge-invariant message passing as a compact and physically grounded framework for learning and simulating Abelian lattice gauge systems.

### [105] [Anisotropy in Fourier space optical memory effect correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03469)
*Niall Byrnes,Matthew R. Foreman*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文研究了无序散射介质中与光学记忆效应（optical memory effect）相关的傅里叶域散斑相关性的各向异性（anisotropy）。在单次散射框架下，发现相关强度不仅依赖于横向波矢偏移，还非平凡地依赖于轴向波矢分量差异，并通过数值模拟验证了理论。研究还表明，这种各向异性行为同样出现在共轭记忆效应（conjugate memory effect）的伪相关性中，强调了轴向无序在散射场相关中的被忽视作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统光学记忆效应主要关注横向波矢偏移对散斑相关性的约束，而轴向（axial）波矢分量差异对相关强度的影响尚未被充分认识。本文旨在填补这一空白，揭示轴向无序在散射场相关中的角色。

Method: 采用单次散射（single scattering）理论框架分析傅里叶域散斑相关性；通过三维单次散射介质的数值模拟（numerical simulations）验证理论预测；并将分析扩展到伪相关性（pseudo-correlations），探讨共轭记忆效应中的各向异性行为。

Result: 传统记忆效应约束横向波矢偏移，但相关强度也非平凡地依赖于轴向波矢分量差异；数值模拟结果与理论高度一致；共轭记忆效应的伪相关性中也出现了类似的各向异性行为。

Conclusion: 轴向无序在散射场相关性中常被忽视，但实际起着重要作用；各向异性散斑相关性为理解和调控无序介质中的光传播提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We investigate anisotropy in Fourier-domain speckle correlations associated with the optical memory effect in disordered scattering media. Within a single scattering framework, we show that while the conventional memory effect constrains transverse wavevector shifts, the correlation strength also depends non-trivially on differences in the axial wavevector components. Our theory is supported by numerical simulations of a three-dimensional, single scattering medium, which show excellent agreement with theory. We extend the analysis to pseudo-correlations, demonstrating that analogous anisotropic behavior arises in the conjugate memory effect. Our results highlight the often neglected role of axial disorder in scattered field correlations.

### [106] [Neural-network reconstruction of THz transmission spectra using electrically tunable AlGaN/GaN plasmonic-crystal analyzer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03778)
*A. Witkowska,M. Dub,P. Sai,P. Tiwari,M. Sakowicz,J. A. Majewski,W. Knap*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统太赫兹光谱重建依赖干涉仪结构（如FTIR），系统复杂且体积庞大。本研究旨在探索一种无需干涉仪、基于电可调谐等离子体滤波与神经网络反演相结合的紧凑型太赫兹光谱重建架构。

Method: 采用电可调谐栅极AlGaN/GaN等离子体晶体分析仪，将透射光谱编码为电压依赖的强度信号；使用前馈神经网络（feedforward neural network）在合成数据集上训练，并在标准傅里叶变换红外（FTIR）模式和直接（固定镜面）采集模式下对四个样品进行实验验证。

Result: 在FTIR模式下，重建的均方误差（MSE）为0.015，直接模式为0.038；两种模式均能正确识别七个地真相（ground-truth）共振峰中的六个。相比一阶差分Tikhonov正则化基线，FTIR模式平均重建误差降低3.6倍，直接模式降低1.55倍，且伪峰更少、峰位误差更小。

Conclusion: 电压可调谐等离子体滤波结合神经网络反演，建立了一种无需干涉仪的太赫兹光谱重建架构，在精度和紧凑性方面均优于传统正则化方法。

Abstract: We demonstrate machine learning (ML) based reconstruction of terahertz transmission spectra using an electrically tunable grating-gate AlGaN/GaN plasmonic-crystal analyzer. The analyzer encodes the transmission spectrum into a voltage-dependent intensity, which is then inverted by an ML algorithm. A feedforward neural network trained on a synthetic dataset is validated experimentally on four samples in standard Fourier Transform Infrared (FTIR) mode and in direct (fixed-mirror) acquisition mode. The network achieves a mean square error (MSE) of the reconstruction of 0.015 in FTIR mode and 0.038 in direct mode, correctly identifying six out of seven ground-truth resonances in each mode. Against a first-difference Tikhonov regularization baseline, the mean reconstruction error is reduced 3.6 times in FTIR mode and 1.55 times in direct mode, with fewer spurious peaks and lower peak-position errors. Voltage-tunable plasmonic filtering combined with neural-network inversion establishes an interferometer-free architecture for THz spectral reconstruction.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从三维线性化弹性动力学方程（linearized elastodynamic equations）出发，利用标量势（scalar potential）与矢量势（vector potential）表示，结合球谐展开（spherical harmonic expansions）；通过施加牵引边界条件（traction boundary conditions）显式确定所有展开系数；静力解作为动力学公式的长时间极限严格导出。

Abstract: We present a complete analytical solution for the stress field inside a homogeneous, inside a homogeneous, linearly elastic solid sphere subjected to a concentrated normal load applied on its surface. Starting from the three-dimensional linearized elastodynamic equations, the displacement and stress fields are derived using scalar and vector potential representations combined with spherical harmonic expansions. All expansion coefficients are determined explicitly by enforcing the traction boundary conditions. The static elastic solution is obtained rigorously as the long-time limit of the dynamical formulation. Closed-form expressions for all components of the stress tensor are provided, enabling direct evaluation of the principal stresses and their differences throughout the interior of the sphere. The analytical solution is further generalized to arbitrary loading positions by means of rotational transformations, allowing systematic treatment of multiple concentrated loads through superposition.

### [108] [Searching for UFOs from the early universe: direct detection prospects for relativistically decoupling dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03014)
*Stephen E. Henrich,Yann Mambrini,Keith A. Olive*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究超相对论冻结（UFO）暗物质候选粒子的直接探测前景，以Z'门介子暗物质为例，发现LZ、XENONnT等实验已排除大部分UFO参数空间，且在中微子雾之上、0.4 GeV至1 TeV质量范围内仍有可行空间；SuperCDMS SNOLAB预计将于2026年覆盖0.5–10 GeV的大片UFO参数区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以Z'门介子暗物质（$Z'$-portal dark matter）作为案例，分析超相对论冻结（ultrarelativistically frozen-out, UFO）候选粒子的直接探测前景，并计算其与现有及下一代实验的交叉区域。

Result: UFO截面通常被重中介子质量尺度压低，但LZ、XENONnT、PandaX和DarkSide-50等实验已排除大部分UFO参数空间；在0.4 GeV至1 TeV的暗物质质量范围内，中微子雾（neutrino fog）之上仍存在可行参数空间；SuperCDMS SNOLAB（预计2026年运行）将在0.5–10 GeV质量区间覆盖大片UFO区域；对于重BSM门户相互作用，UFO的截面通常大于冻结（freeze-in）候选者，因而更易探测。

Conclusion: 超相对论冻结暗物质候选者是当前及下一代暗物质直接探测实验（如SuperCDMS SNOLAB）中有吸引力的目标，尤其在即将到来的后WIMP（post-WIMP）时代具有重要的探测价值；UFO与非相对论冻结（non-relativistic freeze-out）参数空间之间的简并区域也得到了仔细界定。

Abstract: Particles that decouple relativistically from the Standard Model bath during reheating represent a versatile class of well-motivated cold dark matter candidates. In fact, ultrarelativistic decoupling ($T_{\rm FO}\gg m_χ$) is quite generic for beyond the Standard Model (BSM) heavy portal interactions with strong couplings and relatively low reheating temperatures. In this work, we study the direct detection prospects for ultrarelativistically frozen-out (UFO) candidates, using $Z'$-portal dark matter as a case study. Although typical UFO cross sections are suppressed by a heavy mediator mass scale, we find that experiments such as LZ, XENONnT, PandaX, and DarkSide-50 have already excluded a large portion of the UFO parameter space and there remains viable space above the neutrino fog for $0.4 \text{ GeV} \lesssim m_{\rm DM}\lesssim 1$ TeV. Moreover, SuperCDMS SNOLAB, which is expected to begin collecting data in 2026, should access a large region of UFO parameter space in the 0.5-10 GeV mass range. For heavy BSM portal interactions ($M\gtrsim 1$ TeV), UFOs are typically more accessible to detection than freeze-in candidates due to the comparatively larger cross sections. We also carefully delineate regions of parameter space with degeneracy between UFO and non-relativistic freeze-out. In sum, UFOs are attractive candidates for ongoing and next-generation dark matter detection experiments in a looming post-WIMP era.

### [109] [Closing the knowledge gap in semileptonic $B\rightarrow X_c\ellν$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03021)
*Florian Herren,Raynette van Tonder*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文总结当前测量的含粲介子（charm mesons）的独有半轻子衰变（exclusive semileptonic decays）分支比（branching fractions）现状，利用实验数据评估独有测量之和与整体（inclusive）测量之间的差异，并通过半包含（semi-inclusive）衰变数据表明未测量成分主要来自不含D介子的末态，提示重子末态和D_s介子贡献显著。基于此讨论可能弥补差异的候选末态，并提出简化模型用于S波（S-wave）B介子衰变过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 厘清独有半轻子衰变分支比之和与整体测量值之间的差异来源，识别尚未被测量的衰变成分，以更完整地理解B介子半轻子衰变的分支比结构。

Method: 利用现有实验数据，比较独有测量分支比之和与整体测量值之间的差异；结合半包含衰变B→D Xℓν的实验结果，分析未测量成分的末态特征。

Result: 未测量的分支比成分主要由不含D介子的末态主导，提示重子末态和D_s介子有显著贡献；S波衰变过程B→D ηℓν和B→D_s Kℓν对总整体衰变率的未测量部分贡献很小。

Conclusion: 基于获得的分支比数据，讨论可能缩小差异的候选末态，提出新的末态搜索方向，并为特定S波衰变过程提供简化模型。

Abstract: In this work we summarize the current status of measured exclusive semileptonic branching fractions containing charm mesons. We use the available experimental data to evaluate the difference between the sum of exclusive measurements and the inclusive determination. By including experimental results of branching fractions relative to semi-inclusive $B\rightarrow D X\ellν$ decays, we demonstrate that the unmeasured components of the total branching fraction are dominated by final states devoid of $D$ mesons, hinting towards sizeable contributions from baryonic final states and $D_s$ mesons. Based on the obtained fractions, we discuss candidates that could potentially close the remaining difference and propose searches for promising final states. Furthermore, we provide simplified models for S-wave $B\rightarrow Dη\ellν$ and $B\rightarrow D_s K\ellν$ decays that contribute marginally to the unmeasured components of the total inclusive rate.

### [110] [From Information Geometry to Jet Substructure: A Triality of Cumulant Tensors, Energy Correlators, and Hypergraphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03063)
*Aritra Bal,Markus Klute,Benedikt Maier,Michael Spannowsky*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出高阶Fisher张量（higher-order Fisher tensors）来捕捉多观测量（multi-observable）辐射模式中的连通关联结构，并建立了Fisher张量、关联子（correlator）与超图（hypergraph）之间的精确三元对偶性（exact triality），为喷注（jet）物理中的可观测量基压缩、分类及可解释学习提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 成对Fisher图（Pairwise Fisher graphs）虽能捕捉局部协方差信息，但无法区分不可约的多观测量辐射模式与普通成对关联的集合。摘要指出这一缺失的结构信息需要由高阶Fisher张量来自然补充。

Method: 在分箱EEC、ECF或EFP的有限基（finite basis）及其生成的自然指数族坐标（natural exponential-family coordinates）下，局部高阶张量具有三种等价诠释：局部KL展开系数、所选关联子可观测量（correlator observables）的连通累积量（connected cumulant），以及连接这些观测量的超边（hyperedge）上的符号权重。由此导出精确的Fisher-关联子-超图三元对偶性。

Result: 在四个应用中展示了框架效果：三重Fisher张量降低了局部KL截断误差并分离出主导三重态结构；在两喷注vs三喷注喷注子结构基准任务中，超图选择器改进了压缩基分类；在33观测量基设计问题中，Fisher超图在12个观测量处保留了更多三阶局部响应；低容量学习基准展示了Fisher超边可作为关联子可观测量上消息传递（message passing）的可解释归纳偏置（inductive bias）。

Conclusion: 将二次Fisher矩阵扩展到首个非平凡的高阶张量，能够识别真正的连通多观测量辐射模式，为高阶拉普拉斯算子（higher-order Laplacians）和消息传递提供超边权重，并给出超越成对信息的可观测量基压缩原则。精确累积量诠释是自然指数族坐标所特有的性质。

Abstract: Pairwise Fisher graphs capture local covariance information, but they cannot distinguish an irreducible multi-observable radiation pattern from a collection of ordinary pairwise correlations. We show that this missing structure is naturally supplied by higher-order Fisher tensors. In a finite basis of binned EECs, ECFs, or EFPs, and in the natural exponential-family coordinates generated by that basis, the same local tensor has three equivalent interpretations: a coefficient in the local Kullback-Leibler expansion, a connected cumulant of the chosen correlator observables, and a signed weight on a hyperedge linking those observables. This gives an exact Fisher-correlator-hypergraph triality in the local exponential-family embedding. The triality provides a direct construction of physics-informed hypergraphs from correlator data. Extending the quadratic Fisher matrix to the first non-trivial higher tensor identifies genuinely connected multi-observable radiation patterns, supplies hyperedge weights for higher-order Laplacians and message passing, and gives a principled criterion for compressing observable bases beyond pairwise information. We develop these constructions and spell out why the exact cumulant interpretation is special to natural exponential-family coordinates. We illustrate the framework in four applications. In a minimal local-KL study, the cubic Fisher tensor reduces the KL truncation error and isolates the dominant triplet structure. In a two-versus-three prong jet substructure benchmark, the hypergraph selector improves compressed-basis classification. In a 33-observable basis-design problem, the Fisher hypergraph retains more third-order local response at twelve observables. A low-capacity learning benchmark then shows how the same Fisher hyperedges can be used as an interpretable inductive bias for message passing on correlator observables.

</details>

Owing to the same-sign initial state, s-channel contributions are absent, rendering VBS as the dominant production mode and thereby significantly enhancing the sensitivity to aQGCs. Using dimension-8 Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) operators, we classify the relevant operator sets contributing to charged and neutral QGCs, and confront them with existing bounds from the LHC. Abstract: The ATLAS, CMS and LHCb collaborations have reported data for the inclusive production of lepton pairs with invariant mass 80-100 GeV in pp collisions. Associated with this structure is a local maximum of the entropy of the Z-boson polarization density matrix extracted using quantum tomography. Data from CMS and LHCb at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV are broadly consistent. The origin of the observed phenomena is unknown but generally related to observables that are formally odd under charge conjugation, parity and time-reversal. ### [114] [Exclusive photoproduction of a di-meson pair with large invariant mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03880)
*Saad Nabeebaccus,David Perez,Lech Szymanowski,Samuel Wallon*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文在共线因子化（collinear factorisation）框架下研究了轻介子对（ρ和π介子）的遍举光生过程，将振幅因子化为硬散射部分、广义部分子分布（GPD）和两个分布振幅（DA）。论文在领头阶和领头扭度下自动化计算了26个不涉及中性C=+交换的反应道的振幅，特别处理了卷积积分中的极点问题以及硬部分运动学的不自洽性，并数值评估了截面。结果表明，此类遍举双介子光生过程具有非常好的统计量，可为提取GPD提供重要机会。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展遍举光生过程的研究范围，从光子-介子末态扩展到双介子末态，以获取更多可提取GPD的反应道，从而为理解核子的三维部分子结构提供更丰富的实验探针。

Method: 采用共线因子化（collinear factorisation）框架，将振幅分解为可微扰计算的过程依赖硬部分、一个广义部分子分布（GPD）和两个分布振幅（DA）。在领头阶（leading order in α_s）和领头扭度（leading twist）下，以全自动化方式计算了26个不同反应道的振幅；特别处理了三维卷积积分中的极点问题（采用费曼iε因子正规化）以及硬部分运动学与其余过程运动学的不自洽性。

Result: 振幅构建完成后，对部分反应道在CLAS12实验典型能量下评估了截面。结果表明，遍举双介子光生过程具有极好的统计量，可比遍举光子-介子光生过程高出最多两个数量级。

Conclusion: 所研究的双介子遍举光生反应族为提取广义部分子分布（GPD）提供了重要的实验机会。

Abstract: The exclusive photoproduction of a pair of light mesons is studied within the framework of collinear factorisation. The amplitude factorises into a process-dependent perturbatively calculable hard part, a generalised parton distribution (GPD) and two distribution amplitudes (DAs). We focus on the production of any combination of $ρ$ and $π$ mesons (of any charge and polarisation) that do not involve neutral $C=+$ exchanges with the nucleon. This gives a total of 26 distinct channels, which are sensitive to quark GPDs only. We calculate the amplitude for these di-meson processes at leading order in $α_s$ and at leading twist, in a fully-automated way. Depending on the choice of mesons in the final state, some of these processes are sensitive to chiral-odd (helicity-flip) GPDs. Particular attention is given to the treatment of poles in the 3-dimensional convolution integral of the momentum fractions connecting the hard part with the different non-perturbative components. These poles are regularised by usual Feynman $i ε$ factors, but lead to numerical instabilities if not dealt with properly. We also discuss in detail the construction of the phase space. Importantly, we propose a resolution for the inconsistency of the kinematics of the hard part of the process, where hadron masses and other soft scales are neglected, with the rest of the process. As a proof of concept, we explicitly evaluate the cross section, for a subset of processes whose amplitudes have been constructed, at energies typical of the CLAS12 experiment at JLab. Our results indicate that exclusive di-meson photoproduction processes have very good statistics, which can be a factor of up to a hundred more than the exclusive photon-meson photoproduction process. Therefore, the family of processes that we study here represents a great opportunity for GPD extraction.

Abstract: We consider how the recent CMS measurements of the masses and quantum numbers of $X(6600)$, $X(6900)$ and $X(7100)$ can help to reveal the internal structure of these apparent $cc\bar{c}\bar{c}$ tetraquark states. The measured $J^{PC} = 2^{++}$ quantum numbers of $X(6600)$ are consistent with our previous prediction, and imply the existence of lighter $0^{++}$ partner $X(6400)$ which also decays to $J/ψJ/ψ$. We give predictions for the masses and decay properties of the scalar and other partner states, which are key experimental tests to discriminate between quark and diquark models. We urge closer experimental scrutiny in this mass region, to establish an S-wave multiplet of $cc \bar c \bar c$ states (the first of its kind), leading to a breakthrough in exotic hadron research and our understanding of exclusively heavy quark exotics.

### [116] [Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking and the Emergent Einstein-Standard Model: From Weyl x SU (2)L x U (1)Y Gauge Theory to Geometric Mass Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02955)
*Hao-Qian Peng,Yun-Tao Gu,Yu-Xiao Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过扩展四维Weyl二次引力，构建了一个Weyl × SU(2)_L × U(1)_Y规范不变理论，利用Stueckelberg机制提取Weyl Goldstone模式，并通过Weyl规范对称性自发破缺统一导出爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量、Weyl规范场质量项和希格斯势，从而统一了Stueckelberg、Higgs和Yukawa机制，并预言了新的唯象学特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型中希格斯势的形式（-μ²|φ|²+λ²|φ|⁴）在Weyl规范对称性下是被禁止的，因此需要一种自洽的几何框架来生成该势能，并统一解释质量起源。

Method: 构建一个Weyl不变的四维理论，扩展Weyl二次引力（Weyl quadratic gravity），引入Weyl不变的标量、费米子、Yukawa和规范扇区；利用二次结构(R̃-μ²|φ|²)²，通过独立于希格斯场的Stueckelberg机制提取Weyl Goldstone模式，再通过Weyl规范对称性的自发破缺实现理论约化。

Result: Weyl规范对称性自发破缺将Weyl二次曲率约化为爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量并产生正宇宙学常数，生成Weyl规范场质量项，同时产生标准的希格斯势。该框架统一了Stueckelberg、Higgs和Yukawa机制，复现了标准模型的质量生成，并预言希格斯场对Weyl规范场质量的额外贡献以及一组希格斯-Weyl耦合，其中包含一个矢量暗物质候选者。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了质量起源的几何本质（geometric origin of mass），并为超出标准模型的新物理（如暗物质候选者）提供了唯象学途径。

Abstract: We construct a Weyl x SU(2)_L x U(1)_Y invariant theory by extending four-dimensional Weyl quadratic gravity with Weyl-invariant scalar, fermion, Yukawa and gauge sectors. The quadratic structure (R^tilde - mu^2 |phi|^2)^2 allows the Weyl Goldstone mode to be extracted via a Stueckelberg mechanism independent of the Higgs field. Spontaneous breaking of Weyl gauge symmetry reduces the Weyl quadratic curvature to the Einstein-Hilbert action with a positive cosmological constant, generates a mass term for the Weyl gauge field, and simultaneously produces the Higgs potential -mu^2 |phi|^2 + lambda^2 |phi|^4, which is otherwise forbidden by the symmetry. Our framework unifies the Stueckelberg, Higgs and Yukawa mechanisms, reproduces Standard Model mass generation, and predicts additional Higgs-induced contributions to the Weyl gauge field mass, together with a set of Higgs-Weyl couplings. These interactions provide new phenomenological handles, including a vector dark matter candidate, and highlight the geometric origin of mass.

</details>


### [117] [QCD sum rules: Borel parameter vs. Euclidean time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04001)
*A. V. Smilga*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探索了一种基于坐标空间（coordinate space）欧几里得时间（Euclidean time）的QCD求和规则（QCD sum rules）修正方案，以核子道（nucleon channel）为例导出了欧几里得时间求和规则，并与传统的玻雷求和规则（Borel sum rules）进行了比较。结果表明，坐标空间方法虽能粗略估算核子质量和残差（residue），但其受幂次修正（power corrections）和连续谱贡献（continuum contribution）不确定性的影响远大于玻雷求和规则，且可信区间（fiducial interval）几乎不存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统QCD求和规则基于流关联函数（current correlators）的玻雷变换（Borel transforms），本文试图探索一种替代方案：直接在坐标空间中考察关联函数作为欧几里得时间的函数，以检验该方法的可行性与局限性。

Method: 以核子道为例，推导坐标空间下的欧几里得时间求和规则（Euclidean time sum rules），并与传统的玻雷求和规则进行对比分析。

Result: 坐标空间方法能够给出核子质量和残差的粗略估计，但其结果对幂次修正和连续谱贡献的不确定性更为敏感；相比之下，该方法缺乏一个明确的可信区间。

Conclusion: 坐标空间下的欧几里得时间求和规则在估算强子参数方面不如传统的玻雷求和规则稳健，其实际应用价值受到较大限制。

Abstract: We explore a modification of QCD sum rules where, instead of Borel transforms of current correlators, one considers the correlators in coordinate space as functions of Euclidean time. Taking the nucleon channel as an example, we derive such Euclidean time sum rules and compare them with the traditional Borel sum rules. We show that a rough estimate of nucleon mass and residue is also possible working in coordinate space, but such sum rules are much more affected by the uncertainties in power corrections and continuum contribution than the Borel ones: the fiducial interval is practically absent.

</details>


### [118] [Two-loop leading-color QCD corrections for Higgs plus two-jet production in the heavy-top limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04009)
*Giuseppe De Laurentis,Harald Ita,Viktor Kuschke,Michael Ruf,Vasily Sotnikov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在重顶夸克有效理论下计算了通过胶子融合产生的与双喷注关联的希格斯玻色子的领头色双圈QCD修正，提供了基于单位性框架和新型多元分式分解算法的螺旋度振幅有限余项的解析表达式，并验证了非简并物理动量构型下的阈值存在性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为希格斯玻色子与双喷注伴随产生过程提供高精度双圈QCD修正，弥补此前仅在领头阶或近似处理层面上的不足，推动理论预测与实验测量的精确比较。

Method: 采用数值单位性框架（numerical unitarity framework）从有限域数值样本中重构有限余项；引入基于通用双变量切片和理想交集简化处理的多元分式分解（multivariate partial fraction decomposition）新算法，以降低样本需求并获得紧凑解析表达式。

Result: 给出了用单质量五边形函数和旋量-螺旋度系数（spinor-helicity coefficients）表示的螺旋度振幅有限余项的解析表达式；实现了数值评估的高效稳定计算程序；确认了非简并物理动量构型下与虚大质量粒子交换相关的阈值存在性。

Conclusion: 所发展的计算方法和获得的解析表达式为希格斯玻色子与双喷注伴随产生过程的唯象应用提供了可靠且高效的数值工具，同时揭示了振幅奇异结构中的重要物理特征。

Abstract: We present the leading-color two-loop QCD corrections for Higgs-boson production in association with two jets through gluon fusion in the heavy-top effective theory. We provide analytic expressions for the finite remainders of the helicity amplitudes, written in terms of one-mass pentagon functions with spinor-helicity coefficients. These expressions are obtained by reconstructing the amplitudes from numerical finite-field samples computed within the numerical unitarity framework. The reconstruction is made possible by several advances in exploiting the analytic structure of the amplitudes, which both reduce the number of required samples and lead to compact representations. In particular, we introduce a new algorithm for multivariate partial fraction decomposition, based on a generic bivariate slice and a simplified treatment of ideal intersections. Using the resulting analytic expressions, we provide an efficient and stable implementation of their numerical evaluation, ready for phenomenological applications. Finally, we study the singularity structure of the remainders and confirm the existence of a threshold at non-degenerate physical momentum configurations, usually associated with massive virtual particle exchanges.

### [119] [Constraining Tsallis Corrections to Photon Reheating from Electron-Positron Annihilation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03223)
*Matias P. Gonzalez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在Tsallis形式下推广了早期宇宙中电子-正电子湮灭对光子的熵转移，引入了非广延修正，并通过CMB+BAO和BBN数据的χ²分析，给出了非广延参数q的2σ上限为|q-1|≤1.3×10⁻²，表明在MeV时期玻尔兹曼-吉布斯广延性的偏离必须很小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准宇宙学模型假设熵由玻尔兹曼-吉布斯（Boltzmann-Gibbs）统计描述，但尚不清楚在早期宇宙的高能极端条件下，广延性（extensivity）假设是否仍然严格成立。本文旨在检验非广延统计力学（nonextensive statistical mechanics）对电子-正电子湮灭时期熵转移过程的影响。

Method: 基于Tsallis形式（Tsallis formalism），采用Curado-Tsallis约束导出的广义分布函数对熵转移进行推广；仅对电子-正电子对引入非广延修正，光子部分保持广延性；修正结果映射为有效相对论性粒子数N_eff；结合宇宙微波背景（CMB）、重子声学振荡（BAO）和大爆炸核合成（BBN）数据进行联合χ²分析。

Result: 得到非广延参数q在2σ置信水平下的上限为|q-1|≤1.3×10⁻²，即对玻尔兹曼-吉布斯广延性的任何偏离在MeV时期必须小于约1.3%。

Conclusion: 在早期宇宙的MeV能量尺度上，非广延修正虽然理论允许存在，但观测数据强约束其幅度须很小，从而支持标准宇宙学中玻尔兹曼-吉布斯统计在此时期仍是良好近似。

Abstract: In this work we generalize the entropy transfer from electron-positron annihilation to photons in the early Universe. The generalization is implemented within the Tsallis formalism by using generalized distribution functions derived from Curado-Tsallis constraints. Through this deformation, the entropy density of the electromagnetic sector is modified, while the photon component is kept extensive. Therefore, the nonextensive correction is introduced only in the $e^-e^+$ pairs. This affects the entropic degrees of freedom before electron-positron annihilation and consequently modifies the temperature ratio $T_ν/T_γ$. The resulting correction is then mapped into the effective number of relativistic species, $N_{\rm eff}$. Finally, by performing a combined $χ^2$ analysis using CMB$+$BAO and BBN data, we obtain the $2σ$ bound $|q-1|\leq 1.3\times10^{-2}$ for the nonextensive parameter. This result implies that any departure or correction from Boltzmann-Gibbs extensivity must remain small during the MeV era.

### [120] [Charging-up and reverse charging-up phenomena in a double-mask triple GEM detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02922)

TL;DR: 本文实验研究了双掩模三层GEM探测器在氩气与二氧化碳混合气体中的充电效应与反向充电效应，揭示了辐照条件下增益变化及其稳定行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GEM探测器在高能物理实验中广泛用于径迹探测，但其介电材料Kapton在辐照下会产生充电效应（charging-up effect），影响增益稳定性。此前已观察到反向充电效应（reverse charging-up effect），但对其定量行为缺乏系统研究。

Method: 实验采用双掩模（double-mask）三层GEM室（triple GEM chamber），工作气体为氩气与二氧化碳（Argon and Carbon dioxide, 70/30）混合气。通过控制辐照率变化，测量探测器增益的动态响应，分别记录充电过程与反向充电过程的增益变化曲线。

Result: 辐照增加时，GEM箔发生充电效应，增益出现变化；辐照率降低后，观察到反向充电效应，增益逐渐弛豫回归初始值。实验数据给出了增益随辐照变化及其稳定过程的定量描述。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了GEM探测器充电与反向充电效应的详细实验依据，有助于理解增益稳定性机制，为探测器在高辐射环境下的可靠运行提供参考。

Abstract: The Gas Electron Multiplier (GEM) detectors are widely used in high-energy physics (HEP) experiments as tracking devices because of their excellent position resolution and to handle high particle rates capability. Charging-up effect is a well known phenomenon in GEM detectors because of the presence of the dielectric medium -- Kapton in the foil. Charging-up of GEM foil takes place when it is exposed to high radiation after application of high voltage. A new phenomenon of reverse charging-up, a complementary behaviour is also observed when the irradiation rate is reduced, where the gain relaxes gradually towards its initial value. In this study, the charging-up and reverse charging-up effects are investigated for a double-mask triple GEM chamber operated with an Argon and Carbon dioxide (70/30) gas mixture. The measurements provide a detailed understanding of the gain variation under irradiation and its stabilisation behaviour. The experimental setup, methodology and results are presented in this article.

### [121] [Bosonic Ghost Correlators: A Case Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02941)
*Xueting Li,Damodar Rajbhandari,David Ridout*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文通过微分方程方法研究玻色子鬼影系统（bosonic ghost system）中的关联函数（correlation functions），证明了该自由场理论（free-field theory）中四点函数存在对数奇异性（logarithmic singularities），揭示了其关联函数结构比预期更为丰富。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管对数共形场论（logarithmic conformal field theories, LCFTs）的表示论（representation theory）已有大量研究，但对其解析数据（analytic data）、特别是关联函数的理解仍不充分。本文旨在填补这一空白，以最基础的对数模型之一——玻色子鬼影系统为例，探索其关联函数的完整结构。

Method: 采用微分方程（differential equations）方法分析玻色子鬼影系统的关联函数，通过求解微分方程来揭示关联函数的解析结构。后续工作（sequel）将采用库仑气体（Coulomb gas）方法及自举法（bootstrap method）对结果进行进一步精化。

Result: 主要结果是验证了玻色子鬼影系统的四点函数（four-point functions）存在对数奇异性（logarithmic singularities），表明尽管该理论具有自由场（free-field）性质，其关联函数结构仍比预期更为丰富和复杂。

Conclusion: 玻色子鬼影系统的关联函数展现出超出自由场理论预期的丰富结构，四点函数中对数奇异性的存在证实了该模型作为对数共形场论的典型特征。本文为后续使用库仑气体和自举法进行更深入研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: There has been a lot of recent work addressing the representation theory that underlies logarithmic conformal field theories. A full understanding of these models will however also need analytic data, in particular the correlation functions. Here, we explore the correlators of one of the most fundamental of all logarithmic models: the bosonic ghost system. In this first part, we use differential equations to show that the correlation functions exhibit a richness beyond what one might have expected, given the free-field nature of the theory. Our main result is the verification that there are four-point functions with logarithmic singularities. In a sequel, we will employ Coulomb gas and bootstrap methods to further refine the results presented here.

### [122] [Modular functors and CFT correlators via double categories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03708)
*Jürgen Fuchs,Christoph Schweigert,Yang Yang*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文提出双重范畴（double categories）为基于（双范畴）弦网构造（string-net construction）的模函子（modular functors）提供了自然框架，并利用辫论方法证明了一个垂直变换（vertical transformation）是同构（equivalence），进而推导出场函子（field functors）是范畴等价（equivalences of categories），而普适关联子（universal correlators）是向量空间同构（isomorphisms of vector spaces）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模函子与共形场论（conformal field theory）关联子的数学描述缺乏统一的范畴框架，特别是在双重范畴的视角下尚未得到系统阐释。

Method: 采用双重范畴语言，将模函子重新表述为双重函子（double functor），源范畴为对称幺半双重范畴（symmetric monoidal double category）的bordisms，目标为以profunctor和functor作为水平和垂直态射的双重范畴；利用辫论方法（skein theoretic methods）证明垂直变换的等价性。

Result: 基于一个关键枢轴幺半范畴（pivotal monoidal category）C，证明了一个垂直变换在两个模函子之间是同构，进而得出场函子是范畴等价，普适关联子是向量空间同构。

Conclusion: 双重范畴为模函子及其对应的共形场论提供了统一的描述框架，表明该框架下的场函子和关联子具有自然的等价性/同构性，为理解弦网构造与共形场论之间的数学结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: We point out that double categories provide a natural setting for modular functors obtained by a (bicategorical) string-net construction: The source of the modular functor -- which is now a double functor -- is a symmetric monoidal double category of bordisms, with bordisms as horizontal morphisms and smooth embeddings of manifolds as vertical morphisms. The target of the modular functor is a double category with profunctors and functors as horizontal and vertical morphisms.
  The correlators and field functors for a conformal field theory based on a pivotal monoidal category $\mathcal C$ can then be understood in the unified setting of a vertical transformation between the modular functors for two pointed pivotal bicategories, the delooping of $\mathcal C$ and the bicategory of $Δ$-separable symmetric Frobenius algebras in $\mathcal C$. Using skein theoretic methods, we show that this vertical transformation is an equivalence, which implies that field functors are equivalences of categories and that universal correlators are isomorphisms of vector spaces.

</details>

### [123] [Thermodynamic phase transitions reveal the resilience structure of urban traffic congestion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03879)
*Luis E. Olmos*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了城市尺度的交通拥堵会经历一种类似统计力学中“有序-无序相变”（order-disorder phase transition）的非线性转变：以总体移动性（aggregate mobility）为控制参数、拥堵范围（jam extent）为集体序参量（collective order parameter），并定义了具有物理意义的有效热力学温度（effective thermodynamic temperature），量化基础设施异质性（infrastructural heterogeneity）和城市拥堵构型的探索广度。低温城市对拥堵更敏感，微小的移动性增加就可能触发系统性的拥堵转变。该框架还指出宏观基本图（macroscopic fundamental diagram, MFD）是更丰富自由能景观（free-energy landscape）的投影。基于46个拉美及加勒比城市验证，并由全球三大洲8个城市的线圈检测器数据独立确认。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解城市交通如何从自由流（free-flowing）状态过渡到拥堵（congested）状态，是城市科学（urban science）中一个核心的开放问题。现有研究缺乏一个统一的理论框架来描述这一全局性转变。

Method: 将城市交通拥堵的涌现类比为统计力学中的有序-无序相变（order-disorder phase transition），以总体移动性为控制参数（control parameter）、拥堵范围为集体序参量（collective order parameter），并从中推导和实证识别出一个具有物理意义的有效热力学温度（effective thermodynamic temperature），用以刻画基础设施异质性及拥堵构型的探索广度。

Result: 低温城市对拥堵更脆弱（congestion-fragile），小幅移动性增加即可触发系统性的拥堵相变。宏观基本图（MFD）被发现仅是更丰富自由能景观（free-energy landscape）的投影，其受熵-容量权衡（entropy-capacity trade-offs）支配。该框架在46个拉美及加勒比城市得到验证，并由全球三大洲8个城市的线圈检测器数据独立确认。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个基于物理学的城市交通韧性比较基础，并为预测移动性需求变化下的拥堵体制转换（congestion regime shifts）提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Understanding how cities transition from free-flowing to congested traffic remains a central open problem in urban science. Here we show that city-scale congestion undergoes a reproducible nonlinear transition analogous to an order-disorder phase transition in statistical mechanics, in which aggregate mobility acts as a control parameter and jam extent as a collective order parameter. Crucially, this analogy is not merely formal: we derive and empirically identify an effective thermodynamic temperature with concrete physical meaning, quantifying infrastructural heterogeneity and how broadly a city explores congestion configurations as demand increases. Low-temperature cities are congestion-fragile: small mobility increases trigger sharp, system-wide jam transitions. This framework further reveals that the macroscopic fundamental diagram is an incomplete description of the traffic state: it emerges as a projection of a richer free-energy landscape governed by entropy-capacity trade-offs. Validated across 46 cities in Latin America and the Caribbean and independently confirmed with loop-detector data from 8 cities on three continents, these results establish a physics-based foundation for comparing urban traffic resilience and anticipating congestion regime shifts under changing mobility demand.

</details>
