### [125] [Expanding functional protein sequence space using high entropy generative models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03578)

Main category: q-bio.QM

TL;DR: 本研究系统比较了不同参数密度的玻尔兹曼机（Boltzmann Machine）在蛋白质设计中的表现，发现稀疏模型与稠密模型在生成功能性序列方面无显著差异，但高熵的最大熵模型（meDCA）在探索序列空间、减少过拟合和刻画适应性景观方面显著优于低熵模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于进化序列数据的玻尔兹曼机已成为数据驱动蛋白质设计的有力范式，但模型架构（特别是参数密度）与实验性能之间的关系尚不明确。

Method: 以分支酸变位酶（Chorismate Mutase）家族为模型系统，对比标准全连接玻尔兹曼机（bmDCA）与通过渐进边激活（eaDCA）和边抽取（edDCA）生成的稀疏模型；沿抽取轨迹识别出最大熵模型（meDCA），并通过体内互补实验验证各模型生成的序列功能。

Result: 所有架构（无论稀疏程度）均能以高成功率生成功能性酶，但meDCA模型采样的可行序列空间比低熵模型大超过15个数量级；高熵模型系统性地减少了过拟合，并能更好地捕捉天然蛋白质周围的局部中性空间（neutral space）。

Conclusion: 满足共进化统计的各种模型均可生成功能性序列，但高熵玻尔兹曼机（high-entropy Boltzmann Machines）提供了对潜在进化适应性景观（evolutionary fitness landscape）更优越的表征。

Abstract: Boltzmann Machines trained on evolutionary sequence data have emerged as a powerful paradigm for the data-driven design of artificial proteins. However, the relationship between model architecture, specifically parameter density, and experimental performance remains poorly understood. Here, we investigate this relationship using the Chorismate Mutase enzyme family as a model system. We compare standard fully connected Boltzmann Machines for Direct Coupling Analysis (bmDCA) with sparse models generated via progressive edge activation (eaDCA) and edge decimation (edDCA). We identify a maximum-entropy model (meDCA) along the decimation trajectory that represents an optimal balance between constraint satisfaction and the flexibility of the probability distribution. We synthesized and tested artificial sequences from all models using an in vivo complementation assay, finding that all architectures, regardless of sparsity, generate functional enzymes with high success rates, even at significant divergence from natural sequences. Despite this functional equivalence, we demonstrate that the meDCA model samples a viable sequence space that is more than fifteen orders of magnitude larger than its low-entropy counterparts. Furthermore, comparative analyses reveal that high-entropy models systematically minimize overfitting and better capture the local neutral spaces surrounding natural proteins. These findings suggest that while various models satisfying coevolutionary statistics can generate functional sequences, high-entropy Boltzmann Machines provide a superior representation of the underlying evolutionary fitness landscape.

</details>

### [126] [Tunable Odd-Parity Spin Splittings in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03026)
*Yue Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个理论框架，通过在共线交变磁体（collinear altermagnets）中引入双色线性偏振光驱动或耦合奇宇称环流序（P-odd loop-current order），诱导出奇宇称自旋劈裂（odd-parity spin splitting），从而实现对自旋极化电流的电学和光学操控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动量依赖的自旋劈裂（momentum-dependent spin splitting）及其与宇称（inversion, P）和时间反演（time-reversal, T）对称性的关系是非相对论自旋电子学（nonrelativistic spintronics）的核心。现有代表性体系包括具有(P,T)=(+,-)的共线交变磁体（collinear altermagnets）和具有(P,T)=(-,+)的非共线奇宇称磁体（non-collinear odd-parity magnets）。本文旨在将奇宇称自旋劈裂拓展到更为丰富的共线交变磁体中。

Method: 发展了一个理论框架，通过两种机制诱导奇宇称自旋劈裂：一是双色线性偏振光场（two-color linearly polarized light field）驱动；二是耦合到奇宇称环流序（P-odd loop-current order）。适当地锁定相位的双色驱动可诱导产生静态的(P,T)=(-,-)序，该序等价于一个平移不变的奇宇称环流序。将该序耦合到交变磁体可获得可控的混合宇称自旋织构（mixed-parity spin texture）。本文还采用群论（group-theory）和微观Floquet理论（microscopic Floquet theory）来揭示涌现响应。

Result: 双色光驱动诱导的(P,T)=(-,-)序与交变磁体耦合可产生可控的混合宇称自旋织构。将该机制应用于共线PT对称磁体（collinear PT-symmetric magnet），可诱导出具有非相对论无耗散反常自旋霍尔电导（nonrelativistic dissipationless anomalous spin Hall conductivity）的(P,T)=(+,+)态。

Conclusion: 本文提出的机制为自旋电子学应用中对自旋极化电流的电学和光学操控开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Momentum-dependent spin splitting and its relation to inversion ($P$) and time-reversal ($T$) symmetries are central to nonrelativistic spintronics. Representative examples include collinear altermagnets with $(P,T)=(+,-)$ and non-collinear odd-parity magnets with $(P,T)=(-,+)$. In this work, we develop a theoretical framework to induce odd-parity spin splittings in the more abundant collinear altermagnets through two mechanisms: driving by a two-color linearly polarized light field or coupling to a $P$-odd loop-current order. Properly phase-locked two-color driving induces a static $(P,T)=(-,-)$ order, symmetry-equivalent to a translationally invariant $P$-odd loop-current order. Coupling this order to an altermagnet produces a controllable mixed-parity spin texture, opening new avenues for the electrical and optical manipulation of spin-polarized currents in spintronics applications. The same mechanism applied to a collinear $PT$-symmetric magnet induces a distinct $(P,T)=(+,+)$ state with a nonrelativistic dissipationless anomalous spin Hall conductivity. We present group-theory and microscopic Floquet theory to highlight the emergent responses.

</details>


### [127] [Characterizing electronic scattering rates with transport in multiterminal devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03030)
*Jack H. Farrell,Andrew Lucas*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出利用多端器件（multiterminal device）中的电流分配实验，无需空间分辨成像即可区分二维电子系统的弹道（ballistic）、流体动力学（hydrodynamic）、欧姆（Ohmic）和层析（tomographic）等输运 regime，并通过线性化玻尔兹曼模型提取动量弛豫与动量守恒散射率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强相互作用二维电子器件中理论上存在多种输运 regime（弹道、流体动力学、扩散等），但真实样品常处于这些理想极限之间的交叉区（crossover regimes）。现有区分这些 regime 的方法通常依赖空间分辨成像实验，实验复杂度高。因此需要一种更简单的实验手段来区分这些输运 regime 并提取相关散射率。

Method: 采用五端几何结构（five-terminal geometry）中的线性化玻尔兹曼模型（linearized Boltzmann model）进行理论分析。通过研究电流在各漏极（drain contacts）之间的分配（current partition）来诊断输运行为的转变。

Result: 发现五端器件中的电流分配能够诊断弹道-流体动力学-欧姆交叉（ballistic-hydrodynamic-Ohmic crossover），并可在交叉区提取动量弛豫散射率（momentum-relaxing scattering rate）和动量守恒散射率（momentum-conserving scattering rate）。同一几何结构还展现了层析 regime（tomographic regime）的清晰特征，有望在实验中定量区分黏性流（viscous flow）与层析流（tomographic flow）。

Conclusion: 多端器件提供了一种比空间分辨成像实验更简单的实验路径，用于表征电子液体中的输运 regime。

Abstract: Strongly interacting electrons in clean two-dimensional devices are theorized to exhibit many distinct transport regimes, such as ballistic, hydrodynamic, or diffusive. Realistic samples often lie in crossover regimes between these idealized limits. We show how a single experiment on a multiterminal device can distinguish these regimes and constrain the relevant scattering rates without space-resolved imaging. Using a linearized Boltzmann model in a five-terminal geometry, we find that current partition among the drain contacts diagnoses the ballistic-hydrodynamic-Ohmic crossover and allows extraction of momentum-relaxing and momentum-conserving scattering rates in the crossover regime. The same geometry also exhibits clear signatures of the tomographic regime, potentially allowing for a quantitative discrimination between viscous and tomographic flow in experiments. Our results demonstrate that multiterminal devices are a simpler experimental route to characterize transport regimes in electron liquids, relative to space-resolved imaging experiments.

</details>


### [128] [Beam canalization by a non-Abelian gauge field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03047)
*Olha Bahrova,Jiahao Ren,Feng Jin,Rui Su,Guillaume Malpuech,Dmitry Solnyshkov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了由倾斜狄拉克点（tilted Dirac points）产生的双曲线与准平坦等频轮廓（IFCs）在光子体系中的光束渠道化（beam canalization）现象，重点揭示了非阿贝尔规范场（non-Abelian gauge field）通过极化赝旋进（polarization pseudospin precession）对渠道化效应的增强作用，相比仅基于等频轮廓群速度的描述，高斯光束的渠道化程度提升了十倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双曲线与准平坦等频轮廓已被用于光束渠道化，其可通过光子体系中的倾斜狄拉克点实现。微腔中的狄拉克点由横电/横磁分裂（transverse-electric/transverse-magnetic splitting）与线性双折射（linear birefringence）共同产生。本文旨在揭示空间动力学与极化赝旋进之间的耦合如何进一步促进渠道化效应。

Method: 本文采用解析与数值方法，将渠道化动力学描述为非阿贝尔规范场（non-Abelian gauge field）对涌现电荷（emergent charges，即自旋电流 spin current）的作用，并基于此框架分析高斯光束的渠道化行为。

Result: 研究表明，非阿贝尔规范场可使高斯光束的渠道化程度相比仅基于等频轮廓群速度的描述提升十倍。

Conclusion: 空间动力学与极化赝旋进的耦合对渠道化效应有显著增强作用，非阿贝尔规范场框架能够准确描述这一动力学过程，为设计更高效的光束操控器件提供了新思路。

Abstract: Hyperbolic and quasi-flat isofrequency contours (IFCs) are used for beam canalization and can be created by tilted Dirac points in photonic systems. Dirac points in microcavities are generated by the combination of transverse-electric/transverse-magnetic splitting and linear birefringence. We show that the canalization is here strongly assisted by the coupling between the spatial dynamics and polarization pseudospin precession. This dynamics is well described analytically and numerically as the action of a non-Abelian gauge field on emergent charges (spin current). We demonstrate a ten-fold enhancement of the canalization for a Gaussian beam by the gauge field, as compared to a description based solely on the group velocity associated with the IFCs.

</details>


### [129] [Bogoliubov mode dynamics and non-adiabatic transitions in time-varying condensed media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03087)
*A. M. Tishin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究提出一个无量纲参数作为普适量度，量化凝聚态介质（condensed media）中亚稳态到非绝热波动的转变，并在扩展玻色基中数值验证了该框架区分不同绝热与非绝热体系的有效性，建立了一个普适标度律（scaling law），为超越传统衍射极限的快速集体激发探测提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有框架难以统一量化凝聚态介质中亚稳态（adiabatic stability）向谱混沌（spectral chaos）的跃迁，缺乏通用的度规来识别亚波长不均匀性（sub-wavelength inhomogeneities）引发的非绝热动力学。

Method: 引入一个无量纲参数作为普适量度，将缺陷视为绝热性破坏的局域位点，触发基态的非绝热参数激发（non-adiabatic parametric excitation）。在扩展至50级玻色基（bosonic basis）中进行数值验证，并通过非绝热性-调控比（non-adiabaticity-to-regulation ratio）建立标度律。

Result: 该框架在ENZ超材料（ENZ-metamaterials）与超快磁性介质中准确区分绝热与非绝热区域；极端负载下观测到计算奇点（computational singularities），标定了相干模式混合的严格操作边界。数值结果验证了该度规在不同材料类别中的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该工作为动态希尔伯特空间截断（dynamic Hilbert space truncation）提供了严格的物理依据，实现了类费米子有效动力学（effective fermion-like dynamics），为探测超快集体激发和潜在内应力提供了超越传统衍射极限的理论基础。

Abstract: This study investigates non-adiabatic wave dynamics in condensed media and the transition from adiabatic stability to spectral chaos. We introduce a dimensionless parameter, as a universal metric to quantify phase-mode redistribution at sub-wavelength inhomogeneities. Our framework treats defects as localized sites of adiabaticity violation triggering non-adiabatic parametric excitation of the ground state. Numerical validation in an expanded 50-level bosonic basis demonstrates that the framework accurately distinguishes between adiabatic regimes in ENZ-metamaterials and non-adiabatic transitions in ultrafast magnetic media . We establish a universal scaling law governed by the non-adiabaticity-to-regulation ratio, proving that the proposed metric remains a robust metrological tool for identifying sub-wavelength inhomogeneities across diverse material classes. Computational singularities observed at extreme loads identify the rigorous operational boundaries for coherent mode-mixing. The robustness of the proposed framework is numerically validated, proving the method's reliability for a wide class of non-linear condensed media satisfying the stability criterion. This result provides a rigorous physical justification for the dynamic Hilbert space truncation (effective fermion-like dynamics), ensuring metrological consistency in complex structural environments. These results provide a theoretical foundation for probing ultrafast collective excitations and latent internal stresses, extending structural analysis beyond the traditional diffraction barrier.

</details>


### [130] [Thermal bottleneck in a freely suspended superconducting island on InAs nanowire](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03139)
*E. V. Shpagina,E. S. Tikhonov,D. Ruhstorfer,G. Koblmueller,V. S. Khrapai*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过焦耳光谱学（Joule spectroscopy）方法，测量悬浮外延Al/InAs纳米线（nanowires, NWs）中超导岛（S-island）的热平衡，发现周围3He bath导致显著的声子加热和热弛豫瓶颈（thermal relaxation bottleneck），揭示了环境冷却在非平衡超导实验中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导岛（superconducting islands）在纳米线器件中的非平衡热平衡机制尚不明确，特别是环境冷却对超导-正常态转变的影响未被充分理解。

Method: 采用焦耳光谱学（Joule spectroscopy）追踪超导岛中的超导-正常态转变，通过输运电流加热邻近InAs纳米线段实现；利用邻近的介观加热器（mesoscopic heaters）改变周围3He bath的温度，并用纳米线Johnson噪声测温法（Johnson noise thermometry）进行控制。

Result: 实验发现存在显著的与周围3He冷却相关的热弛豫瓶颈（thermal relaxation bottleneck），导致超导岛中出现声子加热（phonon heating）现象。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了环境冷却在纳米线器件超导岛的非平衡实验中起到关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate the heat balance in superconducting islands (S-islands) formed in epitaxial Al/InAs nanowires (NWs) freely suspended above the substrate. We employ a Joule spectroscopy approach, which traces the superconductor-normal transition in the S-island mediated by heating of the neighboring InAs NW segments via transport current. The temperature of the surrounding 3He bath is varied with nearby mesoscopic heaters and controlled with the NW Johnson noise thermometry. The experiment reveals a substantial thermal relaxation bottleneck associated with the cooling via surrounding 3He, which gives rise to phonon heating in the S-island. Our results uncover the role of environmental cooling in non-equilibrium experiments in S-islands in NW devices.

</details>


### [131] [Time-boundary scattering and topological resonant transmissions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03325)
*Haiping Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个时间边界（time boundary, TB）的布洛赫波散射理论，引入时间散射矩阵 S 连接入射与出射布洛赫通道，发现了拓扑共振传输（resonant transmission, RT）现象，并建立了体-时间-边界对应关系（bulk-time-boundary correspondence），将时间与空间散射置于统一框架下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间边界作为空间界面的时间类比物，为操控量子系统提供了有力工具，但缺乏像空间界面散射那样统一的理论框架。现有研究缺少一个适用于时间边界的量子散射统一理论。

Method: 通过引入时间散射矩阵（temporal scattering matrix）$S$ 将入射和出射布洛赫通道（Bloch channels）连接起来，建立了时间边界的布洛赫波散射理论；对全部整数 Altland-Zirnbauer 对称类建立了体-时间-边界对应关系，并进行了拓扑分析以揭示维度依赖性。

Result: 发现了拓扑共振传输——$S$ 矩阵的极点（poles），可产生完美的带间传输（interband transmission）和量子态的动态冻结（dynamical freezing）。在一维情形下导出了时间域的 Levinson 定理。偶数维中 RT 对时间调制和无序具有鲁棒性，而奇数维中 RT 可被动力学对称性破缺破坏。

Conclusion: 该工作将时间散射与空间散射置于同等地位，为工程化与探测量子动力学开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Time boundaries (TBs), temporal analogues of spatial interfaces, offer a powerful handle to engineer quantum systems. However, unlike the well-developed stationary scattering theory at spatial interfaces, a unified framework for quantum scattering at TBs has been missing. Here we develop a Bloch-wave scattering theory for TBs by introducing a temporal scattering matrix $S$ between incoming and outgoing Bloch channels. We uncover topological resonant transmissions (RTs) -- poles of $S$ that yield perfect interband transmission and dynamical freezing of the quantum state. We establish a bulk-time-boundary correspondence for all integer Altland-Zirnbauer classes: the number of RTs equals the jump of the bulk topological invariant across the TB. In one dimension this gives a time-domain Levinson's theorem. A topological analysis further reveals a striking dimensional dependence. In even dimensions RTs are robust to temporal modulations and disorder, whereas in odd dimensions they can be destroyed by dynamical symmetry breaking. Our work places temporal and spatial scattering on the same footing and opens new avenues for engineering and probing quantum dynamics.

</details>


### [132] [Cubic edge dispersion in a semi-Dirac Chern insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03459)
*Marta García Olmos,David Martín Tejedor,Mario Amado,Yuriko Baba,Rafael A. Molina*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发现陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）中拓扑边缘态（topological edge state）的色散关系不一定呈现标准狄拉克（Dirac）型线性行为。通过构建一个半狄拉克（semi-Dirac）陈绝缘体的最小两带晶格模型，理论推导并数值验证了其手性边缘态（chiral edge state）在低能下具有$E(k)\propto k^3$的立方色散，证明了非常规体带结构可以产生性质不同的边界激发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为陈绝缘体的拓扑边缘态继承自体哈密顿量的狄拉克结构，表现为线性色散。本文试图突破这一范式，探索具有各向异性半狄拉克能带结构的系统中是否存在根本不同的边缘态行为。

Method: 设计了一个最小两带晶格模型来实现半狄拉克陈绝缘体；解析计算了其拓扑相图；采用半无穷大几何中的质量畴壁（mass-domain-wall）方法推导了手性边缘态的显式表达式；通过对应紧束缚（tight-binding）条带的数值对角化验证了解析结果。

Result: 该半狄拉克陈绝缘体的手性边缘态在低能下的色散关系与动量呈立方关系，$E(k)\propto k^3$，而非传统预期的线性关系。数值对角化结果与解析预测一致。

Conclusion: 非常规的体带结构可以产生性质上不同的边界激发，为在拓扑材料与合成量子系统中实现非标准手性边缘动力学提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: Topological edge states in Chern insulators are typically characterized by a linear dispersion relation inherited from the Dirac structure of the bulk Hamiltonian. Here we show that this paradigm can be fundamentally altered in systems with anisotropic semi-Dirac band structures. We introduce a minimal two-band lattice model realizing a semi-Dirac Chern insulator and determine its topological phase diagram analytically. Using a mass-domain-wall approach in a semi-infinite geometry, we derive an explicit expression for the chiral edge states and find that their low-energy dispersion scales cubically with momentum, $E(k)\propto k^3$. Numerical diagonalization of the corresponding tight-binding ribbon confirms the analytical prediction. Our results demonstrate that unconventional bulk band structures can produce qualitatively different boundary excitations, providing a route to engineering nonstandard chiral edge dynamics in topological materials and synthetic quantum systems.

</details>


### [133] [First-principles prediction of chiral-phonon-induced orbital accumulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03486)
*A. Pezo,A. Manchon,Y. Nii,K. Ando,T. Kato*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过第一性原理计算，证明手性声子（chiral phonons）在金属中可通过晶格相干运动产生轨道积累（orbital accumulation），并经由自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）伴随产生较小的自旋积累。结果表明，该响应主要由轨道特征、近简并态（near-degeneracies）和电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）控制，而非单纯依赖自旋-轨道耦合，并指出轻过渡金属是实现手性声子驱动轨道学（orbitronics）的理想平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性声子为无需依赖磁序即可传递角动量提供了途径，但金属中手性声子的电子响应（electronic response）在超越自旋基（spin-based）视角之外仍未被充分理解。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），在长波极限（long-wavelength limit）下直接从应变微扰的从头算哈密顿量（strain perturbed ab initio Hamiltonians）中评估轨道和自旋期望值，其中声子微扰由对称性适配的圆偏振晶格畸变（symmetry adapted circular lattice distortions）表示。

Result: 相干手性晶格运动产生轨道积累，并通过自旋-轨道耦合伴随产生较小的自旋积累。响应主要由轨道特征、近简并态和电子-声子耦合控制，而非仅由自旋-轨道耦合主导。

Conclusion: 轻过渡金属（light transition metals）被识别为实现手性声子驱动轨道学的有前景的平台。

Abstract: Chiral phonons offer a route to transfer angular momentum without relying on magnetic order, but their electronic response in metals remains poorly understood from perspectives beyond spin-based scenarios. Using first-principles calculations, we show that coherent chiral lattice motion generates orbital accumulation and, through spin-orbit coupling, a smaller accompanying spin accumulation. Our approach evaluates orbital and spin expectation values directly from strain perturbed ab initio Hamiltonians in the long-wavelength limit, where the phonon perturbation is represented by symmetry adapted circular lattice distortions. We show that the response is controlled mainly by orbital character, near-degeneracies, and electron-phonon coupling, rather than by spin-orbit coupling alone. These results identify light transition metals as promising platforms for chiral-phonon-driven orbitronics.

</details>

Result: 找到了T形和X形线状交叉（wire crossings）的透射率表达式。

Abstract: The transmittance of intersection between narrow quantum strips is studied. It is assumed that strip widths are less than the electron wavelength, so that they are tunnel conductors. In this assumption the Schrödinger equation is reduced to the Laplace one, which can be solved by the conformal mappings. The transmittances of T-like and X-like wire crossings are found.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示磁场（Abelian规范场）与自旋轨道相互作用（non-Abelian规范场）在二维网络量子输运中的协同效应，理解阿贝尔与非阿贝尔规范场耦合如何影响电导行为。

Method: 理论分析和数值计算相结合，研究二维网络中磁场与自旋轨道作用下的量子电荷输运；对扩散区中呈对数发散的弱（反）局域化（weak-(anti)localization）修正进行分类。

Abstract: We study quantum charge transport in two-dimensional networks in the presence of a magnetic field and spin-orbit interaction. The interplay of the corresponding Abelian and non-Abelian gauge fields leads to an intricate behavior of the conductance, which has different periodicities in the diffusive and ballistic regimes. We classify all configurations of magnetic and spin-orbit fields where a logarithmically divergent weak-(anti)localization correction appears in the diffusive regime. The conductivity of topologically distinct configurations is the same in the diffusive regime but different in the ballistic regime. The proposed setup provides a feasible realization of quantum graphs with non-Abelian gauge fields.

### [136] [Remote entropy measurement in coupled quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03876)
*Owen Sheekey,Tim Child,Elena Cornick,Saeed Fallahi,Geoffrey C. Gardner,Michael J. Manfra,Eran Sela,Yaakov Kleeorin,Yigal Meir,Silvia Lüscher,Joshua Folk*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过实验证明，基于麦克斯韦关系（Maxwell relation）的测量方法不仅能够探测添加电子本身的熵变，还能探测周围系统响应该电子时产生的熵变。利用一对电容耦合的GaAs量子点（quantum dots），作者展示了在弱耦合与强耦合两种条件下，对单个量子点的电荷测量能够揭示整个双量子点系统的熵变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有实验证明，测量向半导体或石墨烯量子点添加电子时的熵变，可以准确量化所填充状态的旋简并和轨道简并（spin and orbital degeneracy），但测量更奇异的熵（exotic entropies）则需要探测整个系统在添加粒子时所发生的熵变。

Method: 基于麦克斯韦关系（Maxwell relation）的测量方法，使用一对电容耦合的GaAs量子点，通过对其中一个量子点进行电荷测量来推断整个双量子点系统的熵变。实验覆盖了弱耦合（weak coupling）和强耦合（strong coupling）两种区间，后者需要借助数值重整化群（numerical renormalization group）计算进行解释。

Result: 在弱耦合区间，可用微状态计数（microstate counting）解释熵变；在强耦合区间，则需要数值重整化群（numerical renormalization group）计算才能描述系统的响应行为。

Conclusion: 基于麦克斯韦关系的测量方法能有效探测整个系统对添加粒子的响应熵变，拓展了熵测量在量子点系统中的应用范围。

Abstract: Recent experiments have demonstrated that measurements of the entropy change associated with the addition of electrons to semiconductor- and graphene-based quantum dots accurately quantify the spin and orbital degeneracy of the states into which they are added. However, measuring more exotic entropies requires probing the entropy change of an entire system in response to an added particle. Here, we demonstrate that Maxwell relation-based measurements probe not only the entropy change associated with the added electron but also that of the surrounding system as it responds to that electron. Using a pair of capacitively coupled GaAs quantum dots, we show that charge measurements on one dot reveal entropy changes associated with the entire two-dot system, both at weak dot--reservoir coupling where microstate counting applies and at stronger coupling where numerical renormalization group calculations are required.

</details>


### [137] [Quantum Metric Localization and Quantum Metric Protection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03987)
*Wen-Bo Dai,Jinchao Zhao,Shuai A. Chen,K. T. Law*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发现，在具有量子度量（quantum metric）的孤立能带中，传统安德森局域化（Anderson localization）范式失效：局域化长度（localization length）不再随无序强度增加而单调递减，而是在约两倍量子度量长度处形成平台，称为量子度量局域化（quantum metric localization） regime，并表现出量子度量保护（quantum metric protection）效应，该现象在1D Lieb晶格中通过数值计算、Wannier函数物理解释和超对称场论（supersymmetric field theory）方法得到阐明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统认知认为电子系统无序效应中，安德森局域化长度随无序强度增大而单调递减。本文旨在考察具有量子度量的孤立能带是否仍遵从这一范式，并揭示可能的新局域化行为。

Method: 首先通过1D Lieb晶格进行数值计算演示量子度量局域化现象；随后基于Wannier函数（Wannier functions）性质给出局域化长度平台的简单物理解释；最后采用超对称场论（supersymmetric field theory）方法解释局域化长度为何约为两倍量子度量长度，并刻画从安德森局域化到量子度量局域化的交叉（crossover）。

Result: 对于具有有限带宽且与其他能带相隔能隙Δ的孤立能带，弱无序下表现为常规安德森局域化；随无序增强，局域化长度不再下降，而是稳定在约两倍量子度量长度处，形成局域化长度平台（localization length plateau）；该平台一直维持到无序强度远超Δ为止。

Conclusion: 本文提出了量子度量局域化和量子度量保护的概念，证明了传统安德森局域化范式在具有量子度量的孤立能带中完全失效。该结论广泛适用于无序电子、光子（photonic）和声学（acoustic）系统。

Abstract: The study of disorder effects in electronic systems is one of the central themes in physics. It is well established that in the Anderson localization regime, the localization length of electrons decreases monotonically as the disorder strength increases. Here, we demonstrate that the conventional Anderson localization paradigm fails completely in describing an isolated band with quantum metric, where the quantum metric of the band defines a length scale called the quantum metric length. For an isolated band with a finite bandwidth separated from other bands by a band gap $Δ$, weak disorder results in conventional Anderson localization behavior. However, as the disorder increases, the localization length ceases to decrease and becomes pinned at a value approximately twice the quantum metric length, forming a localization length plateau. We term the regime within this localization length plateau as the quantum metric localization regime. Remarkably, the localization length does not deviate from the plateau until the disorder strength far exceeds $Δ$. We refer to this strong protection against disorder, characterized by the quantum metric length, as quantum metric protection. In this work, we first numerically demonstrate quantum metric localization using a 1D Lieb lattice. We then provide a simple physical picture based on the properties of Wannier functions to explain the origin of the localization length plateau. A supersymmetric field theory approach explains why the localization length is approximately twice the quantum metric length and captures the crossover from Anderson localization to quantum metric localization. Our conclusions are broadly applicable to disordered electronic, photonic, and acoustic systems.

</details>

### [138] [Weyl Cosserat Elasticity and Gravitational Memory: An Effective Microstructured Model of Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02975)
*David Izabel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了真空广义相对论中Weyl张量的电/磁部分与微极性（Cosserat）弹性介质运动学之间的数学对应，将引力记忆（gravitational memory）重新解释为时空中的位错场（dislocation field）拓扑荷，并构造了扩展的Einstein-Cartan理论有效作用量以描述传播中的挠率模（torsion modes）。该框架是经典广义相对论的有效粗粒化描述而非修改，并讨论了其观测可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在经典广义相对论（general relativity）中，引力记忆效应（位移记忆与自旋记忆）的物理解释仍缺乏统一的几何-拓扑图像。本文旨在通过将时空几何与连续介质力学中的位错理论（dislocation theory）建立严格对应，为引力记忆提供一种拓扑场论视角，同时避免对广义相对论本身进行实质性修改。

Method: 首先在真空广义相对论中建立Weyl张量（Weyl tensor）的电/磁部分与微极性弹性介质（Cosserat continuum）运动学量之间的数学对应。然后利用Bianchi恒等式（Bianchi identities）和测地偏离方程（geodesic deviation equation）导出该对应关系的具体形式。最后在Einstein-Cartan理论框架下构造扩展有效作用量，以描述传播中的挠率模。

Result: 位移记忆（displacement memory）对应于具有非平凡Burgers矢量（Burgers vector）的刃型位错（edge dislocation）；自旋记忆（spin memory）对应于与旋转失配相关的螺型位错（screw dislocation）。整体框架被证明是一种有效的粗粒化描述（coarse-grained description），而非对经典广义相对论的修改。

Conclusion: 该对应为引力记忆效应提供了基于拓扑荷的位错场解释，并指出传播挠率模在观测上具有可行性。然而摘要未明确说明具体的观测途径或数值预测，需进一步研究以验证其可检验性。

Abstract: We construct a mathematically controlled correspondence between the electric and magnetic parts of the Weyl tensor in vacuum general relativity and the kinematics of a micropolar (Cosserat) elastic medium. In this framework, gravitational memory is reinterpreted as the topological charge of an effective dislocation field in spacetime. The ordinary displacement memory corresponds to an edge dislocation characterized by a non trivial Burgers vector, while spin memory corresponds to a screw type defect associated with rotational mismatch. We formulate the correspondence explicitly, derive it from the Bianchi identities and the geodesic deviation equation, and construct an effective Lagrangian extension of Einstein Cartan theory describing propagating torsion modes. The framework is shown to be an effective coarse-grained description rather than a modification of classical GR, and we discuss its observational viability.

</details>


### [139] [Orbital Nodal Phase as a Pipeline Invariant in Black Hole Timing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02984)
*Mehmet Baran Ökten*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对吸积黑洞（accreting black holes）的节点时标分析（nodal timing analysis）中依赖约定选择的问题，为略微倾斜的圆形环（slightly tilted circular rings）定义了轨道节点相位（orbital nodal phase）$Δψ_{\rm orb}$，该量在Kerr时空中与每轨道的节点进动（nodal precession per orbit）一致，单调依赖于半径，并建立了固定轨道角速度（fixed-$Ω_φ$）输运框架，提供了不依赖于管道的稳健报告量与Kerr基线诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有吸积黑洞的时标分析（timing analyses）在处理节点信息（nodal information）时，其结果依赖于时间和方位角约定（time and azimuthal convention）的人为选择，导致不同管道（pipeline）之间的结果难以直接比较。因此，需要识别并定义一个不依赖于这些约定选择的管道不变内容（pipeline-invariant content），以实现客观的物理诊断。

Method: 本文将吸积流建模为略微倾斜的圆形环（slightly tilted circular rings），在Kerr时空背景下推导出轨道节点相位（orbital nodal phase）$Δψ_{\rm orb}$，证明其与每轨道的节点进动值等价，并论证其对所考虑的良性重映射（benign remappings）具有不变性。进而建立固定轨道角速度（fixed-$Ω_φ$）输运框架，将纯粹的度规敏感性（metric sensitivity）与半径漂移（radius drift）分离。

Result: $Δψ_{\rm orb}$在Kerr时空中对顺行自旋（prograde Kerr spin）在稳定圆轨道之外随半径单调递减；固定-$Ω_φ$输运框架为远场四极（far-field quadrupolar）及更高多极（higher-multipolar）时标响应计算提供了自然框架；识别了两个分析级效应：来自相干径向呼吸（coherent radial breathing）的二阶偏差（second-order bias），以及精确慢速固定-$Ω_φ$环（exact slow fixed-$Ω_φ$ loops）无内禀几何偏移（intrinsic geometric offset）。对GRO J1655$-$40的观测数据验证表明，一旦指定轨道频率锚点（orbital-frequency anchor）和标识约定（identification convention），$Δψ_{\rm orb}$的观测代理量可直接从标准报道的准周期振荡频率（quasi-periodic oscillation frequencies）重构。

Conclusion: 在薄环极限（thin-ring limit）下，$Δψ_{\rm orb}$可作为管道稳健的报告量（pipeline-robust reporting quantity）和Kerr基线诊断（Kerr-baseline diagnostic），适用于源级别（source-level）、模拟级别（simulation-level）和强引力（strong-gravity）对比应用。

Abstract: Timing analyses of accreting black holes often package nodal information in ways that depend on benign choices of time and azimuthal convention. We identify the corresponding pipeline-invariant content for slightly tilted circular rings and express it as an orbital nodal phase, $Δψ_{\rm orb}$. In Kerr, this quantity gives the clean geodesic baseline for nodal timing: it equals the nodal precession per orbit, is invariant under the benign remappings considered here, and, for prograde Kerr spin, decreases monotonically with radius outside the innermost stable circular orbit. A fixed-$Ω_φ$ transport framework then isolates genuine metric sensitivity from trivial radius drift and provides the natural framework for far-field quadrupolar and higher-multipolar timing-response calculations. Two small analysis-level effects are also identified, namely a second-order bias from coherent radial breathing and the absence of an intrinsic geometric offset from exact slow fixed-$Ω_φ$ loops. A limited published-data illustration for GRO J1655$-$40 shows that the observational proxy for $Δψ_{\rm orb}$ can be reconstructed directly from standard reported quasi-periodic oscillation frequencies once an orbital-frequency anchor and an identification convention are specified. Within the thin-ring limit, $Δψ_{\rm orb}$ therefore provides a pipeline-robust reporting quantity and a Kerr-baseline diagnostic for source-level, simulation-level, and strong-gravity comparison applications.

</details>


### [140] [Polarized Equatorial Emission around Kerr Black Holes with Synchronized Scalar Hair. I. Direct images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03006)
*Valentin O. Deliyski,Galin N. Gyulchev,Daniela D. Doneva,Petya G. Nedkova,Stoytcho S. Yazadjiev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文分析围绕带有同步玻色子毛发（synchronized bosonic hair）的旋转克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）的几何薄吸积盘（geometrically thin accretion disk）直接成像的偏振特性，发现偏振矢量的扭曲出现相位偏移，且标量场最弱的解反而偏移最大，表明偏振观测主要受局部几何与传输效应影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究标量场（scalar field）存在下，旋转黑洞周围时空测地线结构（geodesic structure）的改变如何影响近黑洞区域辐射的偏振信号，从而检验偏振观测能否区分克尔黑洞与带有标量毛发的黑洞模型。

Method: 采用几何薄吸积盘的简单解析模型（analytical model），假设盘位于赤道面并发射同步辐射（synchrotron radiation），计算完全自洽的旋转克尔黑洞（带有同步玻色子毛发）的直接像偏振。

Result: 标量场的存在导致偏振矢量扭曲出现相位偏移（dephasing），且标量化最弱的解偏移反而更大。赤道面磁场（equatorial magnetic field）产生的偏振模式与广义相对论中的克尔黑洞定性相似，但高观测倾角下的垂直磁场（vertical magnetic field）可导致偏振矢量扭曲方向的特征性反转（characteristic reversal）。

Conclusion: 偏振可观测量的敏感性主要源于沿光子路径的局部几何与传输效应（local geometric and transport effects），而非全局标量场强度；垂直磁场在高倾角下的偏振反转可作为区分此类黑洞模型的关键观测特征。

Abstract: We investigate the polarization properties of the direct images of a geometrically and optically thin accretion disk around fully self-consistent models of rotating Kerr black holes with synchronized bosonic hair. The presence of a massive scalar field alters the geodesic structure of the spacetime and thus leaves an imprint on the polarization of radiation emitted near the black hole horizon. To study this effect, we employ a simple analytical model of a geometrically thin accretion disk, orbiting in the equatorial plane and emitting synchrotron radiation. The main deviation from a corresponding Kerr black hole in general relativity is found to be a dephasing in the twist of the polarization vector, which is surprisingly larger for the least scalarized solutions we consider. This behavior suggests that polarization observables are primarily sensitive to local geometric and transport effects along photon trajectories rather than to the overall scalar field strength. Furthermore, our results demonstrate that while equatorial magnetic fields produce qualitatively similar polarization patterns to Kerr black holes in general relativity, vertical magnetic fields at high observer inclinations can lead to a characteristic reversal of the twist direction of the polarization vector.

### [141] [Gravitational electric-magnetic duality at the light ring and quasinormal mode isospectrality in effective field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03018)
*Ibrahima Bah,Emanuele Berti,Valerio De Luca,Bogdan Ganchev,David Pereñiguez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过研究平面波时空中的引力电-磁对偶性（electric-magnetic duality），揭示了该对偶性是在高频（eikonal）极限下黑洞拟正规膜（quasinormal modes）等谱性（isospectrality）的物理组织原理，并证明要求该对偶性在含高阶导数修正的引力理论中成立可约束耦合常数，从而保持等谱性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论中，宇称偶（parity-even）与宇称奇（parity-odd）的拟正规膜谱是简并的，即具有等谱性；但超越广义相对论的修正通常会破坏这一性质。近期发现某些高阶导数算符在高频（eikonal）极限下仍能保持等谱性，但其背后的物理机制尚不明确。本文旨在揭示该现象的组织原理。

Method: 作者利用光环（light ring）的彭罗斯极限（Penrose limit）与高频极限之间的关联，将研究聚焦于一类平面波时空（plane-wave spacetimes）。在此类背景上，对广义相对论中的动力学度规涨落（dynamical metric fluctuations）进行分析，发现其存在引力电-磁对偶性，该对偶性强制了等谱性。进而，要求该对偶性在存在高阶导数修正时依然成立，从而导出对耦合常数的约束条件。

Result: 广义相对论中，平面波背景上的度规涨落确实满足引力电-磁对偶性，该对偶性是等谱性的成因。将这一对偶性作为判据，可筛选出那些在高频极限下保持等谱性的高阶导数修正，从而为已有发现提供统一解释。

Conclusion: 光环处的引力电-磁对偶性是高频极限下等谱性的组织原理（organizing principle）。作者推测，对于其他满足该对偶性的广义相对论修正理论，这一结论同样成立。

Abstract: Black hole perturbations are characterized by a superposition of damped exponentials known as quasinormal modes. In general relativity, the spectra of parity-even and parity-odd quasinormal modes coincide -- a property known as isospectrality, which is typically broken by corrections beyond general relativity. Recently, certain higher-derivative operators were shown to preserve isospectrality in the high-frequency (eikonal) regime. Motivated by the relation between the light ring Penrose limit and the eikonal limit, we study isospectrality in a class of plane-wave spacetimes. In general relativity, we show that dynamical metric fluctuations on these backgrounds admit a gravitational analog of electric-magnetic duality, which enforces isospectrality. Requiring this duality to persist in the presence of higher-derivative corrections constrains the couplings so that isospectrality is preserved. We conclude that gravitational electric-magnetic duality at the light ring is the organizing principle behind isospectrality in the eikonal limit, and we conjecture that this remains true for other duality-invariant corrections to general relativity.

</details>

*Shauvik Biswas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在 $R=0$ 时空中研究了虫洞（wormhole）解的一个特例，通过近似解析计算发现，在严格静态轴向引力扰动下，若将主方程的解保留至几何正规化参数（regularisation parameter）的线性阶，磁型潮汐洛夫数（magnetic-type tidal Love number, $\ell=2$）为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虫洞（wormhole）作为黑洞几何（black hole geometries）的有趣替代方案，其引力响应性质尚未被充分探索。本文旨在研究特定虫洞解在静态轴向引力扰动下的潮汐洛夫数（tidal Love number）行为。

Method: 采用近似解析计算方法，在 $R=0$ 时空背景下考虑一个特殊的虫洞解，施加严格静态轴向引力扰动（strictly static axial gravitational perturbation），并将主方程的解展开至几何正规化参数（regularisation parameter）的线性阶。

Result: 对于 $\ell=2$ 的多极矩，磁型潮汐洛夫数（magnetic-type tidal Love number）在保留至正规化参数线性阶时为零。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，在该特定虫洞几何中，线性阶近似下磁型潮汐洛夫数的消失可能反映了虫洞结构与黑洞在潮汐响应上的某种相似性或特殊对称性。

Abstract: Wormholes are fascinating alternatives to black hole geometries. In this paper, we have studied a special case of wormhole solution in the context of $R=0$ spacetime. Our approximate analytical calculations show that under a strictly static axial gravitational perturbation of this spacetime, the magnetic-type tidal Love number (for $\ell=2$) vanishes if we keep the solution of the master equation up to linear order in the regularisation parameter of the geometry.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验正则黑洞（regular black hole）中不同自旋场（标量场、电磁场、狄拉克场）的散射特性，并验证准正规模与灰体因子之间的对应关系（QNM/GBF correspondence）在黑洞分支下的适用性。

Method: 采用六阶WKB方法（6th-order WKB treatment）处理单势垒有效势（single-barrier effective potential）下的散射问题，直接计算灰体因子，并将其与从最低准正规模（lowest quasinormal modes）重构的结果进行比较。

Result: 增大正则参数会降低有效势垒高度，将透射谱移至更低频率，并增强所有三个场扇区的吸收截面。直接WKB计算与准正规模重构的灰体因子之间吻合良好，典型误差在$10^{-2}$量级或更优。

Conclusion: 在由幻影D-B-I标量场支撑的正则黑洞几何中，准正规模/灰体因子对应关系成立且精度较高，验证了该对应关系的可靠性与普适性。

Abstract: We study grey-body factors and absorption cross sections for massless scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac fields in the exact asymptotically flat regular black-hole geometry supported by a phantom Dirac--Born--Infeld scalar. In the black-hole branch all three sectors are governed by single-barrier effective potentials, which allows a direct 6th-order WKB treatment of the scattering problem and a comparison with the recent quasinormal-mode/grey-body-factor correspondence. We show that increasing the regularity parameter lowers the barriers, shifts transmission to lower frequencies, and enhances the absorption cross sections in all three sectors. By comparing the direct WKB grey-body factors with those reconstructed from the lowest quasinormal modes, we explicitly test the QNM/GBF correspondence and find good agreement, typically at the level of $10^{-2}$ or better.

### [144] [Stability of Synthetic Timelike Ricci Bounds under $C^0$-Limits and Applications to Impulsive Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03172)
*Andrea Mondino,Vanessa Ryborz,Clemens Sämann*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了在全局双曲性（global hyperbolicity）一致假设下，类时Ricci曲率下界在洛伦兹度量（Lorentzian metrics）的低正则性极限下具有稳定性，并以此为基础研究了脉冲引力波（impulsive gravitational waves）等低正则性时空的合成曲率-维数条件，揭示了黎曼与洛伦兹几何在曲率下界理论上的根本差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究类时Ricci曲率下界（timelike Ricci curvature lower bounds）在洛伦兹度量低正则性极限下的稳定性，旨在理解低正则性爱因斯坦方程解（如脉冲引力波）的几何性质，并检验黎曼几何中经典分裂定理（splitting theorems）在洛伦兹框架下的可推广性。

Method: 利用洛伦兹最优传输（Lorentzian optimal transport）框架，基于合成曲率-维数条件TCD^e_p(K,N)构造具有类时Ricci下界的光滑逼近，分析其在局部一致收敛下的极限行为，从而证明稳定性定理。

Result: 证明了在全局双曲性一致假设下，TCD^e_p(K,N)条件在光滑洛伦兹度量局部一致收敛下的稳定性；发现光滑真空时空的局部一致极限仍满足强能量条件（strong energy condition）；构造了满足合成类时Ricci曲率下界的大类脉冲引力波，并在闵可夫斯基背景下建立了合成上Ricci曲率界；证明了Eschenburg-Galloway-Newman洛伦兹分裂定理和Cheeger-Colding几乎分裂定理的直接洛伦兹类比均不成立。

Conclusion: 该研究为低正则性爱因斯坦方程解提供了新的几何洞见，揭示了黎曼与洛伦兹几何在下Ricci曲率界理论上的根本差异；稳定性定理还可应用于脉冲引力波非线性相互作用产生的爱因斯坦方程弱解。

Abstract: We investigate the stability of timelike Ricci curvature lower bounds under low-regularity limits of Lorentzian metrics. Specifically, we prove that the synthetic curvature-dimension condition $TCD^e_p(K,N)$, which provides an optimal transport formulation of the Hawking-Penrose strong energy condition, is stable under locally uniform convergence of smooth Lorentzian metrics, provided a uniform global hyperbolicity assumption holds. As a consequence, smooth locally uniform limits of vacuum spacetimes satisfy the strong energy condition, even though curvature is not controlled a priori. As a main application, we study impulsive gravitational waves - spacetimes with Lipschitz continuous metrics - and show that large classes of such waves satisfy synthetic timelike Ricci curvature lower bounds. In the case of Minkowski background, we further establish synthetic upper Ricci curvature bounds. Our approach relies on constructing suitable smooth approximations with lower bounds on the timelike Ricci, and analyzing the limiting behavior via Lorentzian optimal transport. These results yield new geometric insights into low-regularity solutions of the Einstein equations and, in particular, provide a counterexample to the extension of the Eschenburg-Galloway-Newman Lorentzian splitting theorem to infinitesimally Minkowskian $TCD^e_p(0,N)$ Lorentzian length spaces. Moreover, our construction shows that a direct Lorentzian analogue of the Cheeger-Colding almost splitting theorem - under assumptions of almost non-negative timelike Ricci curvature and the existence of an almost maximizing line - cannot hold. This highlights a fundamental difference between the geometry of Riemannian and Lorentzian lower Ricci curvature bounds. We also apply the aforementioned stability theorem to weak solutions of the Einstein equations arising from the nonlinear interaction of impulsive gravitational waves.

### [145] [Non-radial pulsations of gravitationally coupled two-fluid neutron stars in general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03305)
*Ankit Kumar,Daniel A. Caballero,Hajime Sotani,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个完全广义相对论（general relativistic）框架，用于分析引力耦合双流体中子星（two-fluid neutron stars）的极向扰动（polar perturbations），推导了耦合线性扰动方程并建立数值实现，为相对论星震学（relativistic asteroseismology）向多流体致密星（multi-fluid compact stars）拓展奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星的非径向振荡（non-radial oscillations）是探测恒星结构和相对论性引力的有力手段，但此前缺乏对于具有独立守恒流（independently conserved currents）的引力耦合双流体恒星的全广义相对论处理。

Method: 假设两种流体仅通过公共时空（common spacetime）发生引力相互作用，不涉及熵曳（entrainment）或直接微观物理耦合；推导了度规（metric）与两种流体分量的耦合线性扰动方程，并建立了正则性（regularity）、表面（surface）和外匹配（exterior matching）条件以构成适定的振荡本征值问题（well-posed oscillation eigenvalue problem），最终通过数值方法实现极向模谱（polar mode spectra）的计算。

Result: 成功实现了引力耦合双流体恒星模型的极向模谱数值计算，能够依据本征函数（eigenfunctions）及其节点结构（node structure），将频谱中的基模（fundamental mode, f-mode）和压力模（pressure mode, p-mode）分支按主导的内/外流体特性进行分类。

Conclusion: 所发展的形式为将相对论星震学拓展至多流体致密星提供基础，并支持在全广义相对论框架下探索其潜在引力波特征（gravitational-wave signatures）。

Abstract: Non-radial oscillations of neutron stars provide a powerful probe of stellar structure and relativistic gravity, but a fully general relativistic treatment for gravitationally coupled two-fluid stars with independently conserved currents has so far been lacking. In this work, we develop a fully relativistic framework for polar perturbations of gravitationally coupled two-fluid neutron stars, assuming that the two fluids interact only through the common spacetime and are not coupled by entrainment or direct microphysical interactions. We derive the coupled linear perturbation equations governing the metric and both fluid components, and complete the formulation by establishing the regularity, surface, and exterior matching conditions required for a well-posed oscillation eigenvalue problem. We then implement the resulting system numerically and compute representative polar mode spectra for gravitationally coupled two-fluid stellar models. This implementation provides a practical way to address mode identification in gravitationally coupled two-fluid stars, allowing the fundamental ($\mathsf{f}$) and pressure ($\mathsf{p}$) mode branches of the spectrum to be classified according to their dominant inner- or outer-fluid character through the associated eigenfunctions and their node structure. The formalism developed here provides a foundation for extending relativistic asteroseismology to multi-fluid compact stars and for exploring their potential gravitational-wave signatures in a fully general relativistic setting.

### [146] [Noether charges and the first law of thermodynamics for multifractional Schwarzschild black hole in the q-derivative theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03311)
*Reggie C. Pantig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究多分形理论（multi-fractional theory）中带q导数的黑洞热力学，发现若将霍金温度定义在分形径向坐标下，其会显式依赖于多分形轮廓，导致简单的克劳修斯关系不可积；通过扩大热力学状态空间引入轮廓参数，可构造可积熵泛函并得到扩展的第一定律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨多分形时空框架下黑洞热力学的基本性质，特别是在非平凡分形轮廓（profile）存在时，守恒量与热力学量的行为差异，以及热力学一致性是否得以保持。

Method: 采用带q导数的多分形理论（multi-fractional theory with $q$-derivatives），在球坐标近似下求解静态球对称真空解。在几何框架（geometric frame）中利用标准协变方法定义守恒荷，并在分形径向坐标下定义霍金温度，分析分形轮廓参数对热力学关系的影响。通过扩大热力学状态空间（thermodynamic state space），引入轮廓参数并构造可积熵泛函，推导扩展的第一定律。分析二项式（binomial）和对数振荡（log-oscillating）两类轮廓，并讨论呈现依赖性（presentation dependence）问题。

Result: 守恒质量仅依赖于施瓦西积分常数，Iyer-Wald熵在几何框架下满足通常的面积律。但当霍金温度定义在分形径向坐标下时，其通过局部因子 $q'(r_{\rm h})$ 显式依赖于多分形轮廓。可变轮廓参数破坏了仅以质量和熵表达的克劳修斯关系（Clausius relation）的可积性。通过扩大状态空间并构造径向积分可积熵泛函，可获得包含额外功项的扩展第一定律。

Conclusion: 多分形黑洞热力学中存在轮廓不敏感的规范荷（canonical charges）与轮廓敏感的热学量（thermal quantities）之间的明确分离。扩大热力学状态空间是恢复热力学一致性的关键，扩展第一定律中的额外功项与多分形耦合共轭。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate black-hole thermodynamics in the multi-fractional theory with $q$-derivatives, focusing on static, spherically symmetric vacuum solutions in the spherical-coordinate approximation. In the geometric frame the solution is exactly Schwarzschild in the areal radius $q$, so that canonical charges can be defined using standard covariant methods. The conserved mass depends only on the Schwarzschild integration constant, and the Iyer--Wald entropy satisfies the usual area law in terms of the geometric horizon radius. When the Hawking temperature is defined in the fractional radial coordinate $r$, however, it acquires an explicit dependence on the multi-fractional profile through the local factor $q'(r_{\rm h})$ at the horizon. As a result, variations of the non-dynamical profile parameters generically obstruct integrability of a naive Clausius relation expressed solely in terms of mass and entropy. We show that this obstruction is resolved by enlarging the thermodynamic state space to include the profile parameters and by constructing an integrable entropy functional obtained from a radial integral of the geometric radius. The corresponding extended first law contains additional work terms conjugate to the multi-fractional couplings. We analyze both binomial and log-oscillating profiles, clarify the role of presentation dependence, and delineate the consistency conditions required for a well-defined exterior branch with a single horizon. Our results make explicit the separation between profile-insensitive canonical charges and profile-sensitive thermal quantities in multi-fractional black-hole thermodynamics.

*Omar Mustafa,Abdullah Guvendi*

Main category: gr-qc

Result: 有效势在虫洞喉部（throat）正则且有限，消除了离心奇点；离散能谱由曲率、洛伦兹破缺强度和振荡频率共同决定；能级结构呈现出曲率诱导形变的相对论性粒子-反粒子对称性（relativistic particle-antiparticle symmetry）以及参数依赖的约束效应。

Abstract: We investigate the quantum dynamics of scalar bosonic oscillator fields propagating in a (3+1)-dimensional Lorentz-violating (LV) wormhole spacetime within a modified gravity framework. The underlying geometry, characterized by a smooth minimal-radius throat and a globally regular redshift sector, induces nontrivial curvature effects that significantly modify the spectral properties of the Klein-Gordon (KG) field. The field dynamics are formulated in the presence of a nonminimally coupled vector background of the form $\mathcal{F}_μ=(\mathcal{F}_t(x),0,0,0)$, which, under the physically motivated ansatz $\mathcal{F}_t(x)=Ω\, r(x)$, generates an effective KG-oscillator interaction intrinsically encoded by the wormhole geometry. The resulting effective potential is regular and finite at the throat, eliminating centrifugal singularities and ensuring globally well-defined propagation across the minimal-radius region. The spectral problem reduces to a confluent Heun structure, leading to conditionally exact solutions and a discrete energy spectrum governed by curvature, Lorentz-violation strength, and oscillator frequency. The associated eigenvalue structure exhibits a relativistic particle-antiparticle symmetry with curvature-induced deformation and parameter-dependent confinement. Our results demonstrate that LV wormhole spacetimes act as effective dispersive quantum gravitational media, in which spacetime topology and spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking jointly regulate confinement, spectral quantization, and the global evolution of scalar bosonic modes.

### [148] [Families of regular spacetimes and energy conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03428)
*Zi-Liang Wang,Emmanuele Battista*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种在广义相对论中构造静态球对称正则时空的系统方法，该方法基于物质能量密度的合理假设和Kretschmann标量的有界性，统一描述了Bardeen、Hayward、Dymnikova等已知正则黑洞模型，并推导出若干新系列的正则几何闭式解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的正则黑洞模型（如Bardeen、Hayward、Dymnikova模型）缺乏统一的构造框架，且其构造方法往往依赖特定假设或特殊形式的物质场。本文旨在建立一套系统化、基于物理合理假设的正则时空构造方法。

Method: 方法基于两个核心假设：物质能量密度（energy density）满足物理上的合理性条件，以及Kretschmann标量（Kretschmann scalar）的有界性。后者保证了所有曲率不变量的有限性，并在所考虑的构型中等价于因果测地线（causal geodesic）的完整性。通过按复杂度对可容许的密度分布进行分类，从而统一构造正则时空。

Result: 恢复了Bardeen、Hayward和Dymnikova等已知正则黑洞解，将其自然嵌入统一的广义框架中。推导了多个新系列正则几何的闭式闭式表达式（closed-form expressions），涉及超几何函数（hypergeometric functions）或不完全Gamma函数（incomplete Gamma functions），在许多情况下可简化为包括代数、对数、反正切和指数形式的初等函数。还探讨了视界（horizons）和光子球（photon spheres）的出现条件，以及与Schwarzschild外部解的匹配条件。

Conclusion: 建立的系统化方法为构造满足弱能量条件（weak energy condition）的静态球对称正则时空提供了统一框架，不仅涵盖了已知的正则黑洞模型，还生成了具有丰富解析结构的新解族，有助于深化对正则黑洞几何的理解。

Abstract: We present a systematic method for constructing static, spherically symmetric regular spacetimes in general relativity satisfying the weak energy condition. Our approach relies on physically reasonable assumptions on the matter energy density, together with the boundedness of the Kretschmann scalar. The latter property ensures the finiteness of all curvature invariants and, for the configurations considered, is equivalent to the completeness of causal geodesics. By classifying admissible density profiles according to their complexity, we recover well-known regular black hole solutions such as the Bardeen, Hayward, and Dymnikova models, which are thus naturally embedded in a unified and broader framework. Within this setting, we also derive closed-form expressions for several new families of regular geometries involving hypergeometric or incomplete Gamma functions, which in many cases reduce to elementary functions including algebraic, logarithmic, arctangent, and exponential forms. The emergence of horizons and photon spheres, as well as matching conditions to a Schwarzschild exterior, are also investigated.

### [149] [Ringdown Analysis of GW250114 with Orthonormal Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03576)
*Motoki Suzuki,Kei-ichiro Kubota,Soichiro Morisaki,Hayato Motohashi,Daiki Watarai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究将基于正交化QNM框架的分析方法应用于GW250114事件，发现ℓ=m=2模的第一泛音显著性从之前非正交分析的82.5%提升至99.9%，同时未发现与Kerr黑洞解的显著偏离，表明该框架能更稳健地识别高信噪比铃宕信号中的次主导模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW250114是至今由LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组观测到的信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）最高的引力波事件。此前基于准正则模（quasinormal mode, QNM）叠加的分析已发现ℓ=m=2基模和第一泛音的证据，但由于QNM之间不正交，引入多个QNM会诱导相关性，影响次主导模的稳健识别。

Method: 本文采用基于正交化QNM的分析框架（参考文献arXiv:2507.12376）对GW250114事件进行再分析，该方法通过正交化处理消除了多个QNM之间的相关性。

Result: 在包含三个ℓ=m=2 QNM（直至第二泛音）的模型中，第一泛音的支持度显著增强，显著性（significance）从非正交分析的82.5%提升至99.9%。同时，利用正交QNM框架估计的偏差与Kerr预测一致，未发现显著偏离。

Conclusion: 正交化QNM框架为在高SNR铃宕信号中识别次主导模提供了更稳健的方法，有望在未来引力波观测中发挥重要作用。

Abstract: GW250114 is the loudest gravitational-wave event to date observed by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA Collaboration. Owing to its high signal-to-noise ratio (SNR), previous analyses based on quasinormal mode (QNM) superpositions have suggested evidence of the fundamental and the first overtone of the $\ell=m=2$ mode in this event. However, QNMs are not orthogonal and the inclusion of multiple QNMs induces correlations among them, which can hinder the robust identification of subdominant QNMs. To address this challenge, we apply an analysis based on orthonormalized QNMs [arXiv:2507.12376] to GW250114. We find that, in the model including three $\ell=m=2$ QNMs up to the second overtone, the first overtone of the $\ell=m=2$ mode is more strongly supported than in previous nonorthogonal analyses, with the inferred significance increasing from $82.5\%$ to $99.9\%$. Furthermore, we estimate deviations from the Kerr prediction using the orthonormal QNM framework and find no significant deviation, consistent with previous analyses. These results demonstrate that the orthonormal QNM framework provides a more robust way to identify subdominant modes in high-SNR ringdown signals, highlighting its potential for future gravitational-wave observations.

### [150] [Novel Realizations of Warp Drive Spacetimes as Solutions of General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03653)
*Thomas Buchert,Antony Frackowiak*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在协变3+1（covariant 3+1）框架下重新审视了Alcubierre曲速驱动（warp drive）模型，指出了其速度剖面（velocity profile）受抑制等缺陷；随后基于Natário度规和Synge的G方法分析了两类解，发现曲速场的普遍不稳定性；最后提出了一种包含空间曲率（spatial curvature）和相对论性拉格朗日扰动（relativistic Lagrangian perturbation）的框架，将曲速场研究与相对论宇宙学（relativistic cosmology）联系起来，并讨论了未来实现物理曲速驱动的可能路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深入剖析原始Alcubierre曲速驱动模型在协变3+1框架下的运动学缺陷（如速度剖面受外部振幅主导、变化被抑制），并严格求解爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein's equations）对当前常用时空限制下的曲速度规（metrics）所施加的约束条件，以期澄清曲速驱动理论的数学基础与物理边界。

Method: 采用协变3+1分解分析Alcubierre模型的运动学；利用Natário单分量坐标速度度规的子类给出控制方程；运用Synge的G方法（G-method）对两类示例（先验假定解形式、沿测地线（geodesics）假定解）推导实现约束；引入相对论性拉格朗日扰动方法和Szekeres II类精确解来容纳空间曲率并描述曲速场动力学；最后借助牛顿引力与广义相对论（general relativity）解的直接对应关系进行拓展。

Result: Alcubierre模型中速度剖面的改变受外部振幅抑制；第二类示例解（沿测地线假定）中的曲速场存在预期的普遍不稳定性（generic instability）；通过提出的新框架，曲速场研究可与相对论宇宙学建立直接联系。

Conclusion: 波动的曲速场普遍不稳定，但通过引入空间曲率和相对论性拉格朗日扰动框架，以及利用牛顿引力与广义相对论解的对应关系，可以将曲速驱动问题纳入宇宙学语境；未来可在倾斜流体流（tilted fluid flows）中探索实现物理曲速驱动的可能性。

Abstract: We first take a closer look at the original warp drive proposal by Alcubierre, examine its kinematics in the context of a covariant 3+1 setting, and explain some drawbacks of this construction. In this model, changes of the velocity profile are suppressed, apart from an externally given amplitude. We then discuss Einstein's equations for currently employed spacetime restrictions, and provide the governing equations for the Natário class of metrics with one-component coordinate velocity in a subcase. Following Synge's G-method we determine the constraints on realizations for two examples: assuming the form of the solution a priori as in Alcubierre's model, and determining the solution through an assumption imposed along geodesics. We analyze in detail the role of coordinate acceleration and coordinate vorticity, providing illustrations for both example solutions. For the second we find an expected generic instability of the warp field. We then propose a framework that allows for spatial curvature and the description of warp field dynamics within a relativistic Lagrangian perturbation approach, also including exact solutions of the Szekeres class II. These generalizations allow us to link studies on warp fields to relativistic cosmology. A direct correspondence between solutions of Newtonian gravity and general relativity is exploited. We conclude by discussing possible future paths towards physical warp drives within tilted fluid flows.

</details>


### [151] [Long-lived massive scalar modes, grey-body factors, and absorption cross sections of the Reissner--Nordström-like brane-world black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03659)
*Zainab Malik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究Reissner-Nordström型膜世界黑洞中，由额外维度效应诱导的潮汐电荷参数对大规模标量场准正规模式（包括准共振区）、灰体因子和吸收截面的影响。通过半经典WKB计算与时域演化结合，发现正潮汐电荷降低势垒、增强透射与吸收，而增加场质量或多极数则降低势垒透射率并将吸收移至更高频率；结果还表明长寿命准正规模式出现的迹象，但该行为无法直接由时域轮廓观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索额外维度效应（通过潮汐电荷参数表征）对膜世界黑洞中标量场的准正规模式（quasinormal modes）、准共振（quasi-resonant）行为、灰体因子（grey-body factors）及吸收截面（absorption cross sections）的影响机制与参数依赖性。

Method: 采用半经典WKB（Wentzel–Kramers–Brillouin）近似方法计算准正规模式，同时进行时域演化（time-domain evolution）分析，并确保有效势（effective potential）在相关参数范围内保持单势垒（single-barrier）形状，以保证准正规模式和散射分析的可靠性。

Result: 增加正潮汐电荷（positive tidal charge）会降低势垒高度，使频谱更接近准共振区，并增强透射与吸收；增加场质量（field mass）或多极数（multipole number）则使势垒透射率下降，并将吸收峰移至更高频率；结果还显示任意长寿命准正规模式（arbitrarily long-lived quasinormal mode）出现的开端，但在时域轮廓中该行为被过早建立的渐近尾部（asymptotic tails）掩盖，无法直接观测到晚期振荡。

Conclusion: 潮汐电荷参数显著调控膜世界黑洞的准正规模式与散射特征，正潮汐电荷促进准共振行为与吸收增强，但时域演化无法揭示长寿命模式，因其信号被渐近尾部提前覆盖。

Abstract: We study quasinormal modes, including the quasi-resonant regime, grey-body factors, and absorption cross sections of a massive scalar field in a Reissner--Nordström-like brane-world black hole endowed with a tidal-charge parameter induced by extra-dimensional effects. Combining semiclassical WKB calculations with time-domain evolution, we determine the range of parameters for which the effective potential keeps the single-barrier shape needed for a reliable quasinormal-mode and scattering analysis. We find that increasing positive tidal charge lowers the barrier, drives the spectrum closer to the quasi-resonant regime, and enhances transmission and absorption, whereas increasing the field mass or multipole number makes the barrier less transparent and shifts absorption to higher frequencies. Our results indicate the onset of an arbitrarily long-lived quasinormal-mode regime. At the same time, this behavior cannot be followed directly in the time-domain profiles, because the asymptotic tails set in too early and mask the late-time ringing.

</details>


### [152] [Total transmission modes in draining bathtub model with vorticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03730)
*Zhe Yu,Liang-Bi Wu*

Motivation: 旨在分析具有涡度的排水浴缸模型中总透射模式的行为，特别是其频谱特性及边界条件约束下的模式稳定性。

Method: 采用切比雪夫-洛巴托伪谱方法进行数值求解，边界条件为事件视界（event horizon）和无穷远处均取内行波的TTM条件。

Result: 数值结果表明，（右行）TTM谱可以具有正虚部，但在某些参数下也会出现负虚部；高阶泛音（higher overtones）表现出极端的敏感性，反映为显著的谱迁移性（spectral mobility）。

Conclusion: 含涡度排水浴缸模型中的TTM谱行为比以往认知更为丰富，高阶模式对参数的敏感响应可能对理解旋转黑洞（rotating black hole）中的准正则模（quasinormal modes）具有类比意义。

Abstract: We investigate the total transmission modes (TTMs) in the draining bathtub model (DBM) with vorticity using the Chebyshev-Lobatto pseudospectral method, where the boundary conditions of the total transmission modes are both ingoing at the event horizon and infinity. Numerical results show that the (right) TTM spectra can possess positive imaginary parts, while for certain parameters they acquire negative imaginary parts. The extreme sensitivity of the higher overtones is manifested as their pronounced spectral mobility.

### [153] [Resonances as signatures of scalar clouds in eccentric extreme-mass-ratio inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03756)
*Qi-Xuan Xu,Richard Brito,Riccardo Della Monica,Rodrigo Vicente,Chen Yuan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文在完全相对论性微扰框架下研究了偏心极端质量比旋近（EMRIs）进入由超辐射不稳定性形成的标量云。研究发现，偏心性会在标量流中靠近最后稳定轨道处诱发密集的可探测共振序列，这些共振仅出现在完全相对论计算中，与强场区域方位频率与径向频率的分裂密切相关。通过绝热演化轨道，证明这些共振可导致引力波波形中可探测的失相，表明偏心性对未来空间探测器识别标量云中的EMRIs至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往相对论分析仅限于圆轨道运动，未考虑偏心性对极端质量比旋近（extreme-mass-ratio inspirals, EMRIs）进入标量云（scalar clouds）过程的影响，因此需要拓展到偏心轨道情形以填补这一空白。

Method: 采用完全相对论性微扰框架，研究在Schwarzschild黑洞周围的偏心赤道轨道；绝热演化轨道以分析引力波波形中的失相（dephasing）效应。

Result: 偏心性在标量流中靠近最后稳定轨道附近诱发密集的可探测共振序列；这些共振仅出现在完全相对论计算中，与强场区域方位频率与径向频率的分裂（split）相关；共振可导致引力波波形中可探测的失相。

Conclusion: 偏心性在可靠探测标量云中的极端质量比旋近（EMRIs）方面可能发挥决定性作用，对未来空间引力波探测器具有重要意义。

Abstract: We study eccentric extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) into scalar clouds formed through superradiant instabilities, within a fully relativistic perturbative framework. While previous relativistic analyses were limited to circular motion, we consider eccentric equatorial orbits around a Schwarzschild black hole and show that eccentricity induces a dense sequence of potentially detectable resonances in the scalar fluxes near the last stable orbit. The resonances we uncover only appear in a fully relativistic calculation, as they are intrinsically tied to the split between azimuthal and radial frequencies in the strong-field regime. By evolving the orbit adiabatically, we show that these resonances can induce detectable dephasing in the gravitational waveform. Our results demonstrate that eccentricity could play a decisive role in confidently detecting EMRIs embedded in scalar clouds with future space-based detectors.

### [154] [Shadow of a Noncommutative Thin-Shell Gravastar](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03897)
*M. A. Anacleto,A. T. N. Silva,L. Casarini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在非对易几何框架下构建了一个球对称薄壳引力真空星（gravastar）模型，利用切割-粘贴技术连接非奇异德西特（de Sitter）内部与非对易施瓦西（Schwarzschild）外部，通过以色列（Israel）连接条件分析其稳定性与能量条件，并探讨了非对易参数对光子偏折和模型稳定性的影响，最终表明该模型可作为带电黑洞的稳定替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接观测黑洞是天文学主要挑战之一，但超致密天体（Ultra-Compact Objects）可能存在不稳定圆形光子轨道，导致难以通过光子观测将其与黑洞区分开来。为此，本文旨在构建一个在非对易几何下的引力真空星（Gravastar）模型，以提供一个稳定且可观测的替代方案。

Method: 采用非对易模型（noncommutative model）中由洛伦兹型能量密度分布（最小宽度√θ）描述的球对称薄壳引力真空星，通过切割-粘贴技术（cut-and-paste technique）将非奇异德西特内部与非对易施瓦西外部连接，并满足界面超曲面Σ上的以色列连接条件。引入参数η进行稳定性分析，同时研究非对易参数对光子近距和偏折的影响。

Result: 模型的稳定性受到非对易参数及能量条件（energy conditions）的显著影响；通过参数η可确定引力真空星（gravastar）的稳定区域。随着非对易参数增大，光子的近距（proximity）和偏折（deflection）发生变化。该模型在非对易几何的外部结构下表现出稳定性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的非对易几何外部的引力真空星（gravastar）模型可被视为一种稳定且可行的带电黑洞替代方案。

Abstract: One of the main challenges in astronomy is the direct observation of black holes. However, differentiating them from black holes through photon observations can be difficult if Ultra-Compact Objects with unstable circular photon orbits exist. An example of an Ultra-Compact Object is a Gravastar (gravitational vacuum star), initially proposed by Mazur and Mottola. For definition purposes, we construct a spherically symmetric thin-shell gravastar model within a noncommutative model, in which these effects are integrated by a Lorentzian distribution of the energy density with minimum width $\sqrtθ$. The model is constructed using the cut-and-paste technique to connect a nonsingular de Sitter interior to a noncommutative Schwarzschild exterior, satisfying the Israel junction conditions on the interface hypersurface $Σ$. We examine the stability of the model through its energy conditions, highlighting the influence of the noncommutative parameter on its behavior. The stability analysis of our current model is also studied by introducing the parameter $η$, and we explore the stability region where the gravastar becomes stable. We then also show that, due to noncommutativity, the proximity and deflection of photons change when we increase the noncommutative parameter. Our proposed gravastar model, with noncommutative geometry on its exterior, can be considered a stable and viable alternative to the charged black hole in the context of this gravity.

### [155] [Minimum lifetime of a black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03922)
*Eugenio Bianchi,Matthew Brandsema,Kenneth Czuprynski,Daniel E. Paraizo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在“渐近半经典时空”（asymptotically semiclassical spacetimes）框架下，利用能量守恒和纯化（purification）原理，推导了蒸发黑洞寿命的上下界，并探讨了纯化阶段的时间标度及其与白洞残骸（white-hole remnant）的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞蒸发图像中，霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）的半经典描述在普朗克尺度附近失效，且信息丢失悖论（information loss paradox）尚未完全解决。本文旨在从能量守恒和纠缠纯化（entanglement purification）的角度，约束黑洞蒸发后的纯化时间，以理解信息释放机制。

Method: 利用近期导出的邦迪通量（Bondi flux）表达式和零无穷远处霍金辐射的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）表达式，分析最后一个半经典射线（last semiclassical ray）之后的纯化阶段。通过讨论纠缠纯化的能量成本，推导纯化时间的下限。此外，引入普朗克质量黑洞亚稳态（metastable）的量子引力假设，进一步分析纯化时间标度及红移指数（redshift exponent）的变化。

Result: 纯化时间的下限标度为 \( M_0^4 / \hbar^{3/2} \)（\( M_0 \) 为初始黑洞质量）。在加入普朗克质量黑洞亚稳态假设后，纯化时间被延长为初始黑洞质量平方（即初始面积）的指数函数。同时，纯化阶段的红移指数为负值，暗示存在缓慢释放信息的白洞残骸。

Conclusion: 该研究为黑洞信息释放提供了新的时间约束机制，并预测了白洞残骸的存在，对原初黑洞残骸（primordial black hole remnants）的宇宙学观测具有潜在意义。

Abstract: We derive bounds on the lifetime of an evaporating black hole. The bound follows from energy conservation and purification, within the framework of `asymptotically semiclassical spacetimes'. We use the recently derived expression for the Bondi flux of Hawking radiation, together with the expression for the entanglement entropy of Hawking radiation at null infinity, to investigate the purification phase after the last semiclassical ray. We discuss the energy-cost of entanglement purification and we find a lower bound on the purification time of the black hole, which scales as $M_0^4/\hbar^{3/2}$, where $M_0$ is the initial black hole mass. Additionally, motivated by quantum gravity considerations, we include the additional assumption that a Planck mass black hole is metastable. With this assumption, we find that the the purification time is extended to be exponential in the square of the initial black hole mass, i.e. in its initial area. We find that the redshift exponent is negative in this purification phase, which indicates the existence of a white-hole remnant which releases information slowly. We comment on phenomenological implications for primordial black hole remnants.

</details>
